[4.9	44	rasābhāsaḥ](#heading=h.kgcv8k)

308 verses in nine chapters.


## 


## śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhuḥ


#### uttara-vibhāgaḥ

(4.1) 


### hāsya-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### prathama-laharī

**|| 4.1.1 ||**

**bhakti-bhareṇa prītiṁ kalayann urarīkṛta-vrajāsaṅgaḥ |**

**tanutāṁ sanātanātmā bhagavān mayi sarvadā tuṣṭim ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sanātano nitya ātmā śrī-vigraho yasya saḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ bhakta-niṣṭha-bhakty-atiśayena prītiṁ kurvan | pakṣe, sanātana-nāmā ātmā ātmīyo deho yasya saḥ bhakti-bhareṇa prītiṁ kurvan **||1||**

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.2-5 ||**

**rasāmṛtābdher bhāge’tra turīye tūttārābhidhe |**

**rasaḥ sapta-vidho gauṇo maitrī-vaira-sthitir mithaḥ ||2||**

**rasābhāsāś ca tenātra laharyo nava kīrtitāḥ |**

**prāg atrāniyatādhārāḥ kadācit kvāpy uditvarāḥ ||3||**

**gauṇā bhakti-rasāḥ sapta lekhyā hāsyādayaḥ kramāt ||4||**

**bhaktānāṁ pañcadhoktānām eṣāṁ madhyata eva hi |**

**kvāpy ekaḥ kvāpy anekaś ca gauṇeṣv ālambano mataḥ ||5||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **nanu, śāntādivad dhāsyādbhutādayo’pi pṛthak syur vidūṣaka-senāny-ādiṣu hāsya-vīrādīnāṁ sthiratā-darśanāt tatrāha—bhaktānām iti | bhaktānāṁ pañcadhā rati-pañcakāśrayatvenoktasya tat-tad-bhaktasya ca sarvatrotsarga-siddhatayāsty evālambanatvam | kintu tat-tad-rati-sambandhād ratitvenopacaryamāṇa-hāsādīnāṁ prākrṭa-rasa-śāstrānusāreṇaiva sthāyitvam upacaryate | tad-anusāreṇaiva ca bhayānaka-rasādau dāruṇādīnām ālambanatvam abhyupagaṁsyate | sva-mate tu—


    vibhāvyate hi ratyādir yatra yena vibhāvyate |


    vibhāvo nāma sa dvedhālambanoddīpanātmakaḥ ||

ity ārṣa-pramāṇānusāreṇa saptamy-artha eva sarvatrālambanaḥ | sa cānugatāyā rateḥ sambandhena viṣayāśraya-rūpa eveti ||5||

**mukundaḥ : **śrī-rūpa-caraṇebhyo namaḥ | bhaktānām iti—ālambano viṣayāśraya-rūpaḥ | eva-kārāt na tu ebhyo’nyas taṭastho vipakṣo vety arthaḥ** **||5||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **prāk pūrva**m a**niyatādhārāḥ yathā dāsyādayo mukhya-rasāḥ pūrvaṁ dāsyādiṣu nityādhārā eva teṣu udayaṁ prāpnuvanti, tathā hāsādayo na, kintu kadācit kvāpi bhakte uditvarā udaya-śīlāḥ | sapta atra laharyāṁ kramāl lekhyāḥ ||3-4||

nanu, yathāyaṁ śānta-bhakto’yaṁ dāsya-bhakta iti pṛthak vyavahāras tathāyaṁ hāsya-bhakta iti pṛthak saṁjñā kathaṁ na syād ity ata āha—bhaktānām iti | śāntādi-pañca-vidhānāṁ bhaktānāṁ madhye eva saptasu gauṇa-raseṣu madhye kvāpi hāsyād-rase eko dāsa ālambanaṁ kvāpi karuṇādi-gauṇa-rase śānta-dāsādy aneka ālambanam | ataḥ na tu śānta-dāsyādi-pañca-vidha-bhakta-bhinne hāsyādayo gauṇa-rasā bhavanti | ato dāsyādivaddhāsyādi-gauṇa-rasa-viśeṣṭānāṁ svatantra-saṁjñā nociteti bhāvaḥ ||5||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.6-7||**

tatra **hāsya-bhakti-rasaḥ**—

**vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṁ hāsa-ratir gatā |**

**hāsya-bhakti-raso nāma budhair eṣa nigadyate ||**

**asminn ālambanaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānyo’pi tad-anvayī |**

**vṛddhāḥ śiśu-mukhāḥ prāyaḥ proktā dhīrais tad-āśrayāḥ |**

**vibhāvanādi-vaiśiṣṭhyāt pravarāś ca kvacin matāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **parārthāyā rater visāyatvena tad-vyaktīkrṭa-hāsasya hetutvena ca kṛṣṇo’sminn ālambanaḥ | tad-anvayāt tasya kṛṣṇasyānugata-ceṣṭaś ca tad-rater āśrayatvena tādṛśa-hāsa-hetutvena cālambanaḥ | tasya hāsasyāśrayās tad-āśrayāḥ | hāsasya ceto-vikāśa-mātra-rūpatvād viṣayas tu na vidyate, na hi kamalādi-vikāśaḥ kañcid viṣayaṁ karoti, yam uddiśya pravartata sa eva hi viṣayaḥ | parihāsopahāsa-vācī tu yadā syāt, tadā kañcid viṣayam api kuryān nāma, sa tu nātropādīyata iti bhāvaḥ ||7||

**mukundaḥ : **hāsa-ratir hāsottarā ratiḥ | hāsa-rater āśrayās tad-āśrayaḥ ||6-7||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad-anvayī tasya śrī-kṛṣṇasyānugata-ceṣṭādiś ca tad-rater āśrayatvena tādṛśa-hāse hetutvena cālambanaḥ | tad-āśrayās tasyā rater āśrayā ālambanāḥ ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.8 ||**

tatra **kṛṣṇo**, yathā—

**yāsyāmy asya na bhīṣaṇasya savidhaṁ jīrṇasya śīrṇākṛter**

**mātar neṣyati māṁ pidhāya kapaṭād ādhārikāyām asau |**

**ity uktvā cakitākṣam adbhuta-śiśāv udvīkṣyamāṇe harau**

**hāsyaṁ tasya niruddhato’py atitarāṁ vyaktaṁ tadāsīn muneḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **jaṭila-sannyāsināṁ vastra-nirmita-bhikṣā-pātram **ādhārikā**, tasyāṁ **māṁ** nihnutya sva-sthānaṁ **neṣyati**, **muner** nāradasya ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.9 ||**

atha **tad-anvayī—-**

**yac-ceṣṭā kṛṣṇa-viṣayā proktaḥ so’tra tad-anvayī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : yac-ceṣṭā** iti yad yasya ||9||

**mukundaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

_ —o)0(o—_

**|| 4.1.10 ||**

yathā—

**dadāmi dadhi-phāṇitaṁ vivṛṇu vaktram ity agrato**

**niśamya jaratī-giraṁ vivṛta-komalauṣṭhe sthite |**

**tayā kusumam arpitaṁ navam avetya bhugnānane**

**harau jahasur uddhuraṁ kim api suṣṭhu goṣṭhārbhakāḥ ||10||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : phāṇitaṁ** khaṇḍa-vikṛtiḥ | dadhi-miśritaṁ phāṇitaṁ **dadhi-phāṇitaṁ** | **komala-** iti bālyaṁ vyañjitam ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **phāṇitaṁ khaṇḍa-vikṛtiḥ | **dadhi**-miśritaṁ **phāṇitam** | **komala-** iti bālyaṁ vyañjitam | atra vṛddhā viṣayālambanaṁ, harer **bhugnānanatvam** uddīpanam ||10||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **phāṇitaṁ khaṇḍa-vikṛtiḥ | **dadhi**-miśritaṁ **phāṇitam** | **komala-** iti bālyaṁ vyañjitam | **bhugnānane** tikta-rasāsvādanena kuṭilīkṛtānane ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.11 ||**

yathā vā—

**asya prekṣya karaṁ śiśor muni-pate śyāmasya me kathyatāṁ**

**tathyaṁ hanta cirāyur eṣa bhavitā kiṁ dhenu-koṭīśvaraḥ |**

**ity ukte bhagavan mayādya paritaś cīreṇa kiṁ cāruṇā**

**drāg āvirbhavad-uddhura-smitam idaṁ vaktraṁ tvayā rudhyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **muniṁ prati yaśodāha—he **muni-pate** ! **bhagavan** ! **mayā ity ukte** sati **cāruṇā** manohareṇa **cīreṇa** vastreṇa **āvirbhavad-uddhura-smita**-viśiṣṭaṁ **vaktraṁ tvayā kiṁ rudhyate** ? ||11||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.12-15 ||**

**uddīpanā hares tādṛg-vāg-veṣa-caritādayaḥ |**

**anubhāvās tu nāsauṣṭha-gaṇḍa-niṣpandanādayaḥ ||**

**harṣālasyāvahitthādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ |**

**sā hāsa-ratir evātra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā ||**

**ṣoḍhā hāsa-ratiḥ syāt smita-hasite vihasitāvahasite ca |**

**apahasitātihasitake jyeṣṭhādīnāṁ kramād dve dve ||**

**vibhāvanādi-vaicitryād uttamasyāpi kutracit |**

**bhaved vihasitādyaṁ ca bhāvajñair iti bhaṇyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **uddīpanā ity atra harer ity upalakṣaṇaṁ, tad-anvayino’pi jñeyāḥ ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **uddīpanā ity atra yathā mukhya-raseṣu bhaktānāṁ te noktā grantha-vistāra-bhayāt, tathātrāpi tad-anvayino noktāḥ | kintu sarvatra yathocitaṁ jñeyāḥ | ujjvala-nīlamaṇau guṇā uktā eva ||12||

**jyeṣṭhādināṁ** jyeṣṭha-madhya-kaniṣṭhānāṁ | tatra jyeṣṭhā muni-sakhyādyāḥ, madhyā vṛddhā-dūty-ādyāḥ | kaniṣṭhā bālāḥ ||14||

anubhāvās tu nāsauṣṭha-gaṇḍa-vispandanādayaḥ, vibhāvanādīty ayam arthaḥ—hāsa-rateḥ bālya-vṛddhā prāyaḥ āśrayāḥ, vibhāvanāder vaicitryad iti vaiśiṣṭyāt tu uttarasyapi pravara-jyeṣṭhāpara-paryāyasya vihāsitādyaṁ rati-catuṣṭayaṁ ca bhaved iti ||15||

**viśvanāthaḥ : jyeṣṭhasya** uttamasya **smita-hasite dve**, madhyamasya **vihasitāvahasite dve**, kaniṣṭhasya **apahasitātihasite dve** ||14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.16-17 ||**

tatra **smitam—**

**smitaṁ tv alakṣya-daśanaṁ netra-gaṇḍa-vikāśa-kṛt ||**

yathā—

**kva yāmi jaratī khalā dadhi-haraṁ didhīrṣanty asau**

**pradhāvati javena māṁ subala maṅkṣu rakṣāṁ kuru |**

**iti skhalad-udīrite dravati kāndiśīke harau**

**vikasvara-mukhāmbujaṁ kulam abhūn munīnāṁ divi ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : subala** ! he suṣṭhu-bala ! iti kiñcid baliṣṭhaṁ jyeṣṭhaṁ bhrātaraṁ prati sambodhanaṁ, na tu subala-saṁjñam tat-sama-vayastvaṁ prati | **kāndiśīke** bhaya-drute | **dravati** iti dravasyātiśaya-bodhanāya ||17||

**mukundadāsaḥ : subala** iti | sāhayārthaṁ sakhāyaṁ prati sambodhanam | **kāndiśīke** bhaya-drute | punar dravatīti dravasyātiśaya-bodhanāya ||17||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he subala ! **kva yāmi** ? **khalā jaratī** vṛddhā **māṁ dadhi-haraṁ** jñātvā **dhartum icchantī** satī vegena **dhāvati** | ato **māṁ maṅkṣu** śīghraṁ **rakṣāṁ kuru** | **kāndiśīke** bhaya-drute **harau** **dravati** sati | dravatīti dravasyātiśaya-bodhanāya **munīnāṁ vikasita-mukhāmbujam abhūt** ||17||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.18-19 ||**

**hasitam—**

**tad eva dara-saṁlakṣya-dantāgraṁ hasitaṁ bhavet ||**

yathā—

**mad-veśena puraḥ-sthito harir asau putro’ham evāsmi te**

**paśyety acyuta-jalpa-viśvasitayā saṁrambha-rajyad-dṛśā |**

**mām eti skhalad-akṣare jaṭilayā vyākruśya niṣkāsite **

**putre prāṅgataḥ sakhī-kulam abhūd dantāṁśu-dhautādharam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **mad-veśeneti dūram āyāntam adṛṣṭa-sva-veśi-śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ śrī-rādhikāyāḥ patiṁmanyaṁ jaṭilāyāḥ putram abhimanyuṁ dṛṣṭvā tad-veśena tad-gṛham gatasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya tāṁ prati vacanam | niṣkāsite dūrata eva vidrāvite | tasyā vātulatām āśaṅkya sva-bandhūnām ānayanārthaṁ tasya vidrutatvāt ||19||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad eva smtam īṣat-saṁlaksya-dantāgraṁ cet, tadā hasitaṁ bhavet ||18|| śrī-rādhāyāḥ patiṁmanyaṁ jaṭilāyāḥ putram abhimanyuṁ dṛṣṭvā tad-veśena tad-gṛhaṁ praviṣṭaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇo jaṭilāṁ pratyāha | “he mātaḥ ! tvat-putro’ham | ata eva tāḍanaṁ māṁ mā kuru |” iti samanākṣarāṇāṁ duḥkhenoccāraṇāsāmarthyāt kevalaṁ mā mā iti skhalann akṣaro yasya tathā-bhūte putre abhimanyau mātrā jaṭilayā svasyāṅganato niṣkāsite sati sakhī-kulaṁ danta-kiraṇaiḥ dhautādharam abhūt | katham-bhūtayā ? saṁrambheṇa krodhāveśena rajyantī dṛk yasyās tayā ||19||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.20-21 ||**

**vihasitam—**

**sa-svanaṁ dṛṣṭa-daśanaṁ bhaved vihasitaṁ tu tat ||**

yathā—

**muṣāṇa dadhi meduraṁ viphalam antarā śaṅkase**

**sa-niḥśvasita-ḍambaraṁ jaṭilayātra nidrāyate |**

**iti bruvati keśave prakaṭa-śīrṇa-danta-sthalaṁ**

**kṛtaṁ hasitam utsvanaṁ kapaṭa-suptayā vṛddhayā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **kapaṭa-suptayety anena tayeti pūrvokta-svārasyāl labhyate | suptayāpy etayeti vā pāṭhaḥ ||21||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tad dhasitaṁ sa-svanaṁ sa-śabdaṁ dṛṣṭa-daśanaṁ cet tadā vihasitaṁ bhavet ||20|| śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ subalam āha—he sakhe ! meduraṁ snigdhaṁ dadhi muṣāṇa coraya | niśvāsasya ḍambaram autkaṭyaṁ tat-sahitaṁ yathā syāt tathā jaṭilayātinidrāyate | atas tvam antarā madhye viphalam āśaṅkase | prakaṭa-śīrṇa-danta-sthalaṁ yathā syāt tathā | evam ucchvasanam ucca-śabda-yuktaṁ yathā syāt tathā vṛddhayā hasitaṁ kṛtam ||21|| 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.22-23 ||**

 

**avahasitam—**

**tac cāvahasitaṁ phulla-nāsaṁ kuñcita-locanam ||**

yathā—

**lagnas te nitarāṁ dṛśor api yuge kiṁ dhātu-rāgo ghanaḥ**

**prātaḥ putra balasya vā kim asitaṁ vāsas tvayāṅge dhṛtam |**

**ity ākarṇya puro vrajeśa-gṛhiṇī-vācaṁ sphuran-nāsikā**

**dūtī saṅkucad-īkṣaṇāvahasitaṁ jātā na roddhuṁ kṣamā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **lagnas te ity ādau | putrety atra mitreti vrajeśa-gṛhiṇī-vācam ity atra ca dhṛtārjava-suhṛd-vācam iti vā pāṭhāntaraṁ jñeyam ||23||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **rātrau rādhayā saha vihāra-vaśāt śrī-kṛṣṇasya netrayo lagnaṁ tasyās tāmbūla-rāgaṁ dṛṣṭvā evaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇena bhramād aṅge dhṛtaṁ śrī-rādhikāyāḥ śyāmottarīyaṁ ca dṛṣṭvā yaśoda śrī-kṛṣṇam āha—he putra ! tava netrayoḥ ghanaṁ niviḍaḥ dhātu-rāgaḥ gairikaḥ kiṁ lagnaḥ ? baladevasya asitaṁ śyāmaṁ vastraṁ tvarā kim aṅge dhṛtam ? roddhuṁ na kṣamā na samarthā babhūva ||23||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.24-25 ||**

**apahasitam—**

**tac cāpahasitaṁ sāśru-locanaṁ kampitāṁsakam ||**

yathā—

**udasraṁ devarṣir divi dara-taraṅgad-bhuja-śirā**

**yad abhrāṇy uddaṇḍo daśana-rucibhiḥ pāṇḍarayati |**

**sphuṭaṁ brahmādīnāṁ naṭayitari divye vraja-śiśau**

**jaratyāḥ prastobhān naṭati tad anaiṣīd dṛśam asau ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : prastobhāt** nṛtyānukūla-kara-vādanādeḥ ||25||

**viśvanāthaḥ : kampito’ṁsakaḥ** skandha-deśo yatra tat ||24|| **ud**gatāśru-jalaṁ yathā syāt, tathā **dara-taraṅgad **īṣac-calad **bhuja-śiraḥ** skandha-deśo yasya tathā-bhūto **devarṣir** nāradaḥ dantānāṁ śveta-kāntibhiḥ yad yasmād **abhrāṇi pāṇḍavayati**, tat tasmāt asau nāradaḥ—"he śrī-kṛṣṇa ! tvaṁ nṛtyaṁ kuru, tubhyaṁ khaṇḍa-laḍḍukāni dāsyāmi" iti vṛddhāyāḥ pralobhanāt **naṭati** aprākṛte **vraja-śiśau** śrī-kṛṣṇe **dṛṣṭim anaiṣīt** | tathā ca śrī-kṛṣṇasya nṛtyaṁ dṛṣṭvā nārada uccaiḥ jahāsa ity arthaḥ ||25||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.26-27 ||**

**atihasitam—**

**sahasra-tālaṁ kṣiptāṅgaṁ tac cātihasitaṁ viduḥ ||**

yathā—

**vṛddhe tvaṁ valitānanāsi valibhiḥ prekṣya suyogyām atas**

**tvām udvoḍhum asau balī-mukha-varo māṁ sādhayaty utsukaḥ |**

**ābhir vipluta-dhīr vṛṇe na hi paraṁ tvatto bali-dhvaṁsanād**

**ity uccair mukharā-girā vijahasuḥ sottālikā bālikāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **baliḥ kuñcita-carma | balīmukho vānaraḥ | sādhayati sādhanāya prerayati iti dvir ṇac-pratyayāt | balinas tṛṇāvara-pūtanādayas teṣāṁ dhvaṁsa-kartuḥ, ābhir balibhir viplutā upaplutā dhīr yasyāḥ ||27||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **balibhiḥ kuñcita-carmabhir valitānanā vyāpta-mukhī | balīmukho vānaraḥ | sādhayati tasmin nispādanāya māṁ prerayatīti dvi-nic-pratyayāt | ābhir balibhir viplutā upadrutā dhīr yasyāḥ sā, balinas tṛṇāvarta-pūtanikādayas teṣāṁ dhvaṁsanān nāśa-kartuḥ ||27||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **baliḥ kuñcita-carma tābhir yuktānanāsi, atas tvāṁ sva-yogyāṁ prekṣya asau vānaraḥ udvoḍhu-kāmaḥ san māṁ kṛṣṇaṁ sādhayati sādhanāya prerayati | ābhir balibhir viplutā upadrutā dhīr yasyāḥs tathā-bhūtāhaṁ tvattaḥ kṛṣṇāt paraṁ janaṁ na vṛṇe | tvattaḥ kiṁ-bhūtāt ? yato bali-dhvaṁsanāt, vāstavārthas tu balinaḥ tṛṇāvarta-pūtanādayaḥ teṣāṁ dhvaṁsana-kartuḥ ||27||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.28-29 ||**

**yasya hāsaḥ sa cet kvāpi sākṣān naiva nibadhyate |**

**tathāpy eṣa vibhāvādi-sāmarthyād upalabhyate ||**

yathā—

**śimbī-lambi-kucāsi dardura-vadhū-vispardhi nāsākṛtis**

**tvaṁ jīryad-duli**[^1]**-dṛṣṭir oṣṭha-tulitāṅgārā mṛdaṅgodarī |**

**kā tvattaḥ kuṭile parāsti jaṭilā-putri kṣitau sundarī**

**puṇyena vraja-subhruvāṁ tava dhṛtiṁ hartuṁ na vaṁśī kṣamā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **duḍiḥ kamaṭhī ||29||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **duḍiḥ kacchapī ||29||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dardura-vadhūḥ bhekī | duliḥ kacchapī ||29||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.1.30 ||**

**eṣa hāsya-rasas tatra kaiśikī-vṛtti-vistṛtau |**

**śṛṅgārādi-rasodbhedo bahudhaiva prapañcitaḥ ||30||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **tatra bharatādi-nibandhe sva-kṛta-nāṭaka-lakṣaṇe ||30||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **tatra bharatādi-nibandhe ||30||

**viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

hāsya-bhakti-rasa-laharī prathamā

|| 4.1 ||

 —o)0(o—

(4.2)


### adbhuta-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### dvitīya-laharī

**|| 4.2.1-2 ||**

**ātmocitair vibhāvādyaiḥ svādyatvaṁ bhakta-cetasi |**

**sā vismaya-ratir nītādbhuto-bhakti-raso bhavet ||**

**bhaktaḥ sarva-vidho’py atra ghaṭate vismayāśrayaḥ |**

**lokottara-kriyā-hetur viṣayas tatra keśavaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bhakta** iti sārdha-trayeṇādbhutasya parikarān āha | **vismayāśrayo** **vismaya-rater** āśraya ity arthaḥ | **viṣayas** tasyā eva viṣaya ity arthaḥ | vismayaś ca "idaṁ kathaṁ jātam ?" iti hetv-asambhāvanā-mayī buddhiḥ | etābhyāṁ dvayor apy alambana-vibhāvatvaṁ darśitam | "viṣaya ity atra vibhāvaḥ" iti pāṭho likhana-bhramāt ||2||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bhakta** iti vibhāvā bhakta āśrayā **vismaya-rater** āsvāda-hetuḥ | lokottarārtha-vīkṣāder vismayaś citta-vistṛtir iti sāmānya-rase artha-śabdād rūpa-guṇa-karmāṇi yadyapi labdhāni, tathāpi parakīya-matatayā saṅkṣepārhaṁ sā lokottara-karmataḥ ity uktam | sva-mate tv etāny uddīpanatvenoktāny eva | yathā-yogyaṁ bhaktānām api sakhi-prakara-mārgaṇān ity atra, amaṁsta racita-stutir [bha.ra.si. 4.3.8] ity-āder vakṣyamāṇāt, gumphantu gopāḥ [bha.ra.si. 2.4.45] ity atra hṛdi vismitaḥ srajam [bha.ra.si. 2.4.45] ity-āder uktāc ca tāni jñeyāni | kintu tarkāgocara-sarva-lokottarottaroktir yā sāśrayatvena eva darśitā ||2||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **adbhuta-rasasya parikarān āha—**bhakta** iti sārdha-trayeṇa | **vismayāśrayaḥ** vismaya-rater āśraya ity arthaḥ | **viṣayaḥ** tasyā eva rater viṣaya ity arthaḥ | **vismayaś** ca "idaṁ kathaṁ jātam ?" iti hetv-asambhāvanā-mayī buddhiḥ ||2||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.3-4 ||**

**tasya ceṣṭā-viśeṣādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ |**

**kriyās tu netra-vistāra-stambhāśru-pulakādayaḥ ||**

**āvega-harṣa-jāḍyādyās tatra syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ |**

**sthāyī syād vismaya-ratiḥ sā lokottara-karmataḥ |**

**sākṣād anumitaṁ ceti tac ca dvividham ucyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : lokottara-karmata** ity upalakṣaṇaṁ, tādṛśa-rūpa-guṇābhyāṁ ca | kintu lokottara-tat-prema-hetur bhaktaś cet tadā so’pi tadvaj jñeyaḥ | tathā nemaṁ viriñco na bhavaḥ [bhā.pu. 10.9.20] ity-ādau, itthaṁ satāṁ brahma-sukhānubhūtyā [bhā.pu. 10.12.11] ity-ādau, nāyaṁ śriyo’ṅga [bhā.pu. 10.47.60] ity-ādau ca ||4||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kriyā raty-anubhāvāḥ ||3|| lokottara-karmata ity upalakṣaṇaṁ, lokottara-prema-hetur bhaktaś cet tadā so’pi tadvaj jñeyaḥ | tathā nemaṁ viriñco na bhavaḥ [bhā.pu. 10.9.20] ity ādau, itthaṁ satāṁ brahma-sukhānubhūtyā [bhā.pu. 10.12.11] ity ādau, nāyaṁ śriyo’ṅga [bhā.pu. 10.47.60] ity ādau ca ||4||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.5-7 ||**

tatra **sākṣāt**, yathā—

**sākṣād aindriyakaṁ dṛṣṭa-śruta-saṅkīrtitādikam ||**

tatra **dṛṣṭaṁ**, yathā—

**ekam eva vividhodyama-bhājaṁ**

**mandireṣu yugapan nikhileṣu |**

**dvārakām abhi samīksya mukundaṁ**

**spandanojjhita-tanur munir āsīt ||**

yathoktaṁ śrī-daśame (10.69.2)—

**citraṁ bataitad ekena vapuṣā yugapat pṛthak |**

**gṛheṣu dvy-aṣṭa-sāhasraṁ striya eka udāvahat ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : ekam** iti | eka-vapuṣam eva santam ity arthaḥ | tasmān **munir** atra śrī-nāradaḥ | ata eva kāya-vyūha-samarthānām api tad-vidhānāṁ vismayaḥ ||6|| \


**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : aindriyakam** indriya-janyaṁ jñānaṁ sākṣād ucyate | tac ca trividhaṁ dṛṣṭam ity-ādi ||5|| **ekam** iti eka-vapuṣam ity arthaḥ | tasmān **munir** atra śrī-nāradaḥ ||6|| citram iti—ata eva kāya-vyūha-samarthānām api tad-vidāṁ vismayaḥ ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.8 ||**

yathā vā—

**kva stanya-gandhi-vadanendur asau śiśus te **

**govardhanaḥ śikhara-ruddha-ghanaḥ kva cāyam |**

**bhoḥ paśya savya-kara-kandūkitācalendraḥ**

**khelann iva sphurati hanta kim indra-jālam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : stanya-gandhi** iti | atra alpākhyāyāṁ samāsānta it-pratyayaḥ | **acalendraḥ** pūrvokta eva govardhanaḥ prakṛtatvāt **kandukitaṁ** tam adriṁ kurvan mudaṁ vahatīti vā pāṭhaḥ ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **śrī-nandaṁ prati śrī-yaśodoktiḥ—**kva** iti | **stanya-gandhi** ity atrālpākhyāyāṁ samāsanta it-pratyayaḥ ||8||

**viśvanāthaḥ : stanya-gandhi** iti | atrālpākhyāyāṁ samāsānta it-pratyayaḥ | **acalendraḥ** pūrvokta eva govardhanaḥ ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.9 ||**

**śrutaṁ**, yathā—

**yāny akṣipan praharaṇāni bhaṭāḥ sa devaḥ**

**pratyekam acchinad amūni śara-trayeṇa |**

**ity ākalayya yudhi kaṁsaripoḥ prabhāvaṁ **

**sphārekṣaṇaḥ kṣitipatiḥ pulakī tadāsīt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bhaṭā** narakasyaikādaśākṣauhiṇī-saṅkhyāḥ, **kṣiti-patiḥ** śrī-parīkṣit ||9||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bhaṭā** narakasyaikādaśākṣauhiṇī-saṅkhyāḥ, **kṣiti-patir** yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||9||

**viśvanāthaḥ : bhaṭā** narakāsura-sevakāḥ ekādaśākṣauhiṇī-saṅkhyāḥ **praharaṇāni** **yāni** | **kṣiti-patiḥ **śrī-parīkṣit ||9||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.10 ||**

**saṅkīrtitaṁ,** yathā—

**ḍimbāḥ svarṇa-nibhāmbarā ghana-ruco jātāś caturbāhavo**

**vatsāś ceti vadan kṛto’smi vivaśaḥ stambha-śriyā paśyata |**

**āścaryaṁ kathayāmi vaḥ śṛṇuta bhoḥ pratyekam ekaikaśaḥ**

**stūyante jagad-aṇḍavadbhir abhitas te hanta padmāsanaiḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : ḍimbhā** iti | satya-loka-sabhāyāṁ śrī-brahma-vākyam | **stambha-śriyā paśyata** ity eva pāṭhas tv eṣām iṣṭaḥ | **stūyanta** iti vartamāna-sāmīpye vartamānavad veti nyāyena avilamba-dṛṣṭatvaṁ sūcayati ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : ḍimbhā** iti | satya-loka-sabhāyāṁ śrī-brahma-vākyam | "stambhena sampaśyata" iti pāṭhaḥ | **pratyekam** eka eka **ekaikaśaḥ** ekenaikena | atra svārthe kaḥ, śas pratyayo jñeyaḥ | ṛṣi-sahasram ekāṁ kapilām ekaikaśaḥ sahasra-kṛtvā datteti bhāṣya-prayogāt | **stūyante** iti vartamāna-sāmīpye vartamānavad veti avilamba-dṛṣṭatvaṁ sūcayati ||10||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **satya-loka-sabhāyāṁ śrī-brahmaṇo vākyam | **ḍimbhā** bālakāḥ | **vatsāś** ca **catur-bāhavo jātā** iti vadann ahaṁ **stambha-**bhāvena vivaśaḥ kṛto’smi | **stūyanta** iti vartamāna-sāmīpye vartamānavad veti nyāyenāvilamba-dṛṣṭatvaṁ sūcayati ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.11 ||**

**anumitaṁ**, yathā—

**unmīlya vraja-śiśavo dṛśaṁ purastād**

**bhāṇḍīraṁ punar atulya vilokayantaḥ |**

**sātmānaṁ paśu-paṭalīṁ ca tatra dāvād**

**unmuktāṁ manasi camatkriyām avāpuḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dāvānalād **unmuktām** **ātmanā sahitāṁ paśupālīṁ** ca **vilokayantaḥ** ||11||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.2.12-13 ||**

**apriyādeḥ kriyā kuryān nālaukiky api vismayam | \
asādhāraṇy api manāk karoty eva priyasya sā ||**

**priyāt priyasya kim uta sarva-lokottarottarā |**

**ity atra vismaye proktā raty-anugraha-mādhurī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **śrī-kṛṣṇe evādbhuto rasaḥ samudbhūtaḥ syād iti kathayan sarvam api rasaṁ vismayavatāv eva pratiṣṭhāpayati--apriyāder iti dvayena | tad uktaṁ—


    rase sāraś camatkāraḥ sarvatrāpy anubhūyate |


    tasmād adbhutam evāha kṛtī nārāyaṇo rasam ||[^2] iti |

**manāg** apy asādhāraṇīti yojyam ||12-13||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **nanu parameśa-buddhīnāṁ koṭi-brahmāṇḍa-kartari vismaya eva tāvan na jāyate | yadi vā jāyate, tarhi mukhyāṁ ratim eva puṣṇīta, ratiḥ katham enaṁ tathā cārutāṁ nayati yathā kathañcit kāla-mayaṁ sthāyitāṁ yātīty atrāha--**apriyāder** iti dvābhyām | **sarva-lokottarottarā** ity atrāyaṁ vivekaḥ—yathā priya-janasyālpāpy asādhāraṇī kriyā vismayaṁ karoti, tathā yeṣāṁ śuddha-prema, teṣāṁ svalpāpi sā tat-kartrī | yeṣāṁ paramaiśya-jñānātmakaṁ prema, teṣāṁ tarkāgocara-sarva-lokottarottarā sā tathā | yeṣāṁ paramaiśya-jñāna-miśraṁ tat teṣāṁ tarkāgocara-prabhāva-mātra-prakāśitā sā tatheti ||12-13||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yasmin prītir nāsti, pratyuta dveṣo vartate, tasyālaukiky api **kriyā vismayaṁ** **na kuryāt**, prīty-abhāva-dveṣayoḥ pratibandhakatvāt, **lokottarāpi** kriyā vismayaṁ karoty eva | iti sātra rītiḥ | evaṁ sati **priyād** api **priyasya** śrī-kṛṣṇasya **sarva-lokottarottarā** kriyā **vismayaṁ kuryād** iti kiṁ vaktavyam ? tathā ca śrī-kṛṣṇasya sā kriyā vismayaṁ karoty evety arthaḥ ||12-13||

 iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī dvitīyā

|| 4.2 ||

 —o)0(o—

(4.3)


### vīra-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### tṛtīya-laharī

**|| 4.3.1-3 ||**

**saivotsāha-ratiḥ sthāyī vibhāvādyair nijocitaiḥ |**

**ānīyamānā svādyatvaṁ vīra-bhakti-raso bhavet ||1||**

**yuddha-dāna-dayā-dharmaiś caturdhā vīra ucyate |**

**ālambana iha prokta eṣa eva caturvidhaḥ ||2||**

**utsāhas tv eṣa bhaktānāṁ sarveṣām eva sambhavet ||3||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : utsāha** utsāha-ratiḥ | **sarveṣām** iti kasyacit utsāha-bhedaḥ syād ity abhiprāyeṇa ||3||

**mukundadāsaḥ : eṣa eva** vīra-bhakta eva, na tv abhaktaḥ ||2|| **utsāha** utsāhottarā ratiḥ | **sarveṣām** iti kasyacit kaścid utsāha-bhedaḥ syād ity abhiprāyeṇa ||3||

**viśvanāthaḥ : yuddha-** iti | yuddha-vīra-dāna-vīra-dayā-vīra-dharma-vīrā iti **caturdhā vīra** ucyate ||2|| **sarveṣām** iti | kasyacid bhaktasya yuddhotsāhaḥ | kasyacid dānotsāhaḥ | evaṁ-rītyā **sarveṣāṁ** jñeya iti bhāvaḥ ||3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.4-5 ||**

tatra **yuddha-vīraḥ—**

**paritoṣāya kṛṣṇasya dadhad utsāham āhave |**

**sakhā bandhu-viśeṣo vā yuddha-vīra ihocyate ||**

**pratiyoddhā mukundo vā tasmin vā prekṣake sthite |**

**tadīyecchā-vaśenātra bhaved anyaḥ suhṛd-varaḥ ||**

**viśvanāthaḥ : tasmin** śrī-kṛṣṇe vā draṣṭari sati **tadīyecchā-vaśād anya** eva sakhā **pratiyoddhā** bhavet ||4-5||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.6 ||**

tatra **kṛṣṇo**, yathā—

**aparājita-māninaṁ haṭhāc **

**caṭulaṁ tvām abhibhūya mādhava |**

**dhinuyām adhunā suhṛd-gaṇaṁ **

**yadi na tvaṁ samarāt parāñcasi ||6||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : yadi na tvam** iti | **yadi **samaraṁ tyaktuṁ chalena **samarāt** **parāṅmukho** na bhavasīty arthaḥ | "sa yadi tvaṁ samaraṁ samañcasi" iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||6||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **"yadi samaraṁ tyaktuṁ chalena samarāt samañcasi" iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||6||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.7 ||**

yathā vā—

**saṁrambha-prakaṭīkṛta-pratibhaṭārambha-śriyoḥ sādbhutaṁ**

**kālindī-puline vayasya-nikarair ālokyamānas tadā |**

**avyutthāpita-sakhyayor api varāhaṅkāra-visphūrjitaḥ**

**śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś ca samarāṭopaḥ paṭīyān abhūt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : saṁrambheṇa** kopenaiva **prakaṭīkṛtā pratibhaṭasya** pratiyoddhur **ārambha-śrīr** yābhyām | vastutas tu **avyutthāpita-sakhyayor** avirodhita-maitrayor api | **śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś** **ca** iti śrīdāma-bakīdviṣor dvayor ity arthaḥ | etad-artha-vaśād eva viśeṣaṇānāṁ dvitvam | 

etad uktaṁ bhavati—cārthaḥ khalu caturvidhaḥ—samuccayānvācayetaretara-yoga-samāhāra-bhedena | tatra samuccayārthaś ca śabdas tat-tad-arthānāṁ pṛthak-pṛthaktā-vyañjakaḥ | yathā śrīdāma ca bakīdviṭ cāgata ity atra āgatasya pṛthak pṛthak sambandhaḥ | anvācayārthaś ca tathā—yathā bakīdviṣam ānaya yadi paśyasi śrīdāmānaṁ ca kintūttara-nirdiṣṭenātyāgrahaṁ vyañjayati | yathā śrī-kṛṣṇaś ca lokaś ca dṛśyatām iti | tasmāt samartha-śabdokta-paraspara-sambandhārthatvābhāvād anayor na dvandva-samāsaḥ kriyate, kintu tad-bhāvād uttarayor eva | tatra samāhāre samarthatve saty api milana-mātra-vācitvena tadvatām avācitvāt prativiśeṣaṇānvayitvaṁ syād eva | yathā padaka-kramakam avyavahitam ity-ādi | tadvati vṛttis tatropacārād eva | athetaretara-yogārthaś ca-śabdas tat-tat-pratyeka-saṅkhyā-samudayena yāvatī teṣāṁ saṅkhyā syāt, tāvat saṅkhyānvitatā-vyañjakaḥ | tatra ca dvandve śrīdāma-bakīdviṣāv āgatāv ity atra śrīdāmā ca bakīdviṭ ceti dvāv agatāv ity arthaḥ | samuccayād asyāyam eva bhedaḥ | yadi ca samāse tathārthaḥ syāt, tadā tad-vigrahe’pi syād yam āvalambyaiva samāsānām arthaḥ pravartate | dvandva-samāsasya ca vaikalpikatvāt kevala-vigraho’pi prayujyate | tataś ca śrīdāmā ca bakīdviṭ cāgatāv ity api syāt | yathā sa ca tvaṁ cāhaṁ ca pacāma ity atra vipratiṣedhe paraṁ kāryam [pā. 1.4.2] iti pāṇiner yugapad-vacane paraḥ puruṣāṇām iti sarva-varmaṇaś ca nyāyenottama-puruṣe’pi prāpte bahu-vacanaṁ pūrvavad eva syād iti sādhu vyākhyātaṁ—śrīdāma-bakīdviṣor dvayor ity-ādi ||7||

**mukundadāsaḥ : saṁrambheṇa** yuddha-vīra-rasa-svabhāvajena kopena **prakaṭīkṛtā** **pratibhaṭasya** pratiyoddhur **ārambha-śrīr** udyama-sampat yābhyām | **avyutthāpitam** avirodhitaṁ **sakhyaṁ** maitraṁ yābhyāṁ, tathā-bhūtayor api | ata eva **vayasya-nikaraiḥ** **sādbhutaṁ** yathā syāt, tathā **ālokyamānaḥ** | yathā rāmaḥ kṛṣṇaś cāvagatāv iti tathā **śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś ca** saṁrambhety-ādi viśeṣa-vikramo’tiśaktitā ||7||

**viśvanāthaḥ : saṁrambheṇa** kopena **prakaṭī-kṛtā pratibhaṭasya** pratiyoddhur **ārambha-śrīr **yābhyāṁ tayoḥ | vastutas tu **avyutthāpita-sakhyayor** avirodhita-maitrayor api **samarāṭopaḥ** abhavat | **śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś** **ca** iti śrīdāma-bakīdviṣor dvayor ity arthaḥ | samuccaya-bodhaka-cakāreṇaiva dvitva-pratītir jñeyā ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.8 ||**

**suhṛd-varo**, yathā—

**sakhi-prakara-mārgaṇān agaṇitān kṣipan sarvatas**

**tathādya laguḍaṁ kramād bhramayati sma dāmā kṛtī |**

**amaṁsta racita-stutir vrajapates tanūjo’py amuṁ**

**samṛddha-pulako yathā laguḍa-pañjarāntaḥ-sthitam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : mārgaṇā** atra tṛṇa-pūrṇaś carma-phalaka-bāṇāḥ ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : sakhi-samūhair** ekadaiva preritān **agaṇitān mārgaṇān** bāṇān laguḍa-bhramaṇair eva **kṣipan** dūrīkurvan **śrīdāmā** **laguḍaṁ** **tathādya bhramayati sma** yathā śrī-kṛṣṇo’pi amuṁ śrīdāmānaṁ **laguḍa-pañjara-madhya-sthitam amaṁsta** | kathaṁ-bhūtaḥ ? "dhanyo’si śrīman" iti racitā stutir yena sa dāmā | **kṛtī** iti bhrama-kriyā-viśeṣaṇaṁ | mārgaṇā atra tṛṇa-pūrṇa-carma-phalaka-bāṇāḥ, atas teṣāṁ kṣepaṇe’pi na sakhya-hānir iti ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.9-10 ||**

**prāyaḥ prakṛta-śūrāṇāṁ sva-pakṣair api karhicit |**

**yuddha-keli-samutsāho jāyate paramādbhutaḥ ||**

tathā ca hari-vaṁśe—

**tathā gāṇḍīva-dhanvānaṁ vikrīḍan madhusūdanaḥ | **

**jigāya bharata-śreṣṭhaṁ kuntyāḥ pramukhato vibhuḥ || **iti |

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam |_

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.11-12 ||**

**katthitāsphoṭa-vispardhā-vikramāstra-grahādayaḥ |**

**pratiyodha-sthitāḥ santo bhavanty uddīpanā iha ||**

tatra **katthitam—**

**piṇḍīśūras tvam iha subalaṁ kaitavenābalāṅgaṁ**

**jitvā dāmodara yudhi vṛthā mā kṛthāḥ katthitāni |**

**mādyann eṣa tvad-alaghu-bhujā-sarpa-darpāpahārī**

**mandra-dhvāno naṭati nikaṭe stokakṛṣṇaḥ kalāpī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : piṇḍīśūro** bhojana-mātra-paṭuḥ | **abalāṅgam** api **kaitavena jitvā** ity arthaḥ | **kalāpī** tūṇavān sabhūṣaṇo vā, pakṣe mayūraḥ ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : piṇḍīśūro** bhojana-mātra-paṭuḥ | **abalāṅgaṁ** durbalāṅgam api **kaitavena** kapaṭenaiva | **kalāpī** tūṇavān sa-bhūṣaṇo vā, pakṣe mayūraḥ | asamāse rūpakam idam ||12||

**viśvanāthaḥ : pratiyodha-sthitāḥ** pratiyoddhur vākyādinā bodha-viṣayāḥ **santaḥ** amī **katthitādayaḥ** **iha** rase **uddīpanā** **bhavanti** ||11|| 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.13-14 ||**

**katthitādyāḥ sva-saṁsthāś ced anubhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |**

**tathaivāhopuruṣikā kṣveḍitākrośa-valganam ||13||**

**asahāye’pi yuddhecchā samarād apalāyanam |**

**bhītābhaya-pradānādyā vijñeyāś cāpare budhaiḥ ||14||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **āho-puruṣikā darpād vā syāt sambhāvanātmani | kṣveḍitaṁ siṁha-nādaḥ | ākrośaḥ sāṭopa-vacanam | valganaṁ yuddhārtho gati-viśeṣaḥ | yuddhecchā yuddhodyamaḥ ||13-14||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **āho-puruṣikā darpād vā syāt sambhāvanātmani | kṣveḍitaṁ siṁha-nādaḥ | ākrośa ākrośanaṁ parābhimukhyena vākya-yojanam, ākrośanam abhīṣvaṅgaḥ ity amaraḥ | valganaṁ yuddhāyepsita-gati-bhedaḥ ||13-14||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sva-saṁsthāḥ pratiyoddhur vākyādikaṁ vinaiva sva-jñāna-viṣayāś cet tadā ta eva katthitādayaḥ anubhāvāḥ syuḥ | āho-puruṣikā darpād vā syāt sambhāvanātmani | kṣveḍitaṁ siṁhanādaḥ | ākrośaḥ sāṭopa-vacanam | valganaṁ yuddhārtha-gati-viśeṣaḥ | yuddhecchā yuddhodyamaḥ ity ādy apare’nubhāvā jñeyāḥ ||13-14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.15 ||**

tatra **katthitam, **yathā—

**protsāhayasy atitarāṁ kim ivāgraheṇa **

**māṁ keśisūdana vidann api bhadrasenam |**

**yoddhuṁ balena samam atra sudurbalena **

**divyārgalā pratibhaṭas trapate bhujo me ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhadrasenaṁ vidann api, argalā-sadṛśo me bhujaḥ trapate ||15||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.16 ||**

**āhopuruṣikā**, yathā—

**dhṛtāṭope gopeśvara-jaladhi-candre parikaraṁ**

**nibadhnaty ullāsād bhuja-samara-caryā-samucitam |**

**sa-romāñcaṁ kṣveḍā-niviḍa-mukha-bimbasya naṭataḥ **

**sudāmnaḥ sotkaṇṭhaṁ jayati muhur āhopuruṣikā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **sa-romāñcaṁ sotkaṇṭhaṁ ca yathā syāt tathā naṭata iti yojyam ||16||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **ghṛtāṭopeti | sa-romāñcaṁ sotkaṇṭhaṁ yathā syāt tathā naṭataḥ ||16||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **“aham eva sarvotkṛṣṭa-yoddhā, yūyaṁ ke varākāḥ ?” iti dhṛtāṭope gopeśvara-jaladhi-candre gopeśvarī tathā nanda eva jaladhis tad-utpanne candre śrī-kṛṣṇe adbhuta-samaya-caryā-samucitaṁ parikaraṁ nibadhnati sati siṁha-nādena vyāpta-mukha-bimbasya tathā sa-romāñcaṁ yathā syāt tathā naṭataḥ sudāmnaḥ “aham eva sarvottama-yoddhā | mat-samaḥ ko’pi nāsti |” ity āhopuruṣikā jayati ||16||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.17-18 ||**

**catuṣṭaye’pi vīrāṇāṁ nikhilā eva sāttvikāḥ |**

**garvāvega-dhṛti-vrīḍā-mati-harṣāvahitthikāḥ |**

**amarṣotsukatāsūyā-smṛty-ādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**yuddhotsāha-ratis tasmin sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā |**

**yā sva-śakti-sahāyādyair āhāryā sahajāpi vā |**

**jigīṣā stheyasī yuddhe sā yuddhotsāha īryate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **yad atra jigīyety ādibhir yuddhotsāhādayo lakṣyante, tac ca—satvarā mānasā-śaktir utsāhaḥ [bha.ra.si. 2.5.57] iti pūrvokta-sāmānya-lakṣaṇāntargatam eva | tatrāpi gāḍhecchā-mātrasya vivakṣitatvāt ||18||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sva-śaktyā āhāryā sva-śaktyā sahajā | sahāyena āhāryā sahāyena sahajā yuddha-viṣaye atisthirā yā jetum icchā-ratiḥ sa yuddhotsāha ity anvayaḥ ||18||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.19 ||**

tatra **sva-śaktyā āhāryotsāha-ratir**, yathā—

**sva-tāta-śiṣṭyā sphuṭam apy anicchann **

**āhūyamānaḥ puruṣottamena |**

**sa stoka-kṛṣṇo dhṛta-yuddha-tṛṣṇaḥ**

**prodyamya daṇḍaṁ bhramayāñcakāra ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **svasya tātasya śiṣṭyā “hanta sarva-jīvanena yuddhyase, dhik tvām |” iti śāsanena sphuṭam anicchann ity arthaḥ | pāṭhāntaraṁ tyaktam ||19||

**mukundadāsaḥ : “**anicchur apy adya pitur nideśāt” iti [prathama-caraṇe] pāṭhaḥ | adya asminn evāhani pitur nideśāt, “he ajña ! sarva-prāṇa-bandhunā yudhyase ? dhik tvām | punar evaṁ na kuryāḥ |” iti śāsanād dhetoḥ | nideśaḥ śāsanopānta-bhāṣaṇeṣu prayujyate iti viśvaḥ ||19||

**viśvanāthaḥ : “**he putra ! tavādya janma-tithi-pūjanam | ato bālakaiḥ saha yuddhādikaṁ na kartavyam | śīghram eva gṛhe āgantavyam |” iti pitur nideśe’nicchur api kṛṣṇenāhūyamānaḥ san ||19||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.20 ||**

**sva-śaktyā sahajotsāha-ratir**, yathā—

**śukākāraṁ prekṣya me bāhu-daṇḍaṁ **

**mā tvaṁ bhaiṣīḥ kṣudra re bhadrasena |**

**helārambheṇādya nirjitya rāmaṁ **

**śrīdāmāhaṁ kṛṣṇam evāhvayeya ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : **āhvayeyeti spardhāyām ātmanepadam ||20||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **āhvayāmi krīḍāyai ākārayāmi ||20||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.21 ||**

yathā va—

**balasya balino balāt suhṛd-anīkam āloḍayan**

**payodhim iva mandaraḥ kṛta-mukunda-pakṣa-grahaḥ |**

**janaṁ vikaṭa-garjitair vadhirayan sa dhīra-svaro**

**hareḥ pramadam ekakaḥ samiti bhadraseno vyadhāt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **ekaka ekākī | ekādākinic cāsahāye iti pāṇini-sūtrāt kan | ekākī tv eka ekaka ity amaraḥ | ekala iti lekhaka-pramādāt ||21||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **ekala eka eva, 


    jāyate caikalaḥ prāṇī pralīyate tathaikalaḥ | 


    ekalaḥ sukṛtaṁ bhūṅkte’śnīyād duṣkṛtam ekalaḥ ||

tatra mūlyam api laulyam ekalam ity-ādi prayojād ekala-śabdo’pi ||21||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **balino baladevasya suhṛd-rūpam anīkaṁ senāṁ balād āloḍayan mandatva-parvato yathā samudram āloḍayati tadvat | samiti yuddhe ekaka ekākī, ekākī tv eka ekaka ity amaraḥ ||21||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.22 ||**

**sahāyenāhāryotsāha-ratir**, yathā—

**mayi valgati bhīma-vikrame**

**bhaja bhaṅgaṁ na hi saṅgarāditaḥ |**

**iti mitra-girā varūthapaḥ **

**sa-virūpaṁ viruvan hariṁ yayau ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **balena bhīma-vikrame mayi sati yudha-bhaṅgaṁ na bhajeti girā sa varūthapaḥ yathā virūpaṁ ghoraṁ yathā syāt tathā viruvan śabdaṁ kurvan yuddhārthaṁ hariṁ yayau tat-pakṣa-gataḥ babhūvety arthaḥ ||22||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.23 ||**

**sahāyena sahajotsāha-ratir**, yathā—

**saṅgrāma-kāmuka-bhujaḥ svayam eva kāmaṁ**

**dāmodarasya vijayāya kṛtī sudāmā |**

**sāhāyyam atra subalaḥ kurute balī cej**

**jāto maṇiḥ sujaṭito vara-hāṭakena ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **sujaṭita iti jaṭa jhaṭa saṅhāta ity asya ktānta-pratyaya-rūpam | jaṭilita iti pāṭhas tu neṣṭaḥ | jaītilo hi picchāditvādilaś ca jaṭāvān evābhidhīyate ||23||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **jaṭilitatvaṁ jaṭāvattvaṁ tac ca lakṣaṇayā paritaḥ parama-sauṣṭhavena veṣṭitatvaṁ bodhayati, rūpaṁ cedaṁ tat karoty artha-ṇij-anta-niṣṭhāntasya ||23||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śrī-kṛṣṇasya vijayāya śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ jetuṁ sudāmā svayam eva kṛtī paṇḍitaḥ | tatrāpi balī subalaḥ sāhāyyaṁ cet kurute tadā bhadram eva | yathā maṇiḥ svayam evotkṛṣṭaḥ, tatrāpi vara-hāṭakena śreṣṭha-suvarṇena jaḍito jātaś cet kiṁ punar vaktavyam ||23||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.24 ||**

**suhṛd eva pratibhaṭo vīre kṛṣṇasya na tv ariḥ |**

**sa bhakta-kṣobha-kāritvād raudre tv ālambano rase |**

**rāgābhāvo dṛg-ādīnāṁ raudrād asya vibhedakaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sa ariḥ raudre rase ālambanaḥ | raudra-rasāt vīra-rasasya bhedakaḥ | netrādīnāṁ rakitmābhāvaḥ raudra-rase krodha-vaśān netre raktimā jāyate | sakhibhiḥ saha vīra-rase tu tan nāstīti bhedo jñeyaḥ ||24||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.25-26 ||**

atha **dāna-vīraḥ—**

**dvi-vidho dāna-vīraḥ syād ekas tatra bahu-pradaḥ |**

**upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī cāpara ucyate ||**

tatra **bahu-pradaḥ— **

**sahasā dīyate yena svayaṁ sarvasvam apy uta |**

**dāmodarasya saukhyāya procyate sa bahu-pradaḥ ||**

_na kenāpi vyākhyātam |_

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.27-30 ||**

**sampradānasya vīkṣādyā asminn uddīpanā matāḥ |**

**vāñchitādhika-dātṛtvaṁ smita-pūrvābhibhāṣaṇam ||27||**

**sthairya-dākṣiṇya-dhairyādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ |**

**vitarkautsukya-harṣādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||28||**

**dānotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā |**

**pragāḍhā stheyasī ditsā dānotsāha itīryate ||29||**

**dvidhā bahu-prado’py eṣa vidvadbhir iha kathyate |**

**syād ābhyudayikas tv ekaḥ paras tat-sampradānakaḥ ||30||**

**viśvanāthaḥ : sampradānasya** sat-pātrasya ||27-30||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.31-32 ||**

tatra **ābhyudāyikaḥ—**

**kṛṣṇasyābhyudayārthaṁ tu yena sarvasvam arpyate |**

**arthibhyo brāhmaṇādibhyaḥ sa ābhyudāyiko bhavet ||**

yathā—

**vrajapatir iha sūnor jātakārthaṁ tathāsau**

**vyatarad amala-cetāḥ sañcayaṁ naicikīnām |**

**pṛthur api nṛga-kīrtiḥ sāmprataṁ saṁvṛtāsīd**

**iti nijagadur uccair bhūsurā yena tṛptāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : nṛga-kīrteḥ** **saṁvṛtatve** hetuḥ—**amala-cetāḥ** putra-svarūpa-śrī-kṛṣṇasyodaya-mātra-tatparatayā, na tadval loka-dvaya-gata-lābha-pratiṣṭhā-kāmanā-doṣa-yukta ity arthaḥ ||32||

**viśvanāthaḥ : naicikīnāṁ** dhenūnāṁ **sañcayaṁ** samūhaṁ nandaḥ brāhmaṇebhyo’dāt | **nṛga-kīrteḥ** **saṁvṛtatve** hetuḥ—**amala-cetāḥ** putra-svarūpa-śrī-kṛṣṇasyodaya-mātra-tatparatayā, na tadval loka-dvaya-gata-lābha-pratiṣṭhā-kāmanā-doṣa-yukta ity arthaḥ ||32||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.33-34 ||**

atha **tat-sampradānakaḥ—**

**jñātaye haraye svīyam ahaṁtā-mamatāspadam |**

**sarvasvaṁ dīyate yena sa syāt tat-sampradānakaḥ ||**

**tad-dānaṁ prīti-pūjābhyāṁ bhaved ity uditaṁ dvidhā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : uditaṁ** pūrvoktaṁ tad-dānaṁ **dvidhā** bhaved ity anvayaḥ ||34||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.35-36 ||**

tatra **prīti-dānam—**

**prīti-dānaṁ tu tasmai yad dadyād bandhv-ādi-rūpiṇe ||**

yathā—

**cārcikyaṁ vaijayantīṁ paṭam uru-puraṭodbhāsuraṁ bhūṣaṇānāṁ**

**śreṇiṁ māṇikya-bhājaṁ gaja-ratha-turagān karburān karbureṇa |**

**dattvā rājyaṁ kuṭumbaṁ svam api bhagavate ditsur apy anyad uccair**

**deyaṁ kutrāpy adṛṣṭvā makha-sadasi tadā vyākulaḥ pāṇḍavo’bhūt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **karbureṇa suvarṇena, karburān miśrān makha-sadasi tadeti agrya-pūjāvasara iti na vyākhyeyam | kintu sarva-vidh-pūrty-anantara ity eva | pūrvasya pūrāntargatatvāt | uttaratra vipra-rūpāyety upalakṣaṇaṁ vipra-deva-bhagavad-rūpāyety asya vivakṣitatvāt ||36||

**mukunda-dāsaḥ : **cārcikyaṁ candana-paṅkādi, māṇikyaṁ bhajatīti tad-bhāk tām | karbureṇa svarṇena karburān miśrān makha-sadasi tadā pūjāvasare ||36||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bandhv-ādi-rūpiṇe tasmai śrī-kṛṣṇāya | karbureṇa suvarṇena, karburān miśrān | makhasya rājasūyasya sarva-vidh-pūrty-anantaraṁ sabhāyāṁ pāṇḍavo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ||36||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.37-38 ||**

**pujā-dānaṁ—**

**pujā-dānaṁ tu tasmai yad vipra-rūpāya dīyate ||**

yathā aṣṭame (8.20.11) —

**yajanti yajñaṁ kratubhir yam ādṛtā**

**bhavanta āmnāya-vidhāna-kovidāḥ |**

**sa eva viṣṇur varado’stu vā paro**

**dāsyāmy amuṣmai kṣitim īpsitāṁ mune ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śukrācāryaṁ prati balir āha—vedokta-vidhāne paṇḍitā bhavantaḥ yaṁ yajanti | aparaḥ śatrur vā astu ||38||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.39 ||**

yathā vā daśa-rūpake (4.74f)[^3]—

**lakṣmī-payodharotsaṅga-kuṅkumāruṇito hareḥ |**

**balinaiva sa yenāsya bhikṣā-pātrīkṛtaḥ karaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **yena balinety asya pūrakas tac-chabdas tu tat-prakaraṇa eva labhyaḥ ||39||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **lakṣmī-stana-sambandhi-kuṅkumenāruṇito yo hareḥ karaḥ, yena balinā bhikṣā-pātrīkṛtaḥ ||39||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.40 ||**

atha **upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī—**

**upasthita-durāpārtha-tyagy asau yena neṣyate |**

**hariṇā dīyamāno’pi sārṣṭy-ādis tuṣyatā varaḥ ||40||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **upasthiteti | yadyapi siddha-sādhaka-bhedena dvividho’yaṁ sambhavati, tathāpi yat kiñcij jāta-rucir dṛḍhāgrahaḥ sādhaka evātra lakṣyate | na tu samyag-bhagavan-mādhuryānubhava-siddhaḥ | na hy amṛtāsvāde labdhe guḍādi-tyāgī tathā praśasyate, tasya tasyāpi bhakty-ekāgraha-dṛṣṭyā **tuṣṭaḥ** śrī-hariḥ tad-āgraha-vyakty-arthaṁ kadācit taṁ dātum iva protsāhayatīti | **vara** ity anyair vriyamāṇo’pīty arthaḥ ||40||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **pūjārthatve’pi vipra-rūpābhāvāt prīti-dānam eva | upasthite tulyatā-svāśrayaṇāt prītiṁ kurvatā sārṣṭy-ādiś caturdhā muktis tad-rūpo varaḥ pūrvam abhīṣṭaḥ, yena mukti-bhukti-bahuvidha-saṁsāra-duḥkha-nivṛtty-arthaṁ parama-sukṛtena bhagavad-āśrayaṇāt bhagavad-bhakta-kṛpayā jāta-ratitayā tat-tad-icchā-śūnyena jñāni-cara-śaraṇya-bhakti-bhakta-vargeṇety arthaḥ ||40||

**viśvanāthaḥ : tuṣyatā hariṇā dīyamāno’pi sārṣṭy-ādi-varaḥ** **yena neṣyate, sa upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī** ||40||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.41-42 ||**

**pūrvato’tra viparyasta-kārakatvaṁ dvayor bhavet |**

**asminn uddīpanāḥ kṛṣṇa-kṛpālāpa-smitādayaḥ ||**

**anubhāvās tad-utkarṣa-varṇana-draḍhimādayaḥ |**

**atra sañcāritā bhūmnā dhṛter eva samīkṣyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : viparyasta-kārakatvam**--harer apādānatvaṁ bhaktasya tu sampradānatvam ity eva | **bhūmnā** atiśayena **samīkṣyate** ||41-42||

**mukundadāsaḥ : viparyasta-kārakatvaṁ** harer apādānatvaṁ bhaktasya sampradānatvam ||41||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dvayor bhakta-bhagavator **viparyasta-kārakatvaṁ** bhagavato’pādānatvaṁ, bhaktasya tu sampradānatvam iti pūrvasmāt viparyayo jñeyaḥ ||41|| **dhṛter** dhairya-sañcāriṇa eva bhūmnātiśayena sañcāriṇo īkṣyate ||41-42||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.43 ||**

**tyāgotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihoditaḥ |**

**tyāgecchā tādṛśī prauḍhā tyāgotsāha itīryate ||**

**sarve : **tādṛśī sārṣṭy-ādy-anicchā-mayī ||43||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.44 ||**

yathā hari-bhakti-sudhodaye (7.28)—

**sthānābhilāṣī tapasi sthito’haṁ**

**tvāṁ prāptavān deva-munīndra-guhyam |**

**kācaṁ vicinvann api divya-ratnaṁ**

**svāmin kṛtārtho’smi varaṁ na yāce ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : sthāna-** iti śrī-dhruva-vākyam | tad idam api na samyaṅ-mādhuryānubhava-mayam | śrī-bhāgavate hi pāñcajanyasya sparśād eva tena tat tad uktaṁ, kintu kramād evānubhūtam iti vyaktam ||44||

**mukundadāsaḥ : sthāna-** iti dhruva-vākyam | dhruva-sthānasya bhagaval-lokatvāt tatra caturdhā muktim ity arthaḥ ||44||

**viśvanāthaḥ : sthāna-** iti śrī-dhruva-vākyam | **sthānaṁ** rāja-siṁhāsanaṁ tat-kāmo’haṁ yathā **kācaṁ** **vicinvan** jano divya-ratnaṁ prāpya kṛtārtho bhavati, punaḥ kācaṁ na yācate, tadvad **varaṁ na yāce** ||44||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.45 ||**

yathā vā tṛtīye, (3.15.48)—

**nātyantikaṁ vigaṇayanty api te prasādaṁ**

**kiṁ vānyad arpita-bhayaṁ bhruva unnayais te |**

**ye’ṅga tvad-aṅghri-śaraṇā bhavataḥ kathāyāḥ**

**kīrtanya-tīrtha-yaśasaḥ kuśalā rasa-jñāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : nātyantikam** ity-ādināpi tādṛśa-sādhakā eva vivakṣitāḥ | kuśalā ity anenoktānāṁ bhakti-rasa-śāstrānusāreṇa vivekinām evātrodāhriyamāṇatvaṁ, na tu kaimutyenottaratroktānāṁ rasajñānām iti | **te** tava, **bhruva unnayair** vikṣepa-rūpaiḥ kālaiḥ ||45||

**mukundadāsaḥ : tvad-aṅghri-śaraṇaṁ** rakṣitā yeṣāṁ te tathā jāta-ratayaḥ śaraṇyā ity arthaḥ | ata eva **bhavataḥ kathāyā rasajñāḥ** ||45||

**viśvanāthaḥ : ātyantikaṁ** mokṣaṁ **te prasādaṁ na gaṇayanti**, **tava bhruva unnayair** vikṣepaka-rūpaiḥ kālaiḥ **arpitataram** anyat svargādikaṁ kiṁ gaṇayanti ? evaṁ-bhūtāḥ ke ? tatrāha—**ye** iti | **kīrtanārhaṁ tīrtha-**rūpaṁ yasya tasya **bhagavataḥ kathāyā** ye **rasajñās** ta eva nānye ||45||

 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.46 ||**

**ayam eva bhavann uccaiḥ prauḍha-bhāva-viśeṣa-bhāk |**

**dhuryādīnāṁ tṛtīyasya vīrasya padavīṁ vrajet ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : prauḍha-bhāva-viśeṣa-bhāk** kaścid evety arthaḥ | viśeṣa-śabdo hy atra tādṛśa-dāsya-paryavasānārthaḥ | anyābhilāṣitā-śūnyam [bha.ra.si. 1.1.10] ity-ādibhir asakṛd eva sarvasyāpi bhaktasya tādṛśatayā prāptatvāt ||46||

**mukundadāsaḥ : prauḍha-bhāva-viśeṣaḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇa-niṣṭhaḥ | **bhavann** iti sādhakatvaṁ bodhitam ||46||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ayam upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī **prauḍha**-dāsya-rūpa-**bhāva-viśeṣa**-bhāg **bhavan** ||46||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.47-50 ||**

atha **dayā-vīraḥ—**

**kṛpārdra-hṛdayatvena khaṇḍaśo deham arpayan |**

**kṛṣṇāyācchanna-kṛpāya dayā-vīra ihocyate ||**

**uddīpanā iha proktās tad-ārti-vyañjanādayaḥ |**

**nija-prāṇa-vyayenāpi vipanna-trāṇa-śīlatā ||**

**āśvāsanoktayaḥ sthairyam ity ādyās tatra vikriyāḥ |**

**autsukyam atiharṣādyā jñeyāḥ sañcāriṇo budhaiḥ ||**

**dayotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāva udīryate |**

**dayodreka-bhṛd utsāho dayotsāha ihoditaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **yasmin +++

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.51 ||**

yathā—

**vande kuḍmalitāñjalir muhur ahaṁ vīraṁ mayūra-dhvajaṁ**

**yenārdhaṁ kapaṭa-dvijāya vapuṣaḥ kaṁsa-dviṣe ditsatā |**

**kaṣṭaṁ gadgadikākulo’smi kathanārambhād aho dhīmatā**

**sollāsaṁ krakacena dāritam abhūt patnī-sutābhyāṁ śivaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : vanda** ity-ādau **kaṣṭam** ity-ādi-garbhita-doṣo'pi camatkāra-poṣakatvād guṇaḥ | yathā sāhitya-darpaṇādau—


    diṅ-mātaṅga-ghaṭā-vibhakta-caturā ghāṭā mahī sādhyate


    siddhā sā ca vadanta eva hi vayaṁ romāñcitāḥ paśyata |


    viprāya pratipādyate kim aparaṁ rāmāya tasmai namo


    yasmād āvirabhūt kathādbhutam idaṁ yatraiva cāntaṁ gatam || [sā.da. 7.37][^4] 

ity-ādi-padyāni darśitāni | garbhitatvaṁ ca yad vākyāntara-madhyaṁ vākyāntaraṁ praviśatīti | evam anyatrāpi samādheyam ||51||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vanda** ity-ādau **kaṣṭam** ity-ādi garbhita-doṣo'pi camatkāra-poṣakatvād guṇaḥ | yathā sāhitya-darpaṇādau—diṅ-mātaṅga-ghaṭā [sā.da. 7.37] ity-ādi-padyāni darśitāni | garbhitatvaṁ ca yad vākyāntara-madhyaṁ vākyāntaraṁ praviśatīti | evam anyatrāpi jñeyam ||51||

**viśvanāthaḥ : kapaṭa-dvijāya** kṛṣṇāya **vapuṣo’rdhaṁ ditsatā** yena **dhīmatā** “karāta” iti prasiddhena **krakacena** karaṇena **patnī-putrābhyāṁ** dvārā sva-śiraḥ **sollāsaṁ** yathā syāt tathā **dāritaṁ**, taṁ **mayūra-dhvajam** ahaṁ vande, yasya ceṣṭāyāḥ **kathanārambhata** eva **ahaṁ** **gadgadākulo’smi** | idam eva mahat **kaṣṭam** iti bhāvaḥ ||51||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.52-54 ||**

**hareś cet tattva-vijñānaṁ naivāsya ghaṭate dayā |**

**tad-abhāve tv asau dāna-vīre’ntar bhavati sphuṭam ||**

**vaiṣṇavatvād ratiḥ kṛṣṇe kriyate’nena sarvadā |**

**kṛtātra dvija-rūpe ca bhaktis tenāsya bhaktatā ||**

**antar-bhāvaṁ vadanto’sya dāna-vīre dayātmanaḥ |**

**vopadevādayo dhīrā vīram ācakṣate tridhā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : harer** iti | tataś ca **tad-abhāve** tasyā dayāyā abhāva ity arthaḥ ||52|| **vaiṣṇavatvād** iti | viṣṇur bhaktir bhajanīyo’syeti vaiṣṇavaḥ | sā ca bhaktiḥ [pā. 4.3.95] ity anena sūtreṇa śaiṣikād aṇ-vidhānāt | tataś ca vaiṣṇavatvād viṣṇu-bhakti-yuktatvād ity arthaḥ ||53||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vaiṣṇavatvād** iti | bhajyate iti bhaktiḥ | viṣṇur bhaktir asyeti vaiṣṇavaḥ | sā ca bhaktiḥ [pā. 4.3.95] iti sūtreṇa śaiṣikād aṇ-vidhānāt | tataś ca vaiṣṇavatvaṁ viṣṇau bhaktimattvād ity arthaḥ ||53||

**viśvanāthaḥ : harer** iti | nāyaṁ brāhmaṇaḥ, kintu harir eveti tattva-vijñāne dayā notpadyate, tataś ca tad-abhāve tasyā dayāyā abhāve ||52|| **vaiṣṇavatvād** viṣṇu-bhakti-yuktatvāt dvija-rūpe kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ kṛtā, tena hetunā asya bhaktatā jñeyā ||53||

vopadevādayaḥ paṇḍitāḥ asya dayā-vīrasya dāna-vīre evāntar-bhāvaṁ vadantas tridhā trividhā eva vīram ācakṣate, na tu caturdhā ||54||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.55-57 ||**

atha **dharma-vīraḥ—**

**kṛṣṇaika-toṣaṇe dharme yaḥ sadā pariniṣṭhitaḥ |**

**prāyeṇa dhīra-śāntas tu dharma-vīraḥ sa ucyate ||55||**

**uddīpanā iha proktāḥ sac-chāstra-śravaṇādayaḥ |**

**anubhāvā nayāstikya-sahiṣṇutva-yamādayaḥ |**

**mati-smṛti-prabhṛtayo vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇah ||56||**

**dharmotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihocyate |**

**dharmaikābhiniveśas tu dharmotsāho mataḥ satām ||57||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam |_

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.58 ||**

yathā—

**bhavad abhi rati-hetūn kurvatā sapta-tantūn**

**puram abhi puru-hūte nityam evopahūte |**

**danuja-damana tasyāḥ pāṇḍu-putreṇa gaṇḍaḥ**

**suciram araci śacyāḥ savya-hastāṅka-śāyī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **sapta-tantūn yajñān ||58||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **sapta-tantur yajñaḥ | puruhūte indre ||58||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he danuja-damana ! bhavataḥ prīti-hetūn sapta-tantūn yajñān kurvatā pāṇḍu-putreṇa yudhiṣṭhireṇa puram abhi sva-pure puruhūte indre yajña-bhāga-grahaṇārthaṁ nityam eva upahūte sati tasyā śacyāḥ gaṇḍaḥ vāma-hastāṅka-śāyī cira-kālaṁ vyāpya araci | tathā ca nityaṁ yajña-bhāga-grahaṇārtham āgatasya indrasya viraheṇa śacī vāma-hasta-tale gaṇḍaṁ dattvā śocati smety arthaḥ ||58||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.3.59-61 ||**

**yajñaḥ pūjā-viśeṣo’sya bhujādy-aṅgāni vaiṣṇavaḥ |**

**dhyātvendrādy-āśrayatvena yad eṣv āhutir arpyate ||**

**ayaṁ tu sākṣāt tasyaiva nideśāt kurute makhān |**

**yudhiṣṭhiro’mbudhiḥ premṇāṁ mahā-bhāgavatottamaḥ ||**

**dānādi-trividhaṁ vīraṁ varṇayantaḥ parisphuṭam |**

**dharma-vīraṁ na manyante katicid dhanikādayaḥ**[^5]** ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **athātra vaiṣṇavair yad indrāya svāhety āhutir arpyate, tat khalu indrādi-lokapālāśrayatvena bhagavad-bhujādy-aṅgānāṁ pūjanam eva jñeyam | tathā cendrādayo bhagavad-bhujāṅgānāṁ vibhūtaya iti buddhyaiva vaiṣṇavair āhutir arpyate | na tu indraḥ svatantra-devatā, tasyārādhanam asmābhiḥ | kriyate iti buddhyety āśayenāha—yajña iti | asya bhagavataḥ bhujādy-aṅgāni vaiṣṇavair indrādy-āśrayatvena dhyātvā eṣu yajña-pūjā-viśeṣa-rūpā āhutir arpyate yat, ato vaiṣṇavānām ananyāś cintayanto mām [gītā 9.22] iti gītoktānanyatvasyāhānir iti jñeyam ||59||

 —o)0(o—

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

vīra-bhakti-rasa-laharī tṛtīyā 

|| 4.3 ||

(4.4)


### karuṇa-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### caturtha-laharī

**|| 4.4.1-3 ||**

**ātmocitair vibhāvādyair nītā puṣṭiṁ satāṁ hṛdi |**

**bhavec choka-ratir bhakti-raso hi karuṇābhidhaḥ ||**

**avyucchinna-mahānando’py eṣa prema-viśeṣataḥ |**

**aniṣṭāpteḥ padatayā vedyaḥ kṛṣṇo’sya ca priyaḥ ||**

**tathānavāpta-tad-bhakti-saukhyaś ca sva-priyo janaḥ |**

**ity asya viṣayatvena jñeyā ālambanās tridhā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : avyucchinna-mahānando’pi** **eṣa** śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ yadyapy asminn ānanda-svarūpe’niṣṭa-sambhāvanā nāsti, tathāpi **prema-viśeṣād** dhetoḥ **aniṣṭa-prāpter** āspadatayā **ve**

**dyaḥ** karuṇa-rasa-viṣayaḥ | evam **asya** śrī-kṛṣṇasyāpi **priya-janaḥ** karuṇa-rasa-viṣayaḥ ||2||

tathā **anavāpta-tad-bhakti-saukhyaḥ** vaiṣṇavatvādy-abhāvena bhagavad-bhakti-sukha-rahitaḥ, **sva-priya-janaḥ** sveṣāṁ bhaktānāṁ pitṛ-putrādi-bandhu-vargaḥ karuṇa-rasa-viṣayaḥ | evaṁ sati asya rasasya trividha-jana eva viṣayālambano jñeyaḥ ||3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.4-5 ||**

**tat-tad-vedī ca tad-bhakta āśrayatvena ca tridhā |**

**so’py aucityena vijñeyaḥ prāyaḥ śāntādi-varjitaḥ |**

**tat-karma-guṇa-rūpādyā bhavaty uddīpanā iha ||**

**anubhāvā mukhe śoṣo vilāpaḥ srasta-gātratā |**

**śvāsa-krośana-bhūpāta-ghātoras tāḍanādayaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : tat-tad-vedī** tādṛśa-kṛṣṇādi-trayānubhavitā ||4|| **anubhāvā** iti | **bhuvi pātaḥ** bhuvi **ghātaś** ca hastena bhū-tāḍanam iti dvayaṁ jñeyam ||5||

**mukundadāsaḥ : tat-tad-vedī** tādṛśa-kṛṣṇādi-trayasyānubhavitā | śāntādīty atrādi-śabdo’dhikṛta-śaraṇyānāṁ grāhakaḥ ||4|| **anubhāvā** iti | **bhuvi pāta-ghātau** tatra ghāto hastena bhū-tāḍanam ||5||

**viśvanāthaḥ : tat-tad-vedī** tādṛśa-kṛṣṇādi-trayānubhava-kartā trividho bhakta-janaḥ | asya rasasya **āśrayālambano jñeyaḥ** | śānta-bhakteṣu prāyaḥ karuṇa-raso nodetīti bhāvaḥ ||4|| **anubhāvā** iti | **bhuvi pātaḥ** **bhuvi ghātaś** ca hastena bhū-tāḍanam iti dvayaṁ jñeyam ||5||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.6-7 ||**

**atrāṣṭau sāttvikā jāḍya-nirveda-glāni-dīnatāḥ |**

**cintā-viṣāda-autsukya-cāpalonmāda-mṛtyavaḥ |**

**ālasyāpasmṛti-vyādhi-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**hṛdi śokatayāṁśena gatā pariṇatiṁ ratiḥ |**

**uktā śoka-ratiḥ saiva sthāyī bhāva ihocyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : aṁśena** aniṣṭāpti-pratīti-rūpeṇa nija-viśeṣaṇena ||7||

**mukundadāsaḥ : aṁśena** aniṣṭāpti-jñāna-rūpeṇa nija-viśeṣaṇena | pūrvaṁ hāsādīnāṁ sarveṣāṁ śuddha-sattvato bhinnatayoktis tu prācuryād iti jñeyam ||7||

**viśvanāthaḥ : aṁśena** aniṣṭāpti-pratīti-rūpeṇa svīya-viśeṣaṇena ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.8 ||**

tatra **kṛṣṇo**, yathā śrī-daśame (10.16.10)—

**taṁ nāga-bhoga-parivītam adṛṣṭa-ceṣṭam **

**ālokya tat-priya-sakhāḥ paśupā bhṛśārtāḥ |**

**kṛṣṇe’rpitātma-suhṛd-artha-kalatra-kāmā **

**duḥkhānuśoka-bhayam ūḍha-dhiyo nipetuḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : tat-priya-sakhāś** ca **paśupāś** cānye gopāḥ ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : suhṛt**-śabdena gṛhītasyāpi **kalatrasya** pṛthaṅ-nirdeśo viśeṣa-vivakṣayā ||8||

**viśvanāthaḥ : tat-priya-sakhāś** ca **paśupāś** cānye ||8||

 

 —o)0(o—

	

**|| 4.4.9 ||**

yathā vā—

**phaṇi-hradam avagāḍhe dāruṇaṁ piñcha-cūḍe**

**skhalad-aśiśira-bāṣpa-stoma-dhautottarīyā |**

**nikhila-karaṇa-vṛtti-stambhinīm ālalambe **

**viṣam agatim avasthāṁ goṣṭha-rājasya rājñī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : phaṇi-hradam** iti | "goṣṭha-rājasya patnī" iti pāṭhāntaram ||9||

**mukundadāsaḥ : goṣṭha-rājasya rājñī** strī ||9||

**viśvanāthaḥ : dāruṇaṁ** kāliya-hradaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇe’**vagāḍhe** sati **bāṣpa**-samūhena **dhautam uttarīya**-vastraṁ yasyā evaṁ-bhūtā yaśodā **nikhilāntaḥ-karaṇa-vṛtti-stambhinīm** avasthām ālalambe ||9||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.10 ||**

**tasya priya-jano**, yathā—

**kṛṣṇa-priyāṇām ākarṣe śaṅkhacūḍena nirmite |**

**nīlāmbarasya vaktrendur nīlimānaṁ muhur dadhe ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : śrī-kṛṣṇasya** śrī-rādhādi-**priyāṇām** **ākarṣe** kṛte sati **nīlāmbarasya** baladevasya mukhaṁ **nīlimānaṁ** **dadhe** | śokena vaivarṇya-sāttvikodaya-jāta iti bhāvaḥ ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.11 ||**

**sva-priyo**, yathā haṁsadūte (54)—

**virājante yasya vraja-śiśu-kula-steya-vikala-**

**svayambhū-cūḍāgrair lulita-śikharāḥ pāda-nakharāḥ |**

**kṣaṇaṁ yān ālokya prakaṭa-paramānanda-vivaśaḥ**

**sa devarṣir muktān api tanu-bhṛtaḥ śocati bhṛśam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : virājanta** iti | **lulita** iti lulitvaṁ vimarditatvaṁ “lul vimardana” ity asya niṣṭhāyāṁ prayogāt | atra tv atyanta-saṁsparśatāparyakatvena arthāntara-saṅkramitatvam eva jñeyam | **tanu**-**bhṛta** ity atra "muni-gaṇān" iti pāṭhaḥ | sva-priya-viṣayatvena yuktaḥ ||11||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **“lul vimardana” iti vimardo vācyo’rthaḥ | saṁsparśo lakṣyaḥ | sa prīti-gaurava-sparśo vyaṅgyaḥ | **tanubhṛta** ity atra "muni-gaṇān" ity api pāṭhaḥ ||11||

**viśvanāthaḥ : yasya** śrī-kṛṣṇasya **pāda-nakharā virājante** | kathambhūtāḥ ? **śiśu-gaṇa-cauryeṇa** brahmaṇā mukuṭāgraiḥ karaṇena **lulitāḥ** marditāḥ **śikharā** agra-bhāgā yeṣāṁ, tathā-bhūtāḥ | “lul mardane” ity asya niṣṭhāyāṁ prayogāt | **yān pāda-nakharān ālokya** **paramānanda-vivaśo** **devarṣir** nāradaḥ sva-jātīyatvena **priyān** muni-gaṇān **muktān** prāpta-sādhu-janān **śocati** | sāṁsārikāṇāṁ nāradādi-mahad-anugraha-vaśāt kadācit caraṇāravinda-mādhuryānubhave sambhāvanā vartate, tasmān na śocati | prāpta-sāyujyānāṁ tu punar-utthānābhāvāt sambhāvanāpi nāstīti tān śocatīti jñeyam ||11||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.12 ||**

yathā vā—

**mātar mādri gatā kutas tvam adhunā hā kvāsi pāṇḍo pitaḥ**

**sāndrānanda-sudhābdhir eṣa yuvayor nābhūd dṛśāṁ gocaraḥ |**

**ity uccair nakulānujo vilapati prekṣya pramodākulo**

**govindasya padāravinda-yugala-proddāma-kānti-cchaṭām ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : nakulānujaḥ** sahadevaḥ **govindasya padāravindayoḥ** **kānti-cchaṭā prekṣya vilapati** ||12||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.13-14 ||**

**ratiṁ vināpi ghaṭate hāsyāder udgamaḥ kvacit |**

**kadācid api śokasya nāsya sambhāvanā bhavet ||**

**rater bhūmnā kraśimnā ca śoko bhūyān kṛśaś ca saḥ |**

**ratyā sahāvinā-bhāvāt kāpy etasya viśiṣṭatā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : **kāpi viśiṣṭatā hāsādibhyo’nirvacanīyaṁ svāda-vaiśiṣṭyam ||14||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **rater bhūmnā ādhikyena **śoko**’pi **bhūyān**, bhūyāt, **rateḥ kraśimnā** alpatvena śoko’pi **kṛśaḥ** alpo bhavet | etasya śokasya **ratyā** **sahāvinābhāvāt** śokotpattir na jāyate, hāsādy-apekṣayā viśiṣṭatā ādhikyaṁ jñeyā ity arthaḥ ||14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.4.15-16 ||**

api ca—

**kṛṣṇaiśvaryādy-avijñānaṁ kṛtaṁ naiṣām avidyayā |**

**kintu premottara-rasa-viśeṣeṇaiva tat kṛtam ||15||**

**ataḥ prādurbhavan śoko labdhvāpy udbhaṭatāṁ muhuḥ |**

**durūhām eva tanute gatiṁ saukhyasya kām api ||16||**

 

**śrī-jīvaḥ : kṛṣṇaiśvarya** iti | etad uktaṁ bhavati—bhagavān nāma svarūpa-bhūta-bhagavattā-viśiṣṭaḥ paramānanda-svarūpaḥ | tad uktaṁ caturthe—


    tvaṁ pratyag-ātmani tadā bhagavaty ananta


    ānanda-mātra upapanna-samasta-śaktau [bhā.pu. 4.11.30] iti |


    jñāna-śakti-balaiśvarya-vīrya-tejāṁsy aśeṣataḥ |


    bhagavac-chabda-vācyāni vinā heyair guṇādibhiḥ || [vi.pu. 6.5.79] iti |

bhagavattā tu ṣaḍ-vidhatve’pi sāmānyato dvividhā | paramaiśvarya-rūpā parama-mādhurya-rūpā ceti | tatraiśvaryaṁ nāma prabhāvena vaśīkartṛtvaṁ, yad-anubhavena tasmād bhaya-sambhramādi syāt | mādhuryaṁ tu rūpa-guṇa-līlānāṁ rocakatvaṁ, yad-anubhavena tasmin prema syāt | kevalaṁ svarūpaṁ tu svānanda-mātra-samarpakam | tatra mādhuryānubhavas tu tad-dvayasyāpy anubhavam āvṛṇoti | yathā—tasyāravinda-nayanasya [bhā.pu. 3.15.43] ity atra saṅkṣobham akṣara-juṣām api citta-tanvoḥ iti śrī-sanakādibhis tad-darśane | yathā ca—


    janma te mayy asau pāpo mā vidyān madhusūdana |


    samudvije bhavad-dhetoḥ kaṁsād aham adhīra-dhīḥ || [bhā.pu. 10.3.29] 

ity atra devakī-vākye | sa ca mādhuryānubhavo mādhurya-bhāvanātmaka-sādhanotpanna-prema-viśeṣa-labdha-rasa-paryāyāsvāda-viśeṣaḥ | tasmāt tena yad-aiśvaryādy-anubhavāvaraṇaṁ tat-sarvottama-vidyāmayam eveti brahma-jñānād arvācīnā tv avidyā kathaṁ tatrāvakāśaṁ labhatām ? yathā śrī-baladevasyāpi tan-maṅgalārthaṁ prayatnaḥ śrūyate—


    śrutvaitad bhagavān rāmo vipakṣīya-nṛpodyamam |


    kṛṣṇaṁ caikaṁ gataṁ hartuṁ kanyāṁ kalaha-śaṅkitaḥ ||


    balena mahatā sārdhaṁ bhrātṛ-sneha-pariplutaḥ |


    tvaritaḥ kuṇḍinaṁ prāgād gajāśva-ratha-pattibhiḥ || [bhā.pu. 10.53.20-21] iti |

śrī-yudhiṣṭhirasyāpi, yathā—


    ajāta-śatruḥ pṛtanāṁ gopīthāya madhu-dviṣaḥ |


    parebhyaḥ śaṅkitaḥ snehāt prāyuṅkta catur-aṅgiṇīm || [bhā.pu. 1.10.32] iti |

yasmād evam atas tadānīm api premānanda-maya-kṛṣṇānanda-sphuraṇāt, tad-upalakṣitāt tādṛśa-prema-svabhāvena kathañcit sambhāvanena vā pratyāśānugamāt paryavasāne’pi tat-sukhasyaivābhyudayād asau saukhyasya gatim eva tanute | kintu durūhām āgantuka-duḥkhānubhavenāvṛtām | ata eva kām api anirvacanīyām ity arthaḥ | tasmād asty eva karuṇe’pi sukhamayatvam iti bhāvaḥ ||15-16||

**mukundaḥ : kṛṣṇaiśvarya**- iti | ataḥ **premottara-rasa-viśeṣa-kṛtāt kṛṣṇaiśvaryādy-avijñānāt** prādurbhavan, **durūhāṁ** śoka-kṛtatvāt tarkāgocarām | ataḥ **kām api** śokātītām [gatiṁ] | **eva**-kārāt na tu gocarām ||15-16||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atha **aiśvarya**-jñāna-sattve śrī-kṛṣṇe aniṣṭānusandhānaṁ notpadyate, aniṣṭānusandhānaṁ vinā śokotpattir na jāyate, aiśvaryasyājñānaṁ prema-viśeṣeṇaiva kṛtaṁ, na tu avidyayā, māyottīrṇeṣu tādṛśa-siddha-bhakteṣu avidyāyā adhikārābhāvād ity āśayenāha—**kṛṣṇaiśvarya**- iti | **udbhaṭatāṁ** **labdho’pi śokaḥ kām apy** anirvacanīyāṁ **saukhyasya gatiṁ tanute** | kintu **durūhām** āgantuka-duḥkhānubhavenāvṛtāṁ, tādṛśa-duḥkha-sukha-rūpatvaṁ yuktyā prāk pratipāditam | tasmād asty eva karuṇa-rase’pi sukhamayatvam iti bhāvaḥ ||15-16||

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

karuṇa-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī 

|| 4.4 ||

 —o)0(o—



(4.5)


### raudra-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### pañcama-laharī

**|| 4.5.1-2 ||**

**nītā krodha-ratiḥ puṣṭiṁ vibhāvādyair nijocitaiḥ |**

**hṛdi bhakta-janasyāsau raudra-bhakti-raso bhavet ||**

**kṛṣṇo hito’hitaś ceti krodhasya viṣayas tridhā |**

**kṛṣṇe sakhī-jaraty-ādyāḥ krodhasyāśrayatāṁ gatāḥ |**

**bhaktāḥ sarva-vidhā eva hite caivāhite tathā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhakta-janasya hṛdi vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṁ prāptā **krodha-ratir** eva **raudra-bhakti-raso bhaved** ity anvayaḥ ||1|| **kṛṣṇe** kṛṣṇa-viṣaye **krodhasya** **sakhī-jaraty-ādyāḥ sarva-vidhā bhaktā** evāśrayālambāḥ | evaṁ **hite** viṣaye **ahite** viṣaye ca krodhasya sakhī-jaraty-ādyā āśrayālambanā bhavantīty anvayaḥ ||1-2||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.3 ||**

tatra **kṛṣṇe sakhyāḥ krodhaḥ—**

**sakhī-krodhe bhavet sakhyāḥ kṛṣṇād atyāhite sati ||3||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : atyāhitaṁ** mahā-bhītiḥ | kṛṣṇād ity apādānaṁ bhaya-hetur iti smaraṇāt ||3||

**mukundaḥ : atyāhitaṁ** mahā-bhītiḥ ||3||

**viśvanāthaḥ : sakhyāḥ** sva-yūtheśvaryāḥ śrī-**kṛṣṇāt atyāhite** atibhaye sati śrī-kṛṣṇe **sakhīnāṁ krodho bhavet** ||3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.4 ||**

yathā, vidagdha-mādhave (2.37)—

**antaḥ-kleśa-kalaṅkitāḥ kila vayaṁ yāmo’dya yāmyāṁ purīṁ**

**nāyaṁ vañcana-sañcaya-praṇayinaṁ hāsaṁ tathāpy ujjhati |**

**asmin sampuṭite gabhīra-kapaṭair ābhīra-pallī-viṭe**

**hā medhāvini rādhike tava kathaṁ premā garīyān abhūt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : antaḥ-kleśa-kalaṅkitā** ity asya prakaraṇe parīkṣārthaṁ kṛtaudāsīnya-prāyāt śrī-kṛṣṇāt śrī-rādhāyā atyāhitaṁ jātam iti jñeyam ||4||

**mukundaḥ : antaḥ-kleśa** ity asya prakaraṇe parīkṣārthaṁ kṛtaudāsīnyāt śrī-kṛṣṇāt śrī-rādhāyā atyāhitaṁ jātam iti jñeyam ||4||

**viśvanāthaḥ : antaḥ-kleśena kalaṅkitā** ity asya prakaraṇe prema-parīkṣārthaṁ kṛtaudāsīnya-prāyāt śrī-kṛṣṇāt śrī-rādhāyā atyāhitaṁ dṛṣṭvā sakhyaḥ sa-krodham āhuḥ | **vayaṁ yama-puraṁ** **yāmaḥ**, tathāpy **ayaṁ** śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ **vañcanā**-samūha-karaṇa-śīlaṁ **hāsaṁ na tyajati** | **gabhira-kapaṭaiḥ sampuṭite** ācchanne tathā **ābhira-pallīnāṁ** gopa-jāti-strīṇāṁ **viṭe** kāmuke’**smin** śrī-kṛṣṇe he **rādhe** ! **tava premā garīyān katham abhūt** ? ||4||

[**vidagdha-mādhava-ṭīkā**]**: antaḥ-kleśena kalaṅkitāś** cihnitāḥ satyaḥ | mṛtyor anantaram apy ayaṁ kleśaḥ sthyāsyaty eveti bhāvaḥ | **vāñcana**-samūhasya **praṇayinaṁ** karaṇa-śīlaṁ **hāsam** | **tathāpi** iti akāruṇyaṁ vyajyate | anyāsāṁ premā bhavatu, kāmāndhī-kṛta-dhiyāṁ medhāvinyās tava na yujyate iti bhāvaḥ | **gabhira-kapaṭaiḥ sampuṭite** vyāpte **ābhira-pallīnāṁ** vraja-nāgarīṇāṁ **viṭe** kāmuke ||4||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.5-6 ||**

tatra **jaratyāḥ krodhaḥ—**

**krodho jaratyā vadhv-ādi-sambandhe prekṣite harau ||**

yathā—

**are yuvati-taskara prakaṭam eva vadhvāḥ paṭas**

**tavorasi nirīkṣyate bata na neti kiṁ jalpasi |**

**aho vraja-nivāsinaḥ śṛṇuta kiṁ na vikrośanaṁ**

**vrajeśvara-sutena me suta-gṛhe’gnir utthāpitaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **jaratī-prabhṛti-sarveṣām eva vraja-vāsināṁ śrī-kṛṣṇe sāhajika-premā jāgarūka eveti vidyate, tathāpi **vadhv-ādi**-saha śrī-kṛṣṇasya **sambandhe dṛṣṭe** sati iha loke apratiṣṭhā, para-loke adharmo'nayor nirākaraṇodyame bahir hitaiṣiṇāṁ teṣāṁ śrī-kṛṣṇe krodha ity āśayenāha—he **vraja-vāsinaḥ** mama **vikrośanaṁ kiṁ na śṛṇuta** ? ||5-6||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.7 ||**

**govardhanaṁ mahā-mallaṁ vinānyeṣāṁ vrajaukasām |**

**sarveṣām eva govinde ratiḥ prauḍhā virājate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **nanu jaratyāḥ krodhaḥ kṛṣṇe kathaṁ syāt ? aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṁ [bhā.pu. 10.14.32] ity-ādi śrī-bhāgavata-nirṇaya-śata-rītyā vraja-vāsi-jīva-mātrāṇāṁ sarvātikrameṇa sarva-samarpaṇena ca tad-eka-hitānāṁ nāsau svārthaḥ sambhavatīti ? tatrāha—**govardhanam** iti | so’yaṁ candrāvalyāḥ patiṁmanyaḥ kaṁsasya kaścid gopaḥ āgantukatayā kṛta-vraja-vāsa iti kvacit prasiddhiḥ | tasmāt taṁ **vinānyeṣyām** ity-ādi yojyam | tad evam api tasmiṁs tasyā krodhas tan-maṅgalecchayaiva mukhyam udyamam āvahati, na tu raty-abhāvena iti pūrvaṁ darśitam asti, tathā janeṣv aśṛṇvatsv eva tathā krośanaṁ, na tu śṛṇvatsv apīti bhāvaḥ ||7||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **nanu jaratyā rater abhāvāt krodha eva, na krodha-ratiḥ ? tatrāha—**govardhanam** iti | tośalāpara-paryāyaṁ śrī-candrāvalyāḥ patiṁmanyaṁ **vinā** **sarveṣām eva,** aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṁ [bhā.pu. 10.14.32] ity-ādi-pramāṇāt ||7||

**viśvanāthaḥ : govardhanam** iti | so’yaṁ candrāvalyāḥ patiṁ-manyaḥ kaṁsasya kaścid gopaḥ āgantukatayā kṛta-vraja-vāsa iti kvacit prasiddhiḥ | tasmāt taṁ **vinā** ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.8-9 ||**

atha **hitaḥ—**

**hitas tridhānavahitaḥ sāhasī cerṣyur ity api ||**


    tatra (1) **anavahitaḥ—**

**kṛṣṇa-pālana-kartāpi tat-karmābhiniveśataḥ |**

**kvacit tatra pramatto yaḥ prokto’navahito’tra saḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **tatra **kṛṣṇa-pālane**, **kvacit** tat-sambandhi-bhāvāntareṇa vaicittye sati **pramattaḥ**, tat-tat-parama-hāni-karīm api tad-avasthām avadhātum asamartho **yaḥ so’navahitaḥ proktaḥ** ||9||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kvacin** nirbhaya-sthānādau tatra **kṛṣṇa-pālane pramattaḥ** asāvadhānaḥ ||9||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya bhojanādi-sāmagrī-sampādana-karmaṇi **abhiniveśa**-vaśāt **kadācit** kṛṣṇasya rakṣāyāṁ **yaḥ** **pramattaḥ** asāvadhānaḥ bhavet, **sa anavahitaḥ proktaḥ** ||9||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.10 ||**

yathā—

**uttiṣṭha mūḍhe kuru mā vilambaṁ**

**vṛthaiva dhik paṇḍita-māninī tvam |**

**truṭyat-palāśi-dvayam antarā te**

**baddhaḥ suto’sau sakhi bambhramīti ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : paṇḍita-māninī** putra-śikṣā-vijña-māninī | **truṭyad** iti bhūte’pi vartamāna-sāmīpye vartamānavad vā | tad idaṁ prāyas tasmin dine tūpanandādy-ekatara-gṛhe nimantraṇayā sa-putraṁ gatāyās truṭyad-vṛkṣa-garjitād āgatāyāḥ śrī-dāmodara-nikaṭe śrī-vrajeśvarādy-āgamanaṁ vīkṣya gṛha eva praviṣṭāyāḥ śrī-rohiṇyās tac-chabda-kṛta-bhaya-mūrcchāta utthita-prāyāṁ śrī-vrajeśvarīṁ prati vākyam ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : truṭyad**-vṛkṣa-pracaṇḍa-śabdena nandādīnāṁ tat-kṣaṇam eva śīghrāgamanāt tatra nirṇīta-kṛta-sthityāḥ śrī-rohiṇyās tat-karmābhiniviṣṭāṁ śrī-yaśodāṁ prati **utthiṣṭha mūḍhe** iti vākyam | **paṇḍita-māninī** putra-śikṣā-vijña-māninī ||10||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **athātra dadhi-bhāṇḍa-sphoṭanāparādhena śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ baddhvā tasya bhojanārthaṁ punar dadhi-dugdha-navanītādi-sampādanāya vyagra-cittām ata eva śrī-kṛṣṇa-rakṣāyām asāvadhānāṁ śrī-yaśodāṁ prati upanandādīnāṁ striya āhuḥ—**uttiṣṭha** iti | **dhik yat tvaṁ vṛthaiva paṇḍita-māninī** putra-śikṣā-vijña-māninī | **truṭyad** iti | vartamāna-sāmīpye vartamāṇaḥ | tathā truṭitayoḥ yamalārjunayor madhye **tava** **suto baddhaḥ** san **bambhramīti** ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.11-12 ||**

atha (2) **sāhasī—**

**yaḥ prerako bhaya-sthāne sāhasī sa nigadyate ||**

yathā—

**govindaḥ priya-suhṛdāṁ giraiva yātas**

**tālānāṁ vipinam iti sphuṭaṁ niśamya |**

**bhrū-bheda-sthapuṭita-dṛṣṭir āsyam eṣāṁ**

**ḍimbhānāṁ vraja-pati-gehinī dadarśa ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : sthapuṭitaṁ** viṣamīkṛtam | sthapuṭaṁ viṣamam iti trikāṇḍā-śeṣaḥ | viṣamaṁ tu natonnatam iti jñeyam ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : sthapuṭitaṁ** natonnatam ||12||

**viśvanāthaḥ : iti niśamya** śrutvā krodhena **bhrū-bheda-sthapuṭitā dṛṣṭir** yasyāḥ sā yaśodā **bālakānām āsyaṁ** mukhaṁ **dadarśa** | **sthapuṭitaṁ** viṣamīkṛtaṁ, sthapuṭaṁ viṣamam iti trikāṇḍā-śeṣaḥ | viṣamaṁ tu natonnatam iti ||12||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.13-14 ||**

atha (3) **īrṣyuḥ—**

**īrṣyur māna-dhanā proktā prauḍherṣyākrānta-mānasā ||**

yathā—

**durmāna-mantha-mathite kathayāmi kiṁ te**

**dūraṁ prayāhi savidhe tava jājvalīmi |**

**hā dhik priyeṇa cikurāñcita-piñcha-koṭyā**

**nirmañchitāgra-caraṇāpy aruṇānanāsi ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śrī-kṛṣṇa-kartṛka-bahutara-praṇaty-ādibhis tathā māna-tyajanārthaṁ sakhīnām ananta-prārthanābhir api mānasyābhaṅgaṁ dṛṣṭvā śrī-kṛṣṇe gate sati paścāt-tāpena vigata-mānāsmīti, ata eva śrī-kṛṣṇasyānayānārthaṁ lalitāṁ prārthayamānāṁ śrī-rādhāṁ krodhena sā lalitā āha—**durmāna-** iti | he **durmāna-mantha-mathite** ! durmāna eva manthaḥ manthāna-daṇḍaḥ, tena mathite viloḍite ! **tava savidhe** nikaṭe ahaṁ **jājvalīmi** | atas **tvaṁ dūre prayāhi** | cūḍākāreṇa **kuñcita-picchasya koṭyā** agra-bhāgena praṇāma-samaye **nirmañchitāgra-caraṇāni** tvaṁ tadānīṁ krodhena uddhurā āsīḥ | samprati katham asmābhiḥ sa ānetavyaḥ ? tvam eva gatvā ānayeti bhāvaḥ ||14||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.15-17 ||**

atha **ahitaḥ—**

**ahitaḥ syād dvidhā svasya hareś ceti prabhedataḥ ||**

tatra (1) **svasyāhitaḥ—**

**ahitaḥ svasya sa syād yaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandha-bādhakaḥ ||**

yathā uddhava-sandeśe (74)—

**kṛṣṇaṁ muṣṇan akaruṇa-balād gopa-nārī-vadhārthī**

**mā maryādām yadu-kula-bhuvām bhindhi re gāndineya |**

**ity uttuṅgā mama madhu-pure yātrayā tatra tāsāṁ**

**vitrastānāṁ parivavalire vallavīnāṁ vilāpāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he **gāṇḍineya** akrūra ! tvayi yātrāṁ vidhitsau sati strīṇām asmākaṁ prāṇair api yātrā vyadhāyi, asmākaṁ prāṇā yāsyantīty arthaḥ | tathā ca śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ gṛhītvā tava gamanecchāyāṁ satyām ananta-strī-vadha-janya-pāpena **yadu-kulasya** apratiṣṭhā bhaviṣyaty ato **yadu-kula-bhuvāṁ maryādāṁ** tvaṁ **mā bhindhi re** ||17||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.18-19 ||**

atha (2) **harer ahitaḥ—**

**ahitas tu hares tasya vairi-pakṣo nigadyate ||**

yathā—

**harau śruti-śiraḥ-śikhā-maṇi-marīci-nīrājita-**

**sphurac-caraṇa-paṅkaje’py avamatiṁ vyanakty atra yaḥ |**

**ayaṁ kṣipati pāṇḍavaḥ śamana-daṇḍa-ghoraṁ haṭhāt**

**trir asya mukuṭopari sphuṭam udīrya savyaṁ padam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : śruti-śirasām** upaniṣadāṁ **śikhā**-stha-**maṇi**-dīdhitibhir **nīrājitaṁ** **caraṇa-paṅkajaṁ **yasya, tasmin śrī-kṛṣṇe **yaḥ** śiśupālābhidhaḥ **avajñāṁ vyanakti**, asya **mukuṭopari** bhīma-nāmāyaṁ mal-lakṣaṇo yama-daṇḍād api bhayaṅkaraṁ madīyaṁ vāma-pādam **udīrya** **kṣipati** ||19||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.20-26 ||**

**solluṇṭha-hāsa-vakrokti-kaṭākṣānādarādayaḥ |**

**kṛṣṇāhita-hitasthāḥ syur amī uddīpanā iha ||**

**hasta-nispeṣaṇaṁ danta-ghaṭṭanaṁ rakta-netratā |**

**daṣṭauṣṭhatātibhrū-kuṭī bhujāsphālana-tāḍanāḥ ||**

**tuṣṇīkatā natāsyatvaṁ niśvāso bhugna-dṛṣṭitā |**

**bhartsanaṁ mūrdha-vidhūtir dṛg-ante pāṭala-cchaviḥ ||**

**bhrū-bhedādhara-kampādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ |**

**atra stambhādayaḥ sarve prākaṭyaṁ yānti sāttvikāḥ ||**

**āvego jaḍatā garvo nirvedo moha-cāpale |**

**asūyaugryaṁ tathāmarṣa-śramādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**atra krodha-ratiḥ sthāyī sa tu krodhas tridhā mataḥ |**

**kopo manyus tathā roṣas tatra kopas tu śatru-gaḥ ||**

**manyur bandhuṣu te pūjya-sama-nyūnās tridhoditāḥ |**

**roṣas tu dayite strīṇām ato vyabhicaraty asau ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : vyabhicarati** ādye rase vyabhicāritāṁ prāpnoti | jaratī-sakhyādīnāṁ kopa-manyuvan nāmūṣāṁ roṣaḥ sthāyitām āyātīty arthaḥ | tad evaṁ pūrvam uktā **āvegādayaś** ca vyabhicāriṇaḥ **augrya**-pradhānāḥ śatru-viṣayāḥ, **amarṣa**-pradhānā bandhu-viṣayāḥ | **asūyā**-pradhānā dayita-viṣayā jñeyāḥ ||26||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **te bandhavaḥ pūjyādi-tridhā bhavanti | vyabhicarati śṛṅgāra-rase vyabhicāritāṁ prāpnoti | jaratī-sakhyādīnāṁ kopo manyuvan nāmūṣāṁ roṣaḥ sthāyitām āyātīty arthaḥ | tad evaṁ pūrvam uktā āvegādayaś ca vyabhicāriṇaḥ, augrya-pradhānāḥ manyu-viṣayāḥ, amarṣa-pradhānā bandhu-viṣayāḥ | asūyā-pradhānā dayita-viṣayā jñeyāḥ ||26||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.27-28 ||**

**hasta-peṣādayaḥ kope manyau tuṣṇīkatādayaḥ |**

**dṛg-anta-pāṭalatvādyā roṣe tu kathitāḥ kriyāḥ ||**

tatra **vairiṇi**, yathā—

**nirudhya puram unmade harim agādha-sattva-śriyaṁ**

**mṛdhe magadha-bhūpatau kim api vaktram ākrośati |**

**dṛśaṁ kavalita-dviṣad-visara-jāṅgale lāṅgale**

**nunoda dahad-iṅgala-pravala-piṅgalāṁ lāṅgalī ||**[^6]

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : dviṣad-visara-jāṅgalaṁ** śatru-samūha-māṁsam | **iṅgalo**’ṅgāraḥ ||28||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **madhu-**purīṁ** **nirudhya** **agādhā sattva-śrīḥ** sampattiḥ yasya tathā-bhūtaṁ **hariṁ** **magadha-bhūpatau** jarāsandhe **vaktram ākrośati** sati, **lāṅgalī** baladevaḥ krodhena **dṛśaṁ** **lāṅgale** hale **nunoda** prerayāmāsa | tathā ca, yuddhe lāṅgalaṁ dadarśa ity arthaḥ | lāṅgale kathaṁ-bhūte ? **kavalitaṁ dviṣad-visarasya** śatru-samūhasya **jāṅgalaṁ** māṁsaṁ yena tathā-bhūte | dṛśaṁ kathaṁ-bhūtāṁ ? **jvalad-iṅgalasya** jvalad-aṅgārasyeva **piṅgala**-varṇām ||28||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.29 ||**

**pūjyo**, yathā vidagdha-mādhave (2.21)—

**krośantyāṁ kara-pallavena balavān sadyaḥ pidhatte mukhaṁ**

**dhāvantyāṁ bhaya-bhāji vistṛta-bhujo rundhe puraḥ paddhatim |**

**pādānte viluṭhaty asau mayi muhur daṣṭādharāyāṁ ruṣā **

**mātaś caṇḍi mayā śikhaṇḍa-mukuṭād ātmābhirakṣyaḥ katham ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ**,** mukundadāsaḥ : krośantyām** iti bhāvaṁ parīkṣamāṇāyāṁ paurṇamāsyāṁ kṛṣṇa-sphūrti-mayaṁ caritaṁ sākṣād rūpam iva śrī-rādhayā kathitam ||29||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **prema-parīkṣārthaṁ śrī-rādhikāyai pātivratya-dharmam upadiśantīṁ paurṇamāsīṁ prati sā rādhāha—mayi **krośantyām** satyāṁ **mukhaṁ pidhatte** | **paddhatiṁ** panthānaṁ | **ruṣā** dantena **daṣṭādharāyāṁ** satyāṁ **pādānte viluṭhati** | he **caṇḍi** ! kopane ! śrī-kṛṣṇāt **ātmā** dehaḥ **kathaṁ rakṣyaḥ** ? ||29|| [tathāpi avicāreṇa māṁ praty eva kupyasi kiṁ vaktavyam ? iti |]

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.30 ||**

**same, **yathā—

**jvalati durmukhi marmaṇi murmuras **

**tava girā jaṭile niṭile ca me |**

**giridharaḥ spṛśati sma kadā madād**

**duhitaraṁ duhitur mama pāmari ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : jvalati** iti jaṭilā-mukharayor nibhṛta-kalahaḥ | **murmuras** tuṣāgniḥ | **niṭile** śirasi ||30||

**mukundaḥ : murmuras** tuṣāgniḥ | **niṭile** śirasi ||30||

 

**viśvanāthaḥ : **jaṭilā-mukharayor nibhṛta-kalaham āha—he **durmukhi jaṭile** ! **tava girā** kaṭu-vacanena **mama marmaṇi niṭile** śirasi ca **murmuras** tuṣāgnir jvalati | he **pāmari** ! mama **duhituḥ** kīrtidāyāḥ **duhitaraṁ** rādhikāṁ **giridharaḥ** kadā spṛśati sma ? ||30||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.31 ||**

**nyūne**, yathā—

**hanta svakīya-kuca-mūrdhni manoharo’yaṁ**

**hāraś cakāsti hari-kaṇṭha-taṭī-cariṣṇuḥ |**

**bhoḥ paśyata svakula-kajjala-mañjarīyaṁ**

**kuṭena māṁ tad api vañcayate vadhūṭī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **kadācin nijāṅgāj jhaṭiti śrī-rādhikayāvatāritaṁ hari-hāraṁ vīkṣya tasyāḥ sakhīḥ prati jaṭilā vacanam—**hanta** iti ||31||

**mukundaḥ : **rādhā-vakṣasi hari-hāra-vīkṣaṇena jāta-manyor jaṭilāyās tat-sakhīr anādṛtya śūnye vacanam—**hanta** iti ||31||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kadācin nijāṅgāj jhaṭiti śrī-rādhayāvatāritaṁ hari-hāraṁ vīkṣya tasyāḥ sakhīṁ prati jaṭilāha—**hanta** iti ||31||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.5.32-33 ||**

**asmin na tādṛśo manyau vartate raty-anugrahaḥ |**

**udāharaṇa-mātrāya tathāpy eṣa nidarśitaḥ ||**

**krodhāśrayāṇāṁ śatrūṇāṁ caidyādīnāṁ svabhāvataḥ |**

**krodho rati-vinābhāvān na bhakti-rasatāṁ vrajet ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : na tādṛśa** iti na spaṣṭa ity arthaḥ | govardhanaṁ vinā mallam [4.5.7] ity-ādy-uktatvāt ||32||

**mukundaḥ : tādṛśo** rasa-yogyaḥ | **manyur** ayam amarṣākhyo vyabhicāri-bhāva eva sthāyīti bhāvaḥ ||32||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **na tādṛśa iti na spaṣṭa ity arthaḥ | govardhanaṁ vinā mallam ity ādy uktatvāt ||32||

 —o)0(o—

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

raudra-bhakti-rasa-laharī pañcamī 

|| 4.5 ||

 —o)0(o—

(4.6)


### bhayānaka-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### ṣaṣṭha-laharī

**|| 4.6.1-3 ||**

**vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṁ bhaya-ratir gatā |**

**bhayānakābhidho bhakti-raso dhīrair udīryate ||**

**kṛṣṇaś ca dāruṇāś ceti tasminn ālambanā dvidhā |**

**anukampyeṣu sāgaḥsu kṛṣṇas tasya ca bandhuṣu ||2||**

**dāruṇāḥ snehataḥ śaśvat tad-aniṣṭāpti-darśiṣu |**

**darśanāc chravaṇāc ceti smaraṇāc ca prakīrtitāḥ ||3||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **tad-bhaktāś ceti vaktavye **dāruṇāś** cety uktiḥ prakṛta-rasavin-matānusāreṇa | sva-matānusāreṇa tu pañcamy-arthānāṁ teṣām ālambanatvaṁ na sambhavati | sāmānye viśeṣeṣu ca saptamy-arthasyaivālambanatvena svīkṛtatvāt | prākṛta-rasavin-matānuvāda-mayam etat prakaraṇam iti svayaṁ likhiṣyate—


    hāsyādīnāṁ rasatvaṁ yad gauṇatvenāpi kīrtitam |


    prācāṁ matānusāreṇa tad vijñeyaṁ manīṣibhiḥ || [bha.ra.si. 4.7.13] iti |

sva-mate tu prathama-pakṣe’**nukampyā** eva bhayasya viṣayatvenāśrayatvena **cālambanāḥ** | **kṛṣṇas** tu hetu-mātram | tad-dvitīyā-pakṣe kṛṣṇo viṣayatvena, **bandhava** āśrayatvenālambanāḥ, **dāruṇās** tu hetu-mātram iti jñeyam | ratis tu yathāyatham asty eva ||2||

**mukundadāsaḥ : dāruṇāś** cety uktir bharatādīnāṁ matānusāreṇa | śrī-bhāgavatādy-anusāri-sva-mate hāsyādīnāṁ prāyo vyabhicāritvam | pañcamy-anta ālambano bhāvotpādanāṁśe ubhaya-sammata eva | saptamy-anto bhāvotkarṣa-śaṁsaka eva tasya svotpādita-bhāvotkarṣaka-svarūpatvāt | ato vakṣyate—bhīṣaṇebhyo bhayam [bha.ra.si. 4.6.12] vibhāvyate hi raty-ādir yatrety atra siddhavan nirdeśā, yato jñāna iti ca bodhyam ||2||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **asmin rase śrī-**kṛṣṇaḥ** tathā **dāruṇāḥ** asurādayaś ca **dvidhā viṣayālambanā** jñeyāḥ | **sāgaḥsu** sāparādheṣu **anukampyeṣu** āśrayālambaneṣu śrī-kṛṣṇo viṣayālambanaḥ, tasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya **bandhuṣu** snehāt sarvadā śrī-kṛṣṇasya **aniṣṭāpti-darśiṣu** teṣu āśrayālambaneṣu **dāruṇā darśanādi-**hetoḥ viṣayālambanāḥ kīrtitāḥ ||2-3|| 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.4 ||**

tatra **anukampyeṣu kṛṣṇo**, yathā—

**kiṁ śuṣyad-vadano’pi muñca khacitaṁ citte pṛthuṁ vepathuṁ**

**viśvasya prakṛtiṁ bhajasva na manāg apy asti mantuṁ tava | \
uṣma-mrakṣitam ṛkṣa-rāja rabhasād vistīrya vīryaṁ tvayā **

**pṛthvī pratyuta yuddha-kautuka-mayī sevaiva me nirmitā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : uṣmā** krodha-santāpaḥ | **pṛthvī** pṛthutarā ||4||

**mukundadāsaḥ : uṣmā** krodha-santāpaḥ ||4||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **jāmbavantaṁ prati śrī-kṛṣṇa āha—he **ṛkṣa-rāja** ! **khacitaṁ** vyāptaṁ, **vepathuṁ** muñca | tava **manāg apy** aparādho **nāsti** | **uṣmā** krodha-santāpaḥ, tena **mrakṣitaṁ** yuktaṁ **vīryaṁ** **vistārya** **pṛthvī** mahatī **mama yuddha-kautuka-mayī sevaiva tvayā nirmitā** ||4||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.5 ||**

yathā vā—

**mura-mathana puras te ko bhujaṅgas tapasvī **

**laghu-haram iti kārṣīr mā sma dīnāya manyum |**

**gurur ayam aparādhas tathyam ajñānato’bhūd**

**aśaraṇam atimūḍhaṁ rakṣa rakṣa prasīda ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **kāliyasya vākyam | **tapasvī** varākaḥ | **manyuḥ** krodhaḥ ||5||

**mukundadāsaḥ : tapasvī** varākaḥ ||5||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **bhagavat-tattva-jñānānantaraṁ śaraṇāpannaḥ kāliyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇam āha—**tava puro**’gre mad-vidho **bhujaṅgaḥ tapasvī** varākaḥ kaḥ ? **manyuṁ mā sma kārṣīḥ** ||5||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.6 ||**

**bandhuṣu dāruṇa-darśanād**, yathā—

**hā kiṁ karomi taralaṁ bhavanāntarāle**

**gopendra gopaya balād uparudhya bālam |**

**kṣmā-maṇḍalena saha cañcalayan mano me**

**śṛṅgāṇi laṅghayati paśya turaṅga-daityaḥ ||6||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : śṛṅgāṇi** vṛkṣādīnām agra-bhāgān ||6||

**mukundadāsaḥ : śṛṅgāṇi** parvatoccāgra-bhāgān ||6||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **nandaṁ prati śrī-yaśodāha—**hā kim** iti | he **gopendra** ! **taralaṁ** cañcalaṁ bālaṁ **bhavana-madhye balāt uparudhya** | **gopaya** rakṣa | **turaṅga-daityaḥ** keśī **laṅghayati** ||6||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.7 ||**

**śravaṇād**, yathā—

**śṛṇvantī turaṅga-dānavaṁ ruṣā**

**gokulaṁ kila viśantam uddhuram |**

**drāg abhūt tanaya-rakṣaṇākulā**

**śuṣyad-āsya-jalajā vrajeśvarī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : turaṅga-dānavaṁ** keśinaṁ **gokulaṁ viśantaṁ śṛṇvatī** yaśodā **śuṣyan-mukha-pañkajā** satī **putra-rakṣaṇā**rthaṁ **vyākulā** **abhūt** ||7||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.8 ||**

**smaraṇād,** yathā—

**virama virama mātaḥ pūtanāyāḥ prasaṅgāt**

**tanum iyam adhunāpi smaryamāṇā dhunoti | \
kavalayitum ivāndhīkṛtya bālaṁ ghurantī**

**vapur atiparuṣaṁ yā ghoram āviścakāra ||8||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : virama** iti kāñcid dūrād āgatām ajñāta-vṛttāṁ prati śrī-vrajeśvarī-vākyam | tataḥ **kavalayitum** ity-ādy anuvāda-doṣo’pi na syāt | **ghurantī** bhīma-śabdaṁ kurvantī | ghura bhīmārta-śabdayor ity asya rūpam ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : virama** iti kāñcid dūrāgatāṁ kiñcin-mātra-śruta-vṛttāṁ prati śrī-vrajeśvarī-vākyam | **ghurantī** bhīma-śabdaṁ kurvantī ||8||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kāñcid dūrād āgatām ajñāta-vṛttāntāṁ prati śrī-vrajeśvarī āha—ataḥ **kavalayitum** ity-ādy-anuvāda-doṣo na syāt | **dhunoti** kampayate | **ghurantī** bhīma-śabdaṁ kurvantī | ghura bhīmārta-śabdayoḥ ||8||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.9-10 ||**

**vibhāvasya bhrukuṭy-ādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ |**

**mukha-śoṣaṇam ucchvāsaḥ parāvṛtya vilokanam ||**

**sva-saṅgopanam udghūrṇā śaraṇānveṣaṇaṁ tathā |**

**krośanādyāḥ kriyāś cātra sāttvikāś cāśru-varjitāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : vibhāvasya** viṣayālambanasya **bhrukuṭy-ādyāḥ** ||9|| **kriyā** anubhāvāḥ ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.11-13 || **

**iha santrāsa-maraṇa-cāpalāvega-dīnatāḥ |**

**viṣāda-mohāpasmāra-śaṅkādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**asmin bhaya-ratiḥ sthāyī bhāvaḥ syād aparādhataḥ |**

**bhīṣaṇebhyaś ca tatra syād bahudhaivāparādhitā ||**

**taj-jā bhīr nāparatra syād anugrāhya-janān vinā |**

**ākṛtyā ye prakṛtyā ye ye prabhāveṇa bhīṣaṇāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : tajjā** aparādhajāḥ ||13||
