**viśvanāthaḥ : bhīṣaṇebhyo** bhayānakāsurebhyaḥ **aparādhitā** aparādho bahuvidho bhavati ||12|| **tasmāt** aparādhāt **jātā bhīḥ** **anugrāhya**-bhaktān **vinā** **anyatra na syāt** ||13||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.6.14-16 || **

**etad-ālambanā bhītiḥ kevala-prema-śāliṣu |**

**nārī-bālādiṣu tathā prāyeṇātropajāyate ||**

**ākṛtyā pūtanādyāḥ syuḥ prakṛtyā duṣṭa-bhū-bhujaḥ |**

**bhīṣaṇās tu prabhāveṇa surendra-giriśādayaḥ ||**

**sadā bhagavato bhītiṁ gatā ātyantikīm api |**

**kaṁsādyā rati-śūnyatvād atra nālambanā matāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : duṣṭa-bhūbhujaḥ** śiśupālādayaḥ ||15||

**mukundadāsaḥ : prākṛtyā** svabhāvena keśi-mukhyo yeṣu ariṣṭādiṣu te keśi-mukhyakāḥ ||15||

**viśvanāthaḥ : etad-ālambanā** etad-viṣayālambanā **bhītiḥ** premavatsu **strī-bālakādiṣūpajāyate** ||14|| **duṣṭa-bhūbhujaḥ** śiśupālādayaḥ | bhagavat-sakāśāt kaṁsādyā **ātyantikīṁ** bhītiṁ prāptā api **rati-śūnyatvāt** viṣayālambanatve’pi nāśrayālambanāḥ | bhaktān vinānyeṣām āśrayālambanatvaṁ pūrvam eva dūrīkṛtam iti jñeyam ||15-16||

 —o)0(o—

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

bhayānaka-bhakti-rasa-laharī ṣaṣṭhī 

|| 4.6||

(4.7)


### bībhatsa-bhakti-rasākhyā 


#### saptama-laharī

**|| 4.7.1-2 ||**

**puṣṭiṁ nija-vibhāvādyair jugupsā-ratir āgatā |**

**asau bhakti-raso dhīrair bībhatsākhya itīryate ||**

**asminn āśrita-śāntādyā dhīrair ālambanā matāḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **tatra bībhatsitasya eva ālambanatve’py **āśrita-śāntādīnām ālambanatvaṁ** raty-aṁśena | śānto’tra tapasvi-rūpa eva | **ādya**-grahaṇāt aprāpta-bhagavat-sānnidhyāḥ sarva eva ||2|| 

**mukundadāsaḥ : asminn** iti | **ālambanā** viṣayālambana-rūpāḥ | **ādya**-śabdāt prāyikīī jugupsāśrayā anye’pi bhaktā āśrayatvena dehādikaṁ viṣayatvena gṛhītāni ||2|| 

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ātmocitair **vibhāvādyaiḥ** **puṣṭiṁ** prāptāsau **jugupsā ratiḥ** **bībhatsākhyaḥ** bhakti-raso bhavet ||1|| **asmin** rase **āśrita-śāntādayaḥ** **ālambanā matāḥ** ||2|| 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.3 ||**

yathā—

**pāṇḍityaṁ rata-hiṇḍakādhvani gato yaḥ kāma-dīkṣā-vratī**

**kurvan pūrvam aśeṣa-ṣiḍga-nagarī sāmrājya-caryām abhūt |**

**citraṁ so’yam udīrayan hari-guṇānudbāṣpa-dṛṣṭir jano**

**dṛṣṭe strī-vadane vikūṇita-mukho viṣṭabhya niṣṭhīvati ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : ratahiṇḍako** rata-cauraḥ | **vikūṇita-mukho** vakrita-vadanaḥ | **viṣṭabhya** viśeṣeṇa stabdho bhūtvā ||3||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vikūnita-mukho** viśeṣeṇa saṅkocita-mukhaḥ | **viṣṭabhya** viśeṣeṇa stabdhī-bhūya ||3||

**viśvanāthaḥ : rata-hiṇḍako** rati-cauraḥ | tasya **adhvani** yaḥ **pāṇḍityaṁ** prāpuḥ, tathā aśeṣa-**ṣiḍgāṇāṁ** strī-lampaṭānāṁ yā **nagarī** tasyā **sāmrājya-caryāṁ** yatheṣṭācaraṇaṁ kurvan san pūrvaṁ **kāma-dīkṣā-vratī** abhūt, sa evāyaṁ **hari-guṇān udīrayan** saṅkīrtayan **ud**gata-**bāṣpa**-dhārā-yuktā **dṛṣṭir** yasya tathā-bhūtaḥ san **strī-vadane dṛṣṭe** sati **vikūṇita-mukho** vakrita-vadanaḥ | **viṣṭabhya** viśeṣeṇa **stabdho** bhūtvā **niṣṭhīvati** ||3||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.4-6 ||**

**atra niṣṭhīvanaṁ vaktra-kūṇanaṁ ghrāṇa-saṁvṛtiḥ |**

**dhāvanaṁ kampa-pulaka-prasvedādyāś ca vikriyāḥ ||**

**iha glāni-śramonmāda-moha-nirveda-dīnatāḥ |**

**viṣāda-cāpalāvega-jāḍyādyo vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**jugupsā-ratir atra syāt sthāyī sā ca vivekajā |**

**prāyikī ceti kathitā jugupsā dvi-vidhā budhaiḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : vikriyā** anubhāvāḥ ||4|| \


 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.7-8 ||**

tatra **vivekajā—**

**jāta-kṛṣṇa-rater bhakta-viśeṣasya tu kasyacit |**

**vivekotthā tu dehādau jugupsā syād vivekajā ||**

yathā—

**ghana-rudhira-maye tvacā pinaddhe**

**piśita-vimiśrita-visra-gandha-bhāji |**

**katham iha ramatāṁ budhaḥ śarīre**

**bhagavati hanta rater lave’py udīrṇe ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : piśitaṁ** māṁsam | **visraṁ** syād āma-gandhi yat | tasmād visrasya yo **gandhas** tad-**bhājī** ity arthaḥ | **udīrṇa** iti kry-ādikasya, ṛ gatāv ity asya dīrghasya niṣṭhāyā rūpam | **udita** ity arthaḥ ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kasyacid bhakta-viśeṣasya** sevā-niṣṭhāṁ vinā āśrita-sārūpyasya ||7|| **piśitaṁ** māṁsam | **visraṁ** syād āma-gandhi yat | **āmaḥ** apakva-malaḥ | piśita-miśritasya visrasya yo **gandhas** tad-**bhājī** | **udīrṇa** iti kriyādikasya ṛ gatāv ity asya dīrghasya niṣṭhāntaṁ rūpam | **udita** ity arthaḥ ||8||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śarīre kiṁ-bhūte ? **tvacā pinaddhe** carmaṇācchādite **piśitaṁ** māṁsaṁ **visrasya** yo **gandhaḥ,** tad-**bhājī** ity arthaḥ | **visraṁ** syād āma-gandhi yat ity amaraḥ | **rater lave’py udīrṇe** udite satīty arthaḥ ||8|| 

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.9-10 ||**

atha **prāyikī—**

**amedhya-pūty-anubhavāt sarveṣām eva sarvataḥ |**

**yā prāyo jāyate seyaṁ jugupsā prāyikī matā ||**

yathā—

**asṛṅ-mūtrākīrṇe ghana-śamala-paṅka-vyatikare**

**vasann eṣa klinno jaḍa-tanur ahaṁ mātur udare |**

**labhe cetaḥ-kṣobhaṁ tava bhajana-karmākṣamatayā **

**tad asmin kaṁsāre kuru mayi kṛpā-sāgara kṛpām ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bhajana-karmākṣamatayā** upalakṣite **mayi**, na tu tayā hetunā | "bhajana-karmākṣamatame" iti saptamy-anto vā pāṭhaḥ ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : sarveṣāṁ** pañca-vidha-bhaktānām ||9|| **bhajana-karmākṣamatayā** hetuneti jāta-ratitvaṁ jīvasya darśitam ||10|| 

**viśvanāthaḥ : **garbhastha-bhakta-jīvo bhagavantaṁ stauti | **ghana-śamala-paṅkānāṁ** niviḍa-pāpa-rūpa-paṅkānāṁ **vyatikaraḥ** paunaḥpunyaṁ yatra tathā-bhūte **mātur udare vasann** **eṣa jaḍa-tanur aham cetaḥ-kṣobhaṁ labhe** | **bhajana-karmākṣamatayā** upalakṣite **mayi** ||10||

 —o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.11 ||**

yathā vā—

**ghrāṇodghūrṇaka-pūta-gandhi-vikaṭe kīṭākule dehalī-**

**srasta-vyādhita-yūtha-gūtha-ghaṭanā-nirdhūta-netrāyuṣi |**

**kārā-nāmani hanta māgadha-yamenāmī vayaṁ nārake**

**kṣiptās te smṛtim ākalayya naraka-dhvaṁsinn iha prāṇimaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : nārake** naraka-samūhe ||11||

**viśvanāthaḥ : ghrāṇasya udghūrṇā**-janako yo durgandhaḥ, tena **vikaṭe** evaṁ **dehalyāṁ** **srastā** ye **vyādhi**-yuktā manuṣya-**yūthāḥ,** teṣāṁ **gūthānāṁ** viṣṭhānāṁ **ghaṭanayā** **nirdhūtāni** **netrāṇām** **āyūṁṣi** darśana-sāmārthyāni yasya, tathā-bhūte **kārāgāra-nāmani** **nārake** naraka-samūhe jarāsandha-svarūpeṇa **yamena** **kṣiptā** vayaṁ tava caraṇāravindasya **smṛtim ākalayya** prāpya, he **naraka-dhvamṣin** ! **prāṇimaḥ** jīvāmaḥ ||11||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.7.12-14 ||**

**labdha-kṛṣṇa-rater eva suṣṭhu pūtaṁ manaḥ sadā |**

**kṣubhyaty ahṛdya-leśe’pi tato’syāṁ raty-anugrahaḥ ||**

**hāsyādīnāṁ rasatvaṁ yad gauṇatvenāpi kīrtitam |**

**prācāṁ matānusāreṇa tad vijñeyaṁ manīṣibhiḥ ||**

**amī pañcaiva śāntādyā harer bhakti-rasā matāḥ |**

**eṣu hāsyādayaḥ prāyo bibhrati vyabhicāritām || \
**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : raty-anugrahaḥ** ratyā kartryā poṣaṇam ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : prācāṁ** śrī-bharatānusāri-matānām ||13||

**viśvanāthaḥ : labdha-kṛṣṇa-rater** hetoḥ **suṣṭhu pūtaṁ** nirmalaṁ **manaḥ kṣubhyati** | ata **asyāṁ** jugupsā-ratau **raty-anugrahaḥ** mukhya-ratyā kartryā poṣaṇam ity arthaḥ | sva-mate tu amī śāntādyāḥ pañcaiva bhakti-rasā matāḥ ||12-14||

 —o)0(o—

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe 

bībhatsa-bhakti-rasa-laharī saptamī 

|| 4.7 ||

(4.8)


### rasānāṁ maitrī-vaira-sthiti-nāmnī 


#### aṣṭama-laharī

**|| 4.8.1-2 ||**

**athāmīṣāṁ krameṇaiva śāntādīnāṁ parasparam |**

**mitratvaṁ śātravatvaṁ ca rasānām abhidhīyate ||**

**śāntasya prīta-bībhatsa-dharma-vīrāḥ suhṛd-varāḥ |**

**adbhutaś caiṣa vijñeyaḥ prītādiṣu catuḥṣv api ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **atra svayam aṅgi-rasānubhavī, śrī-kṛṣṇa-bhaktaḥ, śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ, tad-bhaktāntaraṁ, tad-udāsīnaḥ, tad-virodhī ceti pañca-vidha-gatatvena bhāvā lakṣyante | tatrāṅgino rasasya kenacid anucitenāṅgena milane sati rasa-vighātaḥ syāt, ucita-milane tu tat-poṣa iti vaktavye śāntasya tau darśayituṁ tāvad āha—**śāntasya** iti | 

**bībhatsa-dharma-vīrāv** atra tapasvi-śāntasya suhṛdau jñeyau, tad-udāsīna-tad-virodhinor bībhatsitatā-bhāvanayā śrī-kṛṣṇa-tad-bhaktayor dhārmikatā-paryālocanayā ca tadīya-rasodayāt | ātmārāma-śāntasya ca tat-tad-anavadhāne’pi suhṛd-varo jñeyaḥ | kintu śāntasya śānta-prāya-tapasvino’pi dvidhā śrī-bhagavati camatkāro jāyate—bhāvānubhavānandād api tan-mādhuryānubhavānandena, kvacic śatru-pakṣa-nigrahādi-līlāyā apy āścaryatvena | yathā tasyāravinda-nayanasya [bhā.pu. 3.15.43] ity-ādi | yathā ca, na tasya citraṁ para-pakṣa-nigrahas tathāpi martyānuvidhasya varṇyate [bhā.pu. 10.50.30] ity-ādi | martyān anuvidhatte’nukaroti martya-līlocitām eva śaktiṁ vyañjayati nādhikāṁ, tathāpi tan-nigrahādikaṁ karoty eva yat tasyety arthaḥ ||2||

**mukundadāsaḥ : eṣa ca śāntasya suhṛd-varaḥ** | **eṣo’dbhutaḥ** **prītādiṣv api suhṛd-varo jñeyaḥ** ||1-2||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atrāṅgino rasasya kenacid anucitenāṅgena milane rasa-vighātaḥ syāt, tad-ucita-milane tu tat-poṣa iti vaktavye śāntasya tau darśayituṁ tāvad āha—**śāntasya** iti | **bībhatsa-dharma-vīrāv** atra tapasvi-śāntasya **suhṛdau** **jñeyau** | tad-udāsīna-tad-virodhinor bībhatsatā-bhāvanayā śrī-kṛṣṇa-tad-bhaktayor dhārmikatā-paryālocanayā ca tadīya-rasodayāt | ātmārāma-śāntasya ca tat-tad-anavadhāne’pi kavinā tad-aṅgatvena varṇanāyāṁ doṣa eva syāt | **adbhutaś ca śāntasya **suhṛd-varaḥ | **eṣa adbhutaḥ** dāsya-sakhya-vātsalya-śṛṅgāreṣv api **suhṛd-varo jñeyaḥ** | kintu śāntasya śānta-prāya-tapasvinaś ca dvidhā śrī-bhagavataś camatkāro jāyate | bhāvānubhavānandād api tan-mādhuryānubhavānandena kvacic śatru-pakṣa-nigrahādi-līlāyā apy āścaryatvena | yathā tṛtīye, tasyāravinda-nayanasya padāravinda- [bhā.pu. 3.15.43] ity-ādi | yathā śrī-daśame, na tasya citraṁ para-pakṣa-nigrahas tathāpi martyānuvidhasya varṇyate [bhā.pu. 10.52.29] ity-ādi | martyān anuvidhatte’nukaroti martya-līlocitām eva śaktiṁ vyañjayati, nādhikāṁ, tathāpi yas tu nigrahādikaṁ karoti tasyety arthaḥ ||2||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.3 ||**

**dviṣann asya śucir yuddha-vīro raudro bhayānakaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : asya** śāntasya dvividhasyāpi | **śucir** atra samprati ṭīkokta-pañca-vidhāṁ gato’pi **dviṣan**, tathā **yuddha-vīraś** ca | **raudra-bhayānakau** tu ātmārāmasyaiva śatrū | tapasvi-śāntasya tu yamādīnām augrya-darśanān nija-saṁsāra-bhayotpattau śānti-puṣṭeḥ, tasya tu raudraḥ svagato dveṣyaḥ ||3||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : asya** śāntasya dvividhasyāpi | **śuciḥ** śṛṅgāraḥ **dviṣan** śatrur ity arthaḥ | tathā **yuddha-vīraś** ca | **raudra-bhayānakau** tu ātmārāma-śāntasyaiva śatrū | tapasvi-śāntasya tu yamādīnām augrya-darśanān nija-saṁsāra-bhayotpattau śānti-rasasya puṣṭeḥ | asya tu raudraḥ svagato dveṣyaḥ ||3||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.4 ||**

**suhṛt-prītasya bībhatsaḥ śānto vīra-dvayaṁ tathā |**

**vairī śucir yuddha-vīro raudraś caika-vibhāvakaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : suhṛt-prītasya bībhatsaḥ** ity udāsīnādi-dvaye bībhatsatayā tasyaiva puṣyamāṇatvāt, evaṁ tata uparatyā **śānto**’pi tathā | prathama-tritaya-gataṁ **vīra-dvayaṁ** dharma-dāna-vīrākhyaṁ **yuddha-vīro raudraś ca**, **eka-vibhāvakaḥ**, kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ sākṣāt kṛṣṇa-sambandhād utpannaḥ | sa ca sa cātra kṛṣṇena saha sva-kartṛka-yuddha-mayaḥ, kṛṣṇaṁ prati sva-kopa-maya ity arthaḥ | tad etad upalakṣaṇatvenānyatrānuktam api yathāyathaṁ tat-tad-gatatvena vyākhyāsyate ||4||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vīra-dvayaṁ** dharma-dāna-vīrākhyam | **eka-vibhāvakaḥ** kṛṣṇa-bhakta-kartṛkaḥ krodha ity arthaḥ ||4||

**viśvanāthaḥ : suhṛt-prītasya bībhatsaḥ** ity udāsīnādi-vaira-dvaye bībhatsatayā jñāte dāsyasyaiva puṣyamāṇatvāt | evaṁ tābhyām uparatyā **śānto**’pi suhṛt | tathā **vīra-dvayaṁ** dharma-vīra-dāna-vīrākhyaṁ | **yuddha-vīro raudraś** ca **eka-vibhāvakaḥ** śrī-kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ sākṣāt śrī-kṛṣṇa-sambandhād utpanno yuddha-vīraḥ śrī-kṛṣṇena saha sva-kartṛka-yuddha-mayaḥ | sākṣāt śrī-kṛṣṇa-sambandhād utpanno raudraś ca śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ prati kopa-mayaḥ | ubhayam api dāsye viruddham | anyatrāpy anukramam apy evaṁ-rītyā jñeyam ||4||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.5 ||**

**preyasas tu śucir hāsyo yuddha-vīraḥ suhṛd-varāḥ |**

**dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-raudrā bhīṣmaś ca pūrvavat ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : preyasas** tv iti | **śucir** atra kṛṣṇa-gataḥ | **hāsyas** tad-bhakta-dvaya-gataś ca | **yuddha-vīras** tūdāsīnād anyatra gataḥ | pūrvavat kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ, sa cātra kṛṣṇa-viṣayāśrayatā-maya ity arthaḥ ||5||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bhīṣmaḥ** pūrvavat kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ ||5||

**viśvanāthaḥ : preyasaḥ** sakhyasya **dviṣaḥ** śatravaḥ | **bhīṣmaḥ** bhayānakaḥ | **pūrvavat** śrī-kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ ||5||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.6 ||**

**vatsalasya suhṛd dhāsyaḥ karuṇo bhīṣma-bhit tathā |**

**śatruḥ śucir yuddha-vīraḥ prīto raudraś ca pūrvavat ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : vatsalasya** iti | **hāsya-karuṇāv** atra prathama-traya-gatau | **bhīṣma-bhid** virodhi-hetuka-bhayānaka-bhedaḥ | **śuciḥ** sarva-gataḥ | **yuddha-vīra-raudrau** kṛṣṇena saha pārasparikau | **prīto** vatsalasya kṛṣṇa-viṣayakaḥ | ataḥ pūrvavad ity upalakṣaṇam ||6||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bhīṣma-bhid** dāruṇālambanaḥ raudraś ca pūrvavat kṛṣṇa-vibhāvakaḥ ||6||

**viśvanāthaḥ : bhīṣmabhid** asura-viṣayaka-bhayānaka-bhedaḥ | **prīto** dāsyaṁ pūrvavat śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayaḥ ||6||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.7 ||**

**śucer hāsyas tathā preyān suhṛd asya prakīrtitaḥ |**

**dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-śānta-raudra-bhayānakāḥ |**

**prāhur eke’sya suhṛdaṁ vīra-yugmaṁ pare ripum ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : śucer** iti | **hāsya-preyaḥ-**śāntāḥ prathama-dvaya-gatāḥ | **hāsya-preyāṁsau** tu kvacit sakhī-lakṣaṇa-bhaktāntara-gatau ca | **vatsalaḥ** prathama-traya-gataḥ | **bībhatsaḥ** sarva-gataḥ | **raudra-bhayānakau** prāyaḥ sarva-gatau | **vīra-yugmaṁ** yuddha-dharma-vīra-rūpaṁ, tac ca prathama-traya-gatam | **para** iti tad idaṁ na sva-matam ity abhipretam ||7||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vīra-yugmaṁ** yuddha-dharma-vīra-rūpaṁ, tad eva **pare ripuṁ** **prāhuḥ**—sva-mate sarve taṭasthāḥ ||7||

**viśvanāthaḥ : eke’sya** rasasya **vīra-yugmaṁ** yuddha-dharma-vīra-rūpaṁ **suhṛdaṁ prāhuḥ | pare** iti tad idaṁ na sva-matam ity abhipretam ||7||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.8 ||**

**mitraṁ hāsyasya bībhatsaḥ śuciḥ preyān savatsalaḥ |**

**pratipakṣas tu karuṇas tathā prokto bhayānakaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : mitram** iti | **bībhatso**’tra kṛta-bībhatsita-veśa-vidūṣakādi-lakṣaṇa-bhaktāntara-darśanāt prathama-gatatvena jñeyaḥ | na tv atyanta-bībhatsita-daurgandhādi-darśanāt | tad evaṁ para-paratra tat-tad-dhetutvaṁ tat-tad-gatatvaṁ ca svayam unneyam ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : mitram** iti | **bībhatso**’tra kṛta-bībhatsita-veśa-vidūṣakādi-lakṣaṇa-bhaktāntara-darśanāt, na tv atyanta-bībhatsita-darśanāt ||8||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.9 ||**

**adbhutasya suhṛd vīraḥ pañca śāntādayas tathā |**

**pratipakṣo bhaved asya raudro bībhatsa eva ca ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ**,** viśvanāthaḥ: adbhutasya** iti | alaukika-vastv-antarānubhava-jāta-camatkārasya bhīṣaṇa-bībhatsayor anubhavena vighātaḥ syād ity eva vivakṣitam | atas tayoḥ svataś camatkāra-karatvaṁ tu na niṣidhyate | rase sāraś camatkāraḥ ity asya virodhāt ||9||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.10 ||**

**vīrasya tv adbhuto hāsyaḥ preyān prītis tathā suhṛt |**

**bhayānako vipakṣo’sya kasyacic chānta eva ca ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : vīrasya** iti | śrī-baladevādāv iva yuddha-vīrādeḥ śrī-vrajeśvarādāv iva dāna-vīrāder vatsalaś ca kvacit suhṛd dṛśyate | **bhayānakaḥ śāntaś** ca kasyacid yuddha-vīrasya vipakṣaḥ | dāna-vīrāder bhayānakaś ca jñeyaḥ ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : ** **vīrasya** iti | kasyacid yuddha-vīrasya ||13||

**viśvanāthaḥ : vīrasya** iti | śrī-baladevādāv iva yuddha-vīrādeḥ śrī-vrajeśvarādāv iva dāna-vīrāder vatsalaś ca kvacit suhṛd dṛśyate | kasyacid yuddha-vīrasya bhayānakaḥ śāntaś ca vipakṣaḥ ||10||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.11 ||**

**karuṇasya suhṛd raudro vatsalaś ca vilokyate |**

**vairī hāsyo’sya sambhoga-śṛṅgāraś cādbhutas tathā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : karuṇasya** iti | **raudro** jāta-cara-sva-priya-pīḍanatayā anusmṛtayātra gṛhyate | vartamāna-tādṛśasya bhaya-mātra-janakatvāt ||11||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : karuṇasya** iti | **raudra**-padena pūrvotpannasya sva-priya-jana-pīḍanasya jñānena pūrvam eva jāto yo raudraḥ tasya smaraṇam atra gṛhyate | vartamāna-raudrasya tu bhaya-mātra-janakatvāt | aneka-vidha-śṛṅgārāṇāṁ madhye sambhogātmaka-śṛṅgāra eva vairī ||11||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.12 ||**

**raudrasya karuṇaḥ prokto vīraś cāpi suhṛd-varaḥ |**

**pratipakṣas tu hāsye’sya śṛṅgāro bhīṣaṇo’pi ca ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : raudrasya** iti | **bhīṣaṇo **bhayānakaḥ, sugataḥ ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : raudrasya** iti | **bhīṣaṇo** bhayānakaḥ ||12||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.13 ||**

**bhayānakasya bībhatsaḥ karuṇaś ca suhṛd-varaḥ |**

**dviṣantu vīra-śṛṅgāra-hāsya-raudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||13||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bhayānakasya** iti | atra karuṇasya tu suhṛttvaṁ bhāvi-sva-priya-viyoga-smaraṇāt | vīrādayaḥ sva-gatāḥ ||13||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **vīrasyeti | kasyacid yuddha-vīrasya ||13||

**viśvanāthaḥ : bhayānakasya** iti | atra karuṇasya tu suhṛttvaṁ bhāvi-sva-priya-viyoga-smaraṇāt ||13||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.14 ||**

**bībhatsasya bhavec chānto hāsyaḥ prītis tathā suhṛt |**

**śatruḥ śucis tathā preyān jñeyā yuktyā pare ca te ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bībhatsasya** iti | **śānto**’tra tāpasālambanakaḥ, prīta āraddha-rati-bhaktādy-avalambanaḥ | **hāsyasya** suhṛttvaṁ vidūṣakādi-kṛta-kuveśādau jñeyaṁ, na tu sarvatra ||14||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : bībhatsasya** iti | **hāsasya** suhṛttvaṁ vidūṣakādi-kṛta-kuveṣādau jñeyaṁ, na tu sarvatra ||14||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.15-17 ||**

tatra **suhṛt-kṛtyam—**

**kathitebhyaḥ pare ye syus te taṭasthāḥ satāṁ matāḥ ||**

**suhṛdā miśraṇāṁ samyag āsvādaṁ**[^7]** kurute rasam ||**

**dvayos tu miśraṇe sāmyaṁ duḥśakaṁ syāt tulā-dhṛtam |**

**tasmād aṅgāṅgi-bhāvena melanaṁ viduṣāṁ matam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : kathitebhya** iti sākṣād-uktebhyo yuktyā jñātebhyaś cety arthaḥ ||15|| **dvayos tv** ity ardhasya pareṇānvayaḥ | **tulayā** yutam atyantaṁ yathā syāt tathā **duḥśakaṁ** bhāvayitum aśakyam ity arthaḥ | **melanam** ekadā bhāvanam ||15-17||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kathitebhya** iti sākṣād-uktebhyo yuktyā jñātebhyaś cety arthaḥ ||15|| **tūlā-dhṛtam **atyanta-sāmyam | **melanam** ekatra saṅgatiḥ ||17||

**viśvanāthaḥ : kathitebhya** iti | sākṣād uktebhyaḥ yuktyā jñātebhyaś cety arthaḥ | **suhṛdā** saha milanam eva rasaṁ **samyag āsvādyaṁ kurute** | tatra rasa-dvaya-milane **tulayā dhṛtam** ātyantikaṁ **sāmyaṁ** **duḥśakaṁ** bhāvayitum aśakyam ity arthaḥ | melanam ekadotpannatvam ||15-17||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.18-19 ||**

**bhaven mukhyo’thavā gauṇo raso’ṅgī kila yatra yaḥ |**

**kartavyaṁ tatra tasyāṅgaṁ suhṛd eva raso budhaiḥ ||**

**athāṅgitvaṁ prathamato mukhyānām iha likhyate |**

**aṅgatāṁ yatra suhṛdo mukhyā gauṇāś ca bibhrati ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : yatra yo mukhya-rasaḥ gauṇa-raso vā aṅgī bhavet**, **tatra tasya** rasasya **suhṛd** eva **raso**’ṅgīkartavyaḥ, na tu vairī | na vā udāsīna ity arthaḥ ||18|| **athāṅgitvam** iti | **prathamato** **mukhyānāṁ** śāntādīnām **aṅgitvaṁ likhyate** | **yatra** **mukhya**-rasa-rūpe aṅgini **suhṛdo mukhya**-rasāḥ **suhṛdo gauṇa**-rasāś ca **aṅgatāṁ bibhrati** ity anvayaḥ ||19||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.20 ||**

tatra **śānte’ṅgini prītasyāṅgatā**, yathā—

**jīva-sphuliṅga-vahner mahaso ghana-cit-svarūpasya |**

**tasya padāmbuja-yugalaṁ kiṁ vā saṁvāhayiṣyāmi ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atra mukhye’ṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : jīva-sphuliṅga-vahner** iti śrautānuvādaḥ | sa ca jīveśayor aṁśāṁśitā-prāmāṇyāya | **ghanaḥ** śrī-vigrahas tad-ākārā vā **cit** sac-cid-ānanda-lakṣaṇaṁ paraṁ brahma, saiva svarūpaṁ yasya, tādṛśatvena mamālambanasyeti tatra sva-niṣṭhā darśitā | tasmāc chāntasyāṅgitvaṁ, aṅgatve’pi tādṛg-uttama-suhṛd-āliṅgitatvena praśastatvam api dhvanitam | kintv atrāpy aṅgatve’pi prītasya [śāntasya] prābalyaṁ, dadhni sitāyā ivāsvādādhikyād iti jñeyam | pāda-saṁvāhanecchā ca paramānanda-vigrahasya tasya sparśānanda-prāptīcchayaiva, na tu sāhāyyenānanda-dānecchayā, pūrṇānandakatvena tasya sphuraṇāt | evam uttaratrāpi ||20||

**mukundadāsaḥ : ghanā** niviḍā **cit** sac-cid-ānanda-lakṣaṇaṁ paraṁ brahma, saiva **rūpam** ākāro yasya | tasya īdṛśatvena sadānubhūyamānasyeti tatra sva-niṣṭhā darśitā | asya prīte’bhilāṣaḥ kṛpā viśeṣa-lābhāt | sthāyinaḥ śāntasya prīta-sañcāritāṁ prāpya poṣaka iti jñeyam | agre gṛhītatvety atrāpi | atra śloke ||20||

**viśvanāthaḥ : jīva-rūpa-sphuliṅgānāṁ vahner** agni-puñjasya | etena jīveśayor aṁśāṁśitā pratipāditā | **mahasas** tejasaḥ svarūpasyety anena sva-prakāśatvam uktam | **ghana-cit-svarūpasya** niviḍa-jñānānanda-svarūpasya tādṛśatvena mamālambanasyeti | tatra sva-niṣṭhā darśitā | tasmāc chāntasyāṅgitvam ||20||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.21 ||**

tatraiva **bībhatsasya**, yathā—

**aham iha kapha-śukra-śoṇitānāṁ**

**pṛthu-kutupe kutukī rataḥ śarīre |**

**śiva śiva paramātmano durātmā**

**sukha-vapuṣaḥ smaraṇe’pi mantharo’smi ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atra mukhya eva gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : kutupe** svalpa-carma-puṭake | **kutukī** vicitra-viṣayāsvādāya sotsāhaḥ | tatraiva śānte ||21||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kutupe** svalpa-carma-puṭake | **kutukī** vicitra-viṣayāsvāde sotsāhaḥ ||21||

**viśvanāthaḥ : pṛthu-kutupe** vistṛta-carma-puṭake **śarīre** **rato’haṁ durātmā** | kathaṁ-bhūtaḥ ? **kutukī** vicitra-viṣayāsvādāya sotsāhaḥ | tatraiva śānte aṅgini prītāder aṅgitvam ||21||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.22 ||**

tatraiva **prītasyādbhuta-bībhatsayoś ca**, yathā—

**hitvāsmin piśitopanaddha-rudhira-klinne mudaṁ vigrahe**

**prīty-utsikta-manāḥ kadāham asakṛd-dustarka-caryāspadam |**

**āsīnaṁ puraṭāsanopari paraṁ brahmāmbuda-śyāmalaṁ**

**seviṣye cala-cāru-cāmara-marut-sañcāra-cāturyataḥ ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhya eva mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : dustarka-caryāspadam** ity anenādbhuta-rasaḥ | saṁvāhanecchāvat **seviṣya** ity-ādīcchā ca tat-saurabhyādy-atiśayānubhavārthā jñeyā | yathā tasyāravinda-nayanasya [bhā.pu. 3.15.43] ity-ādikaṁ śrī-sanakādīnāṁ śrūyate, tadvat ||22||

**mukundadāsaḥ : hitvāsmin** nityātmārāma-śānta-vacanam | **mudaṁ** svabhāvajāṁ prītim ||22||

**viśvanāthaḥ : asmin vigrahe** dehe **mudaṁ hitvā** **prītyā utsika-manā** **ahaṁ** svarṇa-**siṁhāsanopari** **āsīnaṁ** kṛtopaveśam **ambuda-śyāmalaṁ brahma** bhagavantaṁ **kadā** **seviṣye** ? kathaṁ-bhūtaṁ ? **dustarkasya caryā** ācaraṇaṁ yatra, tathā-bhūtasya **āspadam** dhāma yasya, tathā-bhūtam | dustarkety anenādbhuta-rasaḥ | **piśita-** ity-ādinā bībhatsa-rasaḥ | aṅgini **mukhye** śānta-rase **mukhyasya** dāsyasya **gauṇayor** adbhuta-bībhatsayor aṅgatvaṁ jñeyam ||22||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.23 ||**

atha **prīte śāntasya**, yathā—

**niravidyatayā sapady ahaṁ **

**niravadyaḥ pratipadya-mādhurīm | \
aravinda-vilocanaṁ kadā **

**prabhum indīvara-sundaraṁ bhaje ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atra mukhye mukhyasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : niravidyatayā** avidyā-rahitatayeti śānti-vāsanā ||23||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : niravidyatayā** avidyā-rāhityena **niravadyaḥ** nirdūṣaṇaḥ san **kadāhaṁ prabhuṁ bhaje** ? kathaṁ-bhūtaṁ ? **pratipadyā** prapadyā **mādhurī** yasya tam | niravidyatayeti śānti-vāsanā ||23||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.24 ||**

tatraiva **bībhatsasya**, yathā—

**smaran prabhu-pādāmbhojaṁ naṭann aṭati vaiṣṇavaḥ |**

**yas tu dṛṣṭyā padminīnām api suṣṭhu hṛṇīyate ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : smarann** iti | **aṭati** bhramati | **hṛṇīyate** ghṛnāṁ karoti | pāṭhāntaraṁ tyaktam ||24||

**mukundadāsaḥ : hṛṇīyamāno** hrīṇaḥ | “smaraṇe hariṇī-dṛśāṁ prabho deva jayety uccair naṭann aṭati vaiṣṇavaḥ” iti pāṭhaḥ | **smaraṇe** yathā kathañcin manasā sambandhe hrīṇo lajjitaḥ san hṛṇīyamāno ghṛṇāṁ kurvan **prabho deva jayeti** vākyam **uccair** dūra-vyāpi yathā syāt tathā **naṭan** nṛtyaṁ kurvan **aṭati** mandaṁ mandaṁ gacchati ||24||

**viśvanāthaḥ : aṭati** bhramati **padminīnāṁ** sundarīṇām api **darśanena** **hṛṇīyate** ghṛṇāṁ karoti ||24||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.25 ||**

tatraiva **bībhatsa-śānta-vīrāṇāṁ**, yathā—

**tanoti mukha-vikriyāṁ yuvati-saṅga-raṅgodaye **

**na tṛpyati na sarvataḥ sukha-maye samādhāv api |**

**na siddhiṣu ca lālasāṁ vahati dīyamānāsv**[^8]** api **

**prabho tava padārcane param upaiti tṛṣṇāṁ manaḥ ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : **brahma-samādhāv api nimitte yat sarvaṁ śravaṇa-mananādikaṁ tatra **na** **na tṛpyati**, api tu tṛpyaty eva alaṁ-buddhiṁ karoty evety arthaḥ | **dīyamānasv** ity atra tvayeti gamyam, sādaratayaiva tad-anuktiḥ | “labhyamānāsv api” iti pāṭhāntaraṁ spaṣṭam ||25||

**mukundadāsaḥ : yuvatī-saṅga-raṅgodaye** yuvatibhiḥ saṅge yaḥ pūrvaṁ **raṅgaḥ**, tasya **udaye** manasy udgame **sukha-maye** brahma-sukha-svarūpe **na tṛpyati**, na, api tu tṛpyaty eva, alaṁ-buddhiṁ karoty evety arthaḥ | **dīyamānāsv** apīty atrārthā tvayeti gamyam ||25||

**viśvanāthaḥ : yuvatī-saṅge** kasyacit kautukodaye sati **mukha-vikriyām** ity anena bībhatsaḥ | brahma-samādhāv api nimitte yat śravaṇa-mananādikaṁ tatra **na na tṛpyati**, tṛpyaty eva, alaṁ-buddhiṁ karoty evety arthaḥ | anena śāntaḥ | tvayā **dīyamānāsu** **siddhiṣu lālasāṁ** **na vahati** ity anena prāptānāṁ parityāgād dāna-vīraḥ | **paraṁ** kevalam ||25||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.26 ||**

atha **preyasi śucer, **yathā—

**dhanyānāṁ kila mūrdhanyāḥ subalāmūr vrajābalāḥ |**

**adharaṁ piñcha-cūḍasya calāś culūkayanti yāḥ ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
	<strong>atra mukhye mukhyasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : dhanyānām** ity anumodanātmikaiveyaṁ śuci-bhāvanā, na tu sambhogecchā-mayātmikā, teṣāṁ sva-svarūpa eva nitya-sthiteḥ ||26||

**mukundadāsaḥ : piñcha-cūḍasya** iti preyān ||26||

**viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.27 ||**

tatraiva **hāsasya**, yathā—

**dṛśos taralitair alaṁ vraja nivṛtya mugdhe vrajaṁ**

**vitarkayasi māṁ yathā na hi tathāsmi kiṁ bhūriṇā |**

**itīrayati mādhave nava-vilāsinīṁ chadmanā **

**dadarśa subalo valad-vikaca-dṛṣṭir asyānanam ||**


    <p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : dṛśor** ity atra saty api śucy-aṁśe hāsyāṁś ca naivodāharaṇaṁ darśyate ||27|| 

**mukundadāsaḥ : dṛśor** iti | **ānanaṁ** **dadarśa** iti preyān | **valad-vikaca**- ity anena hāsyo darśitaḥ ||27||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kāñcid vraja-sundarīṁ prati śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ sa-parihāsam āha—he **mugdhe** ! **nivṛtya vrajaṁ gaccha**, **kiṁ bhūriṇā** prayāsena | **nava-vilāsinīṁ** prati **chadmanā mādhave itīrayati** sati **valad-vikaca**-hāsyenātiśaya-praphullā tathā-bhūtaḥ **subalo**’sya śrī-kṛṣṇasya **mukhaṁ dadarśa** ||27||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.28 ||**

tatraiva **śuci**-**hāsyayoḥ**, yathā—

**mihira-duhitur udyad-vañjulaṁ mañju-tīraṁ**

**praviśati subalo’yaṁ rādhikā-veṣa-gūḍhaḥ |**

**sa-rabhasam abhipaśyan kṛṣṇam abhyutthitaṁ yaḥ**

**smita-vikaśita-gaṇḍaṁ svīyam āsyaṁ vṛṇoti ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : vṛṇoti** āvṛṇoti | prācīyaṁ prāntato vṛtiḥ ity amara-darśanāt ||28||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : mihira-duhitur** yamunāyā **mañju-tīraṁ** **rādhikā-veśena guptaḥ subalaḥ praviśati** | kīdṛśaṁ ? **udyan vañjulo** yatra tathā-bhūtam | **sarabhasaṁ** saharṣaṁ yathā syāt tathā bhrameṇa śrī-rādhikā-sparśārtham **abhyutthitaṁ** śrī-**kṛṣṇaṁ paśyan**, **yaḥ** subalaḥ **smitena vikaśitaṁ gaṇḍaṁ** yasmin, tat **svīya-mukhaṁ** vastreṇa **āvṛṇoti** ||28||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.29 ||**

atha **vatsale karuṇasya—**

**nirātapatraḥ kāntāre santataṁ mukta-pādukaḥ |**

**vatsān avati vatso me hanta santapyate manaḥ ||29||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : nirātapatra** iti | atra aniṣṭāśaṅkīnīva bandhu-hṛdayāṇi iti śaṅkā-cintātiśayena śokaṁ sambhāvya śrī-vrajeśvarī-vacanāt karuṇāvakāśaḥ ||29|

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : kāntāre** durga-vartmani **nirātapatraḥ** ātapa-nivartaka-cchatrādi-rahitaḥ pāda-trāṇa-rahitaś ca me bālako **vatsān avati** | atra "aniṣṭa-śaṅkīni bandhu-hṛdayāṇi" iti cittasya śaṅkātiśayena śokaṁ sambhāvya śrī-vrajeśvarī-vacanāt karuṇāvakāśaḥ ||29||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.30 ||**

tatraiva **hāsyasya**, yathā—

**putras te navanīta-piṇḍam atanuṁ muṣṇan mamāntar-gṛhād**

**vinyasyāpasasāra tasya kaṇikāṁ nidrāṇa-ḍimbhānane |**

**ity uktā kula-vṛddhayā suta-mukhe dṛṣṭiṁ vibhugna-bhruṇi**

**smerāṁ nikṣipatī sadā bhavatu vaḥ kṣemāya goṣṭheśvarī ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atrāpi mukhye gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : tava putraḥ atanuṁ** sthūlaṁ **navanīta-piṇḍaṁ muṣṇan** **mama gṛha**-madhye **nidrāṇasya bālakasyānane** tasya piṇḍasya **kaṇikāṁ vinyasya apasasāra** **kula-vṛddhayā ity uktā goṣṭheśvarī suta-mukhe smerāṁ** hāsya-yuktāṁ **dṛṣṭiṁ nikṣipantī** satī **vaḥ kṣemāya bhavatu** | suta-mukhe kathaṁ-bhūte ? vṛddhāṁ praty asūyayā **vibhugnā bhrūr** yasya tathā-bhūte ||30||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.31 ||**

tatraiva **bhayānakādbhuta-hāsya-karuṇānāṁ**, yathā—

**kamprā svedini cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe sphārekṣaṇā tuṅgite **

**savye doṣṇi vikāśi-gaṇḍa-phalakā līlāsya-bhaṅgī-śate |**

**bibhrāṇasya harer girīndram udayad-bāṣpā cirordhva-sthitau **

**pātu prasnava-sicyamāna-sicayā viśvaṁ vrajādhīśvarī ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
	<strong>atrāpi mukhye catūrṇāṁ gauṇānām |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : savye doṣṇi girīndraṁ bibhrāṇasya hareś** **cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe svedini** sati **kamprā** ity-ādikaṁ yojyam ||31||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : govardhanaṁ bibhrāṇasya hareś cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe prasvedini** sati **kamprā**, govardhanasya patanāśaṅkayā **vrajeśvarī viśvaṁ pātu** | tasya **hareḥ savye doṣṇi** vāme haste **tuṅgite** govardhana-dhāraṇārtham uccī-kṛte sati **sphārekṣaṇā**, sapta-varṣa-bālakasya sāhasa-darśanād vismayena vistṛtekṣaṇā | harer līlayā sahacara-bālakaiḥ saha hāsyopahāsyena mukhasya bhaṅgī-śate sati hāsyena **vikāśi-gaṇḍa-phalakā**, saptāha-rūpa-**cira**-kālaṁ vyāpya harer vāma-bhuje **ūrdhva-sthitau** **udayad-bāṣpa**-dhārā-yuktā yaśodā vātsalyāt **prasnavena sicyamānaṁ sicayaṁ** vastraṁ yasyās tathā-bhūtā ||31||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.32 ||**

**kevale vatsale nāsti mukhyasya khalu sauhṛdam |**

**ato’tra vatsale tasya natarāṁ likhitāṅgatā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : kevale** śuddhe **vatsale** tatra nāstīty upalakṣaṇaṁ kutracid anyatrāpy unneyam | **tasya** mukhyasya ||32||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : kevale** śuddhe **vātsalye mukhyasya** rasasya **aṅgatā** nāsti, kintu gauṇasyaivety arthaḥ | **tasya** mukhyasya ||32|| 

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.33 ||**

atha** ujjvale preyaso**, yathā—

**mad-veṣa-śīlita-tanoḥ subalasya paśya**

**vinyasya mañju-bhuja-mūrdhni bhujaṁ mukundaḥ |**

**romāñca-kañcuka-juṣaḥ sphuṭam asya karṇe**

**sandeśam arpayati tanvi mad-artham eva ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atra mukhye mukhyasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : mad-veśa-** iti | subalena tad-veśa-karaṇam idaṁ narmaṇeti jñeyam ||33||

**mukundadāsaḥ : mad-veśa-** iti | atra subala-viṣayakau kṛṣṇa-rasau ||33||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **subalena tad-veśa-karaṇam idaṁ narmaṇeti jñeyam ||33||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.34 ||**

tatraiva **hāsyasya**, yathā—

**svasāsmi tava nirdaye paricinoṣi na tvaṁ kutaḥ **

**kuru praṇaya-nirbharaṁ mama kṛśāṅgi kaṇṭha-graham |**

**iti bruvati peśalaṁ yuvati-veṣa-gūḍhe harau**

**kṛtaṁ smitam abhijñayā guru-puras tadā rādhayā ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye gauṇasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : svasāsmi tava nirdaye** ity ardhe | “tavāsmi savayaś-carī smarasi māṁ kaṭhore na kiṁ ? kuru pranāya-nirbharaṁ mama sukaṇṭhi kaṇṭha-graham” iti pāṭhāntaram ||34||

**mukundadāsaḥ : abhijñayā** iti śuciḥ ||34||

**viśvanāthaḥ : abhijñayā** śrī-kṛṣṇa eva **yuvati-veśaṁ **gṛhītvā **mat-kaṇṭha-grahaṇārtham** āgata iti viśeṣa-jñānavatyā **rādhayā** **gurūṇām** agre **smitaṁ kṛtam** ||34||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.35 ||**

tatraiva **preyo-vīrayor **yathā—

**mukundo’yaṁ candrāvali-vadana-candre caṭulabhe**

**smara-smerām ārād dṛśam asakalām arpayati ca |**

**bhujām aṁse sakhyuḥ pulakini dadhānaḥ phani-nibhām **

**ibhāri-kṣveḍābhir vṛṣa-danujam udyojayati ca ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : mukundo’yam** iti | śrī-**candrāvalī**-sakhyā bhāvanā | sā ca tayor madhurāṁ ratim ālambyaiva pravṛttā | preyo-vīrau tu tad-anusaṅginau vidhāyeti yuktam uktaṁ **tatraiva preyo-vīrayor yathā **iti | evam anyatrāpi jñeyam | **ibhānām arayo** vidrāvikā yā **kṣveḍāḥ** siṁha-nādās tābhiḥ ||35||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kṣveḍā** syāt siṁhavan nāda iti kṣveḍā-śabdāl labdhasyāpi **ibhāreḥ** punar grahaṇaṁ śrī-candrāvaly-ādau tāsāṁ madhura-bhara-prakāśena acintya-prabhāvatārthaṁ puṣpa-māletivat | atra vīrasya citratvaṁ para-matam api svīkṛtam ||35||

**viśvanāthaḥ : mukunda** iti candrāvalī-sakhyā vacanam | **smareṇa** kandarpeṇa **smerām asakalām** asampūrṇāṁ duḥkha-saṅkaṭābhyām iti yāvat | **phaṇi-nibhāṁ** sarpa-tulyāṁ **bhujāṁ** pulaka-viśiṣṭe **sakhyuḥ** skandha-deśe **dadhānaḥ**, **ibhāri-kṣveḍābhiḥ** siṁha-nādaiḥ ariṣṭaṁ yuddhārtham **udvejayati** ||35||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.36-37 ||**

atha **gauṇānām aṅgitā—**

**hāsyādīnāṁ tu gauṇānāṁ yad udāharaṇaṁ kṛtam |**

**tenaiṣām aṅgitā vyaktā mukhyānāṁ ca tathāṅgatā |**

**tathāpy alpa-viśeṣāya kiñcid eva vilikhyate ||**

atha **hāsye’ṅgini śucer aṅgatā**, yathā—

**madanāndhatayā tri-vakrayā **

**prasabhaṁ pīta-paṭāñcale dhṛte |**

**adadhād vinataṁ janāgrato**

**harir utphulla-kapolam ānanam ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra gauṇe’ṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : janāgrato vinatam** iti śuciḥ ||37||

**viśvanāthaḥ : trivakrayā** kubjayā ||37||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.38 ||**

**vīre preyaso**, yathā—

**senānyaṁ vijitam avekṣya bhadrasenaṁ**

**māṁ yoddhuṁ milasi puraḥ kathaṁ viśāla |**

**rāmāṇāṁ śatam api nodbhaṭoru-dhāmā **

**śrīdāmā gaṇayati re tvam atra ko’si ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atrāpi gauṇe’ṅgini mukhyasya |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : **atrāpity **atra** mukhyasyeti śrīdāmno rāma-pratiyoddhuh kṛṣṇa-pakṣa-praveśena tat-sakhye spaṣṭatāpatteḥ ||38||

**mukundadāsaḥ : senānyam** ity atra śrīdāmnaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-prītaye yuddhādi-karaṇāt preyān ||38||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he **viśāla** ! **bhadrasenaṁ** mama **senānyaṁ parājitam avekṣya kathaṁ yoddhuṁ māṁ milasi** ? **udbhaṭa-tejā** ahaṁ **śrīdāmā** **rāmāṇāṁ śatam api na gaṇayati** ||38||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.39 ||**

**raudre preyo-vīrayor**, yathā—

**yadunandana nindanoddhataṁ **

**śiśupālaṁ samare jighāṁsubhiḥ |**

**atilohita-locanotpalair **

**jagṛhe pāṇḍu-sutair varāyudham ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>atra gauṇe mukhya-gauṇayoḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ, viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : varāyudhaṁ jagṛhe** iti vīraḥ ||39||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.40 ||**

**adbhute preyo-vīra-hāsyānāṁ**, yathā—

**mitrāṇīka-vṛtaṁ gadā-yudhi guruṁ-manyaṁ pralamba-dviṣaṁ **

**yaṣṭyā durbalayā vijitya purataḥ solluṇṭham udgāyataḥ |**

**śrīdāmnaḥ kila vīkṣya keli-samarāṭopotsave pāṭavaṁ**

**kṛṣṇaḥ phulla-kapolakaḥ pulakavān visphāra-dṛṣṭir babhau ||**


    <p style="text-align: right">
atra <strong>gauṇe mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca </strong>|</p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : mitrāṇīka-vṛtam** iti kasyacid anyasya sakhyur vākyam | asyaiva caite rasā udāhāryāḥ, na tu śrī-kṛṣṇasya, bhakti-rasasyaiva prakṛtatvāt | **durbalayā yaṣṭyā vijitya** iti śikṣā-viśeṣādhikyam abhipretam | sakhitvenāṅgīkṛteṣu sambhavati ca tat tad iti | “samarāṭopa-krame” ity eva pāṭhaḥ ||40||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **“samarāṭopotsave” iti pāṭhaḥ | **śrīdāmna** iti viṣayālambanoktyā preyān | **kṛṣṇaḥ phulla-kapolaka** ity-ādi viśiṣṭo **babhāv** ity asyāyam arthaḥ—vibhāvādīnāṁ śravaṇādinā puṣṭā sādhakānāṁ ratiḥ rasaḥ syāt | vibhāvair ālambanair ity-ādinā darśitam eva | vibhāvāś ca vairūpya-rahitā eva śravaṇādinānubhūtā ratiṁ puṣṭāṁ kurvanti | teṣāṁ vairūpye rateḥ saṅkoca eva, kutaḥ puṣṭatā ? rater asyāḥ prabhāvo’pi vairūpye ati kuñcatīti, vairūpyaṁ tu vibhāvāder anaucityam udīryata iti ca | ekatra rati-varṇane sthāyi-vairūpyaṁ syāt | paraspara-raty-ādeḥ kṛṣṇa-bhaktau viṣayāśrayau darśitāv eva | ata eva sahacara-nikurambaṁ bhrātar ārya praviṣṭam [bha.ra.si. 3.3.20] ity ādau | kaṁsāsuram api [?] ity ādau | mukundo’yam [bha.ra.si. 4.8.35] ity ādau | **mitrānika-** ity atrānyatra ca bahutra śrī-kṛṣṇasyāpi bhakta-viṣayo raty-ādir darśita iti ||40||

**viśvanāthaḥ : mitrāṇīka-vṛtam** iti kasyacid anyasya sakhyur vacanam | tasyaiva caite rasā udāhāryāḥ, na tu śrī-kṛṣṇasya, bhakti-rasasyaiva prakṛtatvāt | **durbalayā yaṣṭyā vijitya** iti śikṣā-viśeṣādhikyam abhipretam | hāsyena **phulla-kapolakaḥ,** vismayena **visphāra-dṛṣṭiḥ** ||40||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.41-43 ||**

**evam anyasya gauṇasya jñeyā kavibhir aṅgitā |**

**tathā ca mukhya-gauṇānāṁ rasānām aṅgatāpi ca ||**

**so’ṅgī sarvātigo yaḥ syān mukhyo gauṇo’thavā rasaḥ |**

**sa evāṅgaṁ bhaved aṅgi-poṣī sañcāritāṁ vrajan ||**

tathā ca nāṭyācāryāḥ paṭhanti—

**eka eva bhavet sthāyī raso mukhyatamo hi yaḥ |**

**rasās tad-anuyāyitvād anye syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **athāṅgāṅginoḥ sāmānyato lakṣaṇam āha—**so’ṅgī** iti | bahūnāṁ **rasānāṁ** milane **mukhyo** vā **gauṇo** vā **raso** bhavatu, kintu yaḥ **sarvātigaḥ** sarvāpekṣayā āsvādyatvenādhikaḥ, **so’ṅgī**, yaḥ svayaṁ **sañcāritāṁ** **vrajan** san **aṅgi-poṣakaḥ** **sa evāṅgam** | anye rasā mukhyasyānuyāyitvād vyabhicāriṇaḥ syuḥ ||42||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.44-45 ||**

śrī-viṣṇu-dharmottare ca—

**rasānāṁ samavetānāṁ yasya rūpaṁ bhaved bahu |**

**sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇo matāḥ ||**[^9]

**stokād vibhāvanāj jātaḥ samprāpya vyabhicāritām |**

**puṣṇan nija-prabhuṁ mukhyaṁ gauṇas tatraiva līyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : rūpaṁ** svarūpaṁ, **bahu** adhikam _|_ **śeṣāḥ** **sañcāriṇo matāḥ** iti tan-mate’pi sva-svādhārād avyabhicāriṇau śṛṅgāra-śāntau sañcāriṇāv iva, sva-svādhārād vyabhicāriṇo hāsyādayas tu sañcāriṇa eveti bhedāṁśe labdhe’pi yathā poṣakatāṁśena sahayogitāṁśa-bheda-vivakṣā, tathātrāpi—sa evāṅgam [bha.ra.si. 4.8.42] ity-ādinoktam iti darśitam ||44||

**mukundadāsaḥ : rasānām **iti | **rūpaṁ** svarūpaṁ **bahu** sarvātigam ||44|| **stokād** iti | tatraiva **nija-prabhāv** eva ||45||

**viśvanāthaḥ : rūpaṁ** svarūpaṁ **bahu** adhikaṁ bhavet, **śeṣā** rasāḥ **sañcāriṇo matāḥ** ||44|| aneka-rasānāṁ milanena yaḥ **stokāt** svalpāt **vibhāvanāj** **jātaḥ,** sa eva gauṇaḥ san vyabhicāritāṁ samprāpya mukhyaṁ puṣṇan, tatraivamukhye rase līyate, prapāṇaka-rase marīcādival līnaḥ san āsvādyo bhavatīty arthaḥ ||44-45||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.46-48 ||**

**prodyan vibhāvanotkarṣāt puṣṭiṁ mukhyena lambhitaḥ |**

**kuñcatā nija-nāthena gauṇo’py aṅgitvam aśnute ||**

**mukhyas tv aṅgatvam āsādya puṣṇann indram upendravat |**

**gauṇam evāṅginaṁ kṛtvā nigūḍha-nija-vaibhavaḥ || \
anādi-vāsanodbhāsa-vāsite bhakta-cetasi |**

**bhāty eva na tu līnaḥ syād eṣa sañcāri-gauṇavat ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : anādi-** ity upalakṣaṇaṁ pūrva-siddhatve tātparyam | **sañcāri gauṇavad** iti vyatireke dṛṣṭāntaḥ, yathā sañcāri-gauṇo **līno** bhavati, tathā na mukhyo līno bhavatīty arthaḥ, sañcārivad gauṇavac ca nety arthaḥ _|_|48||

**mukundadāsaḥ : anādi-** iti | nitya-siddha-bhakta-prakaraṇatvāt | anya-bhakta-prasaṅge tu pūrva-siddhasyopalakṣaṇaṁ tat | sañcārī cāsau gauṇaś ca sañcāri-gauṇas tadvat _|_|48||

**viśvanāthaḥ : gauṇo’pi **rasaḥ **vibhāvanotkarṣād** dhetoḥ **pra**karṣeṇa** udyan** san **saṅkucatā** **nija-nāthena** **mukhyena** rasena **puṣṭiṁ lambhitaḥ** prāpitaḥ **aṅgitvam aśnute** prāpnoti ||46||

**anādi-** ity upalakṣaṇaṁ pūrva-siddhatve tātparyam | **eṣa** aṅgi-rasaḥ sphuṭaṁ **bhāty eva**, **na tu sañcārival līno** bhavati | **sañcāri gauṇavad** iti vyatireke dṛṣṭāntaḥ, **sañcāri-gauṇavac** ca nety arthaḥ _|_|48||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.49 ||**

**aṅgī mukhyaḥ svam atrāṅgair bhāvais tair abhivardhayan |**

**sajātīyair vijātīyaiḥ svatantraḥ san virājate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : svam atrāṅgair** ity eva pāṭhaḥ | **vijātīyaiḥ** śatru-varjitaiḥ kaiścit pūrva-darśitair anyair api ||49||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bhāvair **nirvedādi-hāsādibhiḥ **sva-jātīyair** ātmānaṁ **vardhayan vijātīyair** viruddhaiḥ **svatantras** tad-vaśyatā-rahitaḥ ||49||

**viśvanāthaḥ : sajātīyaiḥ** samāna-jātīyaiḥ, **vijātīyaiḥ** śatru-varjitaiḥ kaiścit pūrva-darśitair api ||49||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.50 ||**

**yasya mukhyasya yo bhakto bhaven nitya-nijāśrayaḥ |**

**aṅgī sa eva tatra syān mukhyo’py anyo’ṅgatāṁ vrajet ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : mukhyasya** iti | līlā-bhedena prakaṭita-nija-mukhyatā-viśeṣasyety arthaḥ ||50||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : yasya mukhya-rasasya yo bhaktaḥ nityam** eva **nijāśrayo bhavati**, **sa eva mukhyo **rasaḥ **aṅgī** | **anya** āgantuko rasas tasya **aṅgatāṁ vrajet** ||50||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.51-52 ||**

**kiṁ ca—**

**āsvādodreka-hetutvam aṅgasyāṅgatvam aṅgini |**

**tad vinā tasya sampāto vaiphalyāyaiva kalpate ||**

**yathā mṛṣṭa-rasālāyāṁ yavasādeḥ kathañcana |**

**tac-carvaṇe bhaved eva satṛṇābhyavahāritā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : aṅgini** yad **aṅgasyāṅgatvaṁ,** tat khalv **āsvādodreka-hetutvam** eva, nānyad ity arthaḥ | tad eva darśayati—**tad vinā** iti ||51||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **taṭasthasyāṅgini saṅgatiḥ kāryā na vā ? tatrāha—**kiṁ ca** ity-ādi | **tad vinā** aṅgaṁ vinā **tasya** anyasya taṭasthasya **sampāto** melanam ||51||

**viśvanāthaḥ : aṅgini** rase ya **āsvādodrekaḥ,** tasya **hetutva**-rūpam **evāṅgasyāṅgatvaṁ**, nānyat | tad eva darśayati—**tad vinā** iti | **tad vinā** āsvādodreka-hetutvaṁ vinā **tasya** aṅga-rasasya rasa-varṇanāyāṁ **sampāto** **vaiphalyāya** ||51|| yathā pānaka-prabheda-mārjita-**rasālāyāṁ** **kathañcana** daivāt patitasya **yavasādeḥ** ghāsādeḥ **carvaṇe** sati sa-tṛṇābhyavahāritā[^10] tṛṇa-sahitottama-bhojana-kartṛkatā bhavet ||52||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.53-54 ||**

atha **vairi-kṛtyam—**

**janayaty eva vairasyaṁ rasānāṁ vairiṇā yutiḥ |**

**sumṛṣṭa-pānakādīnāṁ kṣāra-tiktādinā yathā ||**

yathā hi— 

**brahmiṣṭhāyā niṣphalo me vyatītaḥ**

**kālo bhūyān hā samādhi-vratena |**

**sāndrānandaṁ tan mayā brahma mūrtaṁ**

**koṇenākṣṇaḥ sāci savyasya naikṣi ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	tatra śāntasyojjvalena vairasyam |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : vairiṇā** rasena saha **yutir** milanaṁ **vairasyam** ||53|| brahma-jñānavatyā **mama** **samādhi-vratena bhūyān kālo niṣphalaṁ vyatītaḥ**, **sāndrānandaṁ mūrtaṁ tad brahma savyasya** vāmasya **akṣṇaḥ** **koṇena** **sāci** vakraṁ yathā syāt, tathā **naikṣi** na dṛṣṭam ity arthaḥ ||54||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.55 ||**

**kṣaṇam api pitṛ-koṭi-vatsalaṁ taṁ**

**sura-muni-vandita-pādam indireśam |**

**abhilaṣati varāṅganā-nakhāṅkaiḥ **

**prabhum īkṣituṁ mano me ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	tatra prītasyojjvalenaiva |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : kṣaṇam api** ity atrāśraya-bhede’pi vairiṇo mukhyād vairasyam eva tat ||55||

**viśvanāthaḥ : varāṅganā-nakha-** ity anena śṛṅgāra-rasaḥ ||55||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.56 ||**

**dorbhyām argala-dīrghābhyāṁ sakhe parirabhasva mām |**

**śiraḥ kṛṣṇa tavāghrāya vihariṣye tatas tvayā ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra preyaso vatsalena |</strong></p>


_na kenāpi vyākhyātam._

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.57 ||**

**yaṁ samasta-nigamāḥ parameśaṁ **

**sātvatās tu bhagavantam uśanti |**

**tat suteti bata sāhasikīṁ tvāṁ**

**vyājihīrṣatu kathaṁ mama jihvā ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
	<strong>atra vatsalasya prītena |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : samasta-nigamā** iti | tat tu samanvayāt [ve.sū. 1.1.4] iti nyāyena samastaṁ nigamayanti nigamārthaṁ samastaṁ samanvitaṁ kurvanti ye te vedāntina ity arthaḥ | **parameśaṁ** para-brahma-paryāyaṁ **sātvatāḥ** pāñcarātrikāḥ | **bhagavantaṁ** vāsudeva-paryāyam ||57||

**mukundadāsaḥ : yaṁ samasta-** iti śrī-vasudeva-vākyam | **nigamā** vedāḥ | **parameśaṁ** paraṁ brahmākhyaṁ tattvam ||57||

**viśvanāthaḥ : samasta-nigamā** iti | samastaṁ nigamayanti nigamārthaṁ samastaṁ samanvitaṁ kurvanti ye, te vedāntina ity arthaḥ | **parameśaṁ** param-brahma-paryāyaṁ **sātvatāḥ** pāñcarātrikāḥ **bhagavantam uśanti** manyante, **sāhasikī mama jihvā tvaṁ** **suta iti kathaṁ vyājihīrṣatu** ? ||57||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.58 ||**

**taḍid-vilāsa-taralā nava-yauvana-sampadaḥ |**

**adyaiva dūti tena tvaṁ mayā ramaya mādhavam ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
	<strong>atrojjvalasya śāntena </strong>|</p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : taḍid** ity atra—viṣaya-bhede’pi vairasyam ||58||

**viśvanāthaḥ : taḍitaḥ** acira-sthāyī **vilāsa** iva **taralāś** cañcalā **nava-yauvana-sampattayo** bhavanti, tena hetunā he **dūti** ! **adyaiva mayā saha mādhavaṁ ramaya** ||58||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.59 ||**

**ciraṁ jīveti saṁyujya kācid āśīrbhir acyutam |**

**kailāsa-sthā vilāsena kāmukī pariṣaṣvaje ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra śucer vatsalena |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : ciraṁ jīva** ity-ādy udāharaṇāya kalpanā-mātram | evam anyatrāpi jñeyam ||59||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : kācit** **kailāsa**-vāsinī **kāmukī** mano-vilāsena manorathena śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ **pariṣasvaje** ||59||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.60-61 ||**

**śuceḥ sambandha-gandho’pi kathañcid yadi vatsale |**

**kvacid bhavet tataḥ suṣṭhu vairasyāyaiva kalpate ||**

**piśitāsṛṅ-mayī nāhaṁ satyam asmi tavocitā |**

**svāpāṅga-viddhāṁ śyāmāṅga kṛpayāṅgī-kuruṣva mām ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
atra <strong>śucer bībhatsena |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : kvacid** āśraye viṣaye vā | vairasyaṁ viṣaya-niṣṭha-prīter api vaira-kṛtyam eva na tāṭasthyam | yathā vimocayārgalā-bandham [bha.ra.si. 4.8.75] ity-ādau darśayiṣyate ||61||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **māṁsa-rudhira-**mayī aham**, atas **tava** yogyā **nāsmi**, tathāpi **tavāpāṅgena** pīḍitāṁ **mām** ||61||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.62 ||**

**evam anyāpi vijñeyā prājñai rasa-virodhitā |**

**prāyeṇeyaṁ rasābhāsa-kakṣāyāṁ paryavasyati ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : prāyeṇa** iti kecid** rasābhāsād** apy adhama-**kakṣāyāṁ paryavasyanti **ity arthaḥ ||62||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : prāyeṇa** iti kecid bhāvā **rasābhāsād** apy adhama-**kakṣāyāṁ paryavasyanti** ity arthaḥ ||62||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.63-64 ||**

**kiṁ ca—**

**dvayor ekatarasyeha bādhyatvenopavarṇane |**

**smaryamāṇatayāpy uktau sāmyena vacane’pi ca ||**

**rasāntareṇa vyavadhau taṭasthena priyeṇa vā |**

**viṣayāśraya-bhede ca gauṇena dviṣatā saha |**

**ity-ādiṣu na vairasyaṁ vairiṇo janayed yutiḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bādhyatvaṁ** bādha-yogyatvaṁ, ayam atra bādhā-yogyā bhavatīty **upavarṇane**, yukti-saṁvalitatayā nirūpaṇa ity arthaḥ | ato bādhāyā ayogyasya tathā varṇane tu vairasyam eveti bhāvaḥ | dvitīyo’py api-śabdaḥ pūrvavat | ato varṇanīyānāṁ śṛṅgārādīnāṁ bībhatsādibhiḥ sāmya-vacanam anucitam | api-śabdasya dviruktyā **rasāntareṇa** ity-ādau ca vyabhicāro draṣṭavyaḥ | vatsalādīnāṁ vairi-yoge **vyavadhāna**-śatenāpi vairasyābhāvānupapatteḥ | **viṣayāśraya-bhede** ca tatra bhakti-rasikābhīṣṭasya rasa-viśeṣasyānyatra samatāṁ darśayadbhir anyaiḥ pratītottamatve’pi bhakti-rasikair bībhatsitatvam udbhāvyate, tatraiva na tūbhayair eva bībhatsitatayā jñāte’pīty-ādi jñeyam ||64||

**mukundadāsaḥ : bādhyatvaṁ** bādhā-yogyatvaṁ, ayam atra bādhā-yogyo bhavatīty **upavarṇane** yukti-saṁvalitatayā nirūpaṇe ity arthaḥ | ato bādhāyā ayogyasya tathā varṇane tu vairasyam eveti bhāvaḥ | **api**-śabdasya sambhava-vacanatvād dhāsyādau karuṇa-smaraṇaṁ vairasyāyaiva bodhyam | dvitīyo’py api-śabdaḥ pūrvavat | ato varṇanīyānāṁ śṛṅgārādīnāṁ bībhatsādibhiḥ sāmya-vacanam anucitam ||64||

**viśvanāthaḥ : dvayo** rasayor madhye **ekatarasya** **bādhyatvena** **varṇane** sati paraspara-vairiṇo rasayor yuktir milanaṁ na vairasyaṁ janayet, tathā virodhi-rasasya **smaryamāṇatvena** varṇane na doṣaḥ | evaṁ-vidha-dvayasya sāmyena varṇane na doṣaḥ vairasyam | **taṭasthena** **priyeṇa vā rasāntareṇa vyavadhāne** sati na vairasyam | **vairiṇo** rasayor eka-viṣayatve tathā ekāśrayatve ca na vairasyam asti | **viṣayāśraya-bhede ca gauṇena dviṣatā** vairiṇā **saha** varṇane **na vairasyaṁ** na vartate evety agre vyaktībhaviṣyati ||63-64||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.65 ||**

tatra **ekatarasya bādhyatvena varṇane**, yathā vidagdha-mādhave (2.18)—

**pratyāhṛtya muniḥ kṣaṇaṁ viṣayato yasmin mano dhitsate**

**bālāsau viṣayeṣu dhitsati tataḥ pratyāharantī manaḥ |**

**yasya sphūrti-lavāya hanta hṛdaye yogī sumutkaṇṭhate **

**mugdheyaṁ kila tasya paśya hṛdayān niṣkrāntim ākāṅkṣati ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : pratyāhṛtya** iti | atra pūrvārdhe muner bālāyāś ca prathamā niṣṭhā | uttarārdhe yoginas tasyāś ca, sphuṭam uttarā ||65||

**mukundadāsaḥ : pratyāharantī** nirbhara-gabhīra-premormi-nirmita-manaḥ-kṣobhatvenākarṣantī | **yasya** ity ardhe muni-bālayor uttara-niṣṭhā, atrāśraya-bhedo’pi vairiṇo mukhād vairasyo’pi ||65||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śrī-rādhāyāḥ premotkarṣa-kathanāya paurṇamāsī āha—**pratyāhṛtya** iti | **viṣayebhyaḥ manaḥ pratyāhṛtya yasmin** śrī-kṛṣṇe **dhitsati** dhartum icchati, ity anena munīnām icchā-mātraṁ, na tu dhāraṇa-sāmarthyam iti jñeyam | tataḥ śrī-kṛṣṇātmanaḥ pratyāharantī loka-dharma-bhayād ākarṣantī **asau bālā** śrī-rādhā **viṣayeṣu dhartum icchati **ity atrāpi tasyā viṣaye dhāraṇecchā-mātraṁ, na tu dhāraṇa-sāmarthyam ||65||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.66 ||**

**bādhyatvam atra śāntasya śucer utkarṣa-varṇanāt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : bādhyatvam** iti | pūrva-padye śrī-rādhā-mādhava-rahasya-sahāyatayā paurṇamāsy-ākhya-tapasvinyā rasa-dvayaṁ bhāvitam | muny-ādy-anusāreṇa śāntaḥ | śrī-rādhādy-anusāreṇa sūciḥ | atra muni-yoginor yoga-balena pravartamānasyāpi manasas tatrāpravṛtteḥ śrī-rādhāyā dharma-bhayena ruddhyamānasyāpi tasya tasmin pravṛtteḥ pūrvasya nikarṣaḥ, parasya tu prakarṣaḥ spaṣṭa eveti | kiṁ tv īdṛg varṇanaṁ vaktṛ-bhedenaivādoṣāya jñeyaṁ, na tu sarvatra ||66||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tena śṛṅgāra-rasasya **sarvotkarṣa**-kathanāt **śāntasya** apakarṣa-rūpa-bādhyatvam uktam ||66||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.67 ||**

**smaryamāṇatve**, yathā—

**sa eṣa vaihāsikatā-vinodair**

**vrajasya hāsodgama-saṁvidhātā |**

**phaṇīśvareṇādya vikṛṣyamāṇaḥ**

**karoti hā naḥ paridevanāni ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : sa eṣa** iti padya-dvayaṁ keṣāñcit kṣodiṣṭha-diviṣṭhānām eva vacanam | yad idam atisnigdha-svabhāvānāṁ neti lakṣyate, vraja-sthānāṁ tu sutarām | tadā **vaihāsikādi**-śabdānāṁ prayogānaucityāt | na cedaṁ brahma-śivādīnāṁ, teṣāṁ svayaṁ bhagavattva-jñānāt ||67||

**mukundadāsaḥ : sa eṣa** iti vṛddhānāṁ vacanam | **paridevanāni** vilāpān ||67||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **kāliyena veṣṭitaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ dṛṣṭvā gopo duḥkhenāha—**sa** iti | yaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ **adya** kāliyena **ākṛṣyamāṇaḥ** ākarṣaṇa-vaśāt kliśyamāna ity arthaḥ | **paridevanāni** vilāpa-vacanāni, vilāpaḥ paridevanam ity amaraḥ | yadyapi śrī-kṛṣṇasyāsura-kartṛka-parābhavābhāvena vilāpo sambhavati, tathāpy aiśvarya-jñāna-śūnyasya gopasya kṛṣṇa-niṣṭha-bandhana-janita-snehena vilāpānumānaṁ jñeyam | **sa eṣa vaihāsikatā-vinodair** **vrajasya hāsodgama-saṁvidhātā** pūrvam āsīd iti karuṇa-rasena saha hāsasya virodhe’pi tasya smaryamāṇatvena na vairasyam iti jñeyam ||67||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.68 ||**

**sāmyena vacane**, yathā—

**viśrānta-ṣoḍaśa-kalā nirvikalpā nirāvṛtiḥ |**

**sukhātmā bhavatī rādhe brahma-vidyeva rājate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : viśrāntāḥ** prāpta-viśramāḥ, **ṣoḍaśa-kalā** racanāḥ śṛṅgārā yasyāṁ, pakṣe viśrāntaṁ nirudyamaṁ ṣoḍaśa-kalaṁ liṅga-śarīraṁ yasyāṁ, **nirvikalpā** suṣṭhu pratyakṣatayā nirṇītā, pakṣe bheda-rahitā | tatra hetur **nirāvṛtir** latādi-vyavadhāna-rahitā, pakṣe guṇāvaraṇa-śūnyā | **brahma-vidyā** brahmānubhavaḥ, tad etad-vidham api varṇanaṁ narma-mayam eva rasāya sampadyate, iti tathodāhṛtaḥ | “mukti-śrīr iva” pāṭhas tyaktaḥ ||68||

**mukundadāsaḥ : viśrānta-** iti | śrī-kṛṣṇasya suratānte vacanam | viśrāntāḥ prāpta-viśramāḥ ṣoḍaśa-kalā racanāḥ śṛṅgārā yasyām | pakṣe viśrāntaṁ nirudyamaṁ ṣoḍaśa-kalaṁ liṅga-śarīraṁ yasyām | nirvikalpā sarvāṅga-darśane nirṇītā, pakṣe bheda-rahitā | atra hetur nirāvṛtir vastrādi-vyavadhāna-rahitā | pakṣe guṇāvaraṇa-śūnyā ||68||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he rādhe ! **viśrāntāḥ** prāpta-viśramāḥ **ṣoḍaśa-kalā**tmaka-śṛṅgārā yasyāṁ tathā-bhūtā **bhavatī rājate** | **brahma-vidyā**-pakṣe viśrāntaṁ nirudyamaṁ ṣoḍaśa-kalaṁ liṅga-śarīraṁ yasyām | tathā **nirvikalpā** iyaṁ rādhā na veti vikalpa-rahitā suṣṭhu pratyakṣatayā nirṇītety arthaḥ | pakṣe, bheda-rahitā | pratyakṣatayā nirṇīteti hetuḥ—**nirāvṛtiḥ,** latādi-vyavadhāna-rahitā | pakṣe, guṇāvaraṇa-śūnyā | brahma-vidyā brahmānubhavaḥ | tad etad-vidham api varṇanaṁ narma-mayam eva rasāya sampadyata iti ||68||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.69 ||**

yathā vā—

**rādhā śāntir ivonnidraṁ nirnimeṣekṣaṇaṁ ca mām |**

**kurvatī dhyāna-lagnaṁ ca vāsayaty adri-kandare ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : rādhā śāntir iva mām unnidraṁ nimiṣa-rahitekṣaṇaṁ dhyāna-lagnaṁ ca kurvatī adri-kandarāyāṁ vāsayati** ||69||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.70 ||**

**rasāntareṇa vyavadhau**, yathā—

**tvaṁ kāsi śāntā kim ihāntarīkṣe**

**draṣṭuṁ paraṁ brahma kutas tatākṣī |**

**asyātirūpāt kim ivākulātmā**

**rambhe samāviśya bhidā smareṇa ||70||**

<p style="text-align: right">
	<strong>atrādbhutena vyavadhiḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : tvaṁ kāsi** ? iti | **atra** rūpasya **adbhutatayā** tasyā śānti-ratim ācchādya madhura-ratir udbhāvitā | **vyavadhi**-śabdasyāpy etāvān avadhiḥ, sākṣāt smaroktyā tu yad vairasyaṁ, tat khalu na niṣidhyate | kintu śānta-saṅgena yat, tad eveti bhāvaḥ | evam anyatrāpi ||70||

**mukundadāsaḥ : tvaṁ kāsi** ? iti | **atra** rūpasya **adbhutatayā** śānti-ratir madhura-ratitayobhāvitā | vyavadhi-śabdasyāpy etāvān avadhiḥ ||70||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **rambhā-nāmnī apsarāḥ pṛcchati—**tvaṁ kāsi** ? **śāntāsmi** śānti-rati-maty aham | **ihāntarīkṣe kiṁ** ? punaḥ tatrottaraṁ—**paraṁ brahma** śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ **draṣṭum** | vismayena **kutas** tvaṁ **vistṛtākṣī** ? punas tatrottaram āha—he **rambhe** ! kṛṣṇasyātiśaya-rūpāt **kim iva** anirvacanīyā **ākulātmāhaṁ** bhedābheda-kartrā **smareṇa** samārambhi | adyāvadhi mama kandarpārambhaḥ jāta iti paryavasitārthaḥ | **atra** rūpasya **atyantādbhutatayā** tasyā śānti-ratim ācchādya madhura-ratir udbhāviteti jñeyam ||70||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.71 ||**

**viṣaya-bhinnatve**, yathā śrī-daśame (10.60.45)—

**tvak-śmaśru-roma-nakha-keśa-pinaddham antar**

**māṁsāsthi-rakta-kṛmi-viṭ-kapha-pitta-vātam |**

**jīvac-chavaṁ bhajati kāntam ativimūḍhā**

**yā te padābja-makarandam ajighratī strī ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : tava** caraṇa-kamalasya **makarandā**svāda-rahitā **yā strī**, saiva **jīvan**-mṛte rūpe **kānta**-matiḥ | ata eva tvāṁ na **bhajati** | atra rukmiṇyāṁ śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayaka-śṛṅgāra-rasaḥ prākṛta-puruṣa-viṣayaka-bībhatsa-rasaś ca | ato viṣaya-bhedena na vairasyam iti jñeyam ||71||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.72 ||**

yathā vā, vidagdha-mādhave (2.31)—



**tasyāḥ kānta-dyutini vadane mañjule cākṣi-yugme**

**tatrāsmākaṁ yad-avadhi sakhe dṛṣṭir eṣā niviṣṭā |**

**satyaṁ brūmas tad-avadhi bhaved indum indīvaraṁ ca**

**smāraṁ smāraṁ mukha-kuṭilatā-kāriṇīyaṁ hṛṇīyā ||72||**


                            **ubhayatra śuci-bībhatsayoḥ **|

**śrī-jīvaḥ : smāraṁ** **smāram** iti **hṛṇīya** iti dvayam apy asmākam ity asyaika-kartuḥ kriyā-dvaye cāsmin smṛti-kriyāyāḥ pūrvatvān ṇamul yujyata eva ||72||

**mukundadāsaḥ : smāraṁ smāraṁ** tāpin iti śeṣaḥ ||72||

**viśvanāthaḥ : tasyā** rādhāyāḥ **kamanīya-dyuti**-viśiṣṭe **vadane** evaṁ manojñe **akṣi-yugme ca dṛṣṭir** **niviṣṭā indum indīvaraṁ** nīla-kamalaṁ ca **smṛtvā** mama **mukha-kuṭilatā-kāriṇī** ghṛṇā bhavet | mukha-darśanāt candre netra-darśanān nīla-kamale ghṛṇā bhaved iti jñeyam ||72||

**tasyāḥ kamanīyā dyutir** yasya tathā-bhūte **vadane** kānteti vadana-sādṛśyārthaṁ **induṁ smṛtvā hṛṇīyā** lajjā ghṛṇā vā **mukha-kuṭilatā-kāriṇī bhavet** || (vidagdha-mādhava-ṭīkā)

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.73 ||**

**āśraya-bhinnatve**, yathā—

**vijayinam ajitaḥ vilokya raṅga-**

**sthala-bhuvi sambhṛta-sāṁyugīna-līlam |**

**paśupa-savayasāṁ vapūṁṣi bhejuḥ **

**pulaka-kulaṁ dviṣatāṁ tu kālimānam ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra vīra-bhayānakayoḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : sambhṛtā** **samyak dhṛtā sāṁyugīna-līlā** yena, taṁ **vijayinaṁ** śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ **vilokya** bālakānāṁ **vapūṁṣi** **pulakaṁ bhejuḥ** | sāṁyugīno raṇe sādhuḥ ity amaraḥ | **dviṣatāṁ** kaṁsādīnāṁ vapūṁṣi bhayena **kālimānaṁ** bhejuḥ ||73||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.74-75 ||**

**viṣayāśraya-bhede’pi mukhyena dviṣatā saha |**

**saṅgatiḥ kila mukhyasya vairasyāyaiva jāyate ||**

tatra **viṣaya-bhede**, yathā—

**vimocayārgala-bandhaṁ vilambaṁ tāta nācara |**

**yāmi kāśya-gṛhaṁ yūnā manaḥ śyāmena me hṛtam ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra śuceḥ prītena |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : kāśyaḥ** sāndīpaniḥ | prītena tasyāḥ pitṛ-viṣayeṇa | bhāvanā-viśeṣaṁ tv atrāpi na doṣaḥ | yathā, 


    ahaṁ trayīmayāj jātā sātvatānāṁ patiḥ sa tu |


    tasmād anyo varaḥ ko vā mamālambāya kalpatām || 

_trayīmayāt_ sūryāt ||75||

**mukundadāsaḥ : kāśyaḥ** sāndīpaniḥ | prītena tasyāḥ pitṛ-viṣayeṇa ||75||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vairiṇā mukhyena saha mukhyasya saha milanaṁ viṣayāśraya-bhede’pi vairasya-janakaṁ bhavati | gauṇena saha milanaṁ tu sa vairasya-janakam iti pūrvam apy uktam ||74||

he **tāta** ! mama gamana-pratibandhaka **argala-bandhaṁ** **vimocaya**, **vilambaṁ nācara**, **yūnā** **śyāmena mama manaḥ hṛtam** | ataḥ tasya darśanārthaṁ sāndīpaner **gṛhaṁ** **yāmi** | atra kanyāyāḥ pitṛ-viṣayaka-dāsya-ratiḥ, śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayaka-śṛṅgāra-ratiś ca dvayor mukhyatvena bhinna-viṣayatve’pi vairasyaṁ jñeyam ||75||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.76 ||**

**āśraya-bhede**, yathā—

**rukmiṇī-kuca-kāśmīra-paṅkiloraḥ-sthalaṁ kadā |**

**sadānandaṁ paraṁ brahma dṛṣṭyā seviṣyate mayā ||76||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra śāntasya śucinā |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : rukmiṇī** iti | eṣā atra śucer āśrayaḥ | vaktā tu śāntasya | rukmiṇīty-ādi bhāvanāyāṁ tu śucer āśrayaḥ syād iti | pakṣe tu sutarām eva doṣa iti bhāvaḥ ||76||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : rukmiṇī** iti | eṣā atra śucer āśrayaḥ | vaktā śāntasya ||76||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.77 ||**

**anurakta-dhiyo bhaktāḥ kecana jñāna-vartmani |**

**śāntasyāśraya-bhinnatve vairasyaṁ nānumanvate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : jñāna-vartmani anurakta-dhiyo bhaktāḥ** ||77||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.78-79 ||**

**kiṁ ca—**

**bhṛtyayor nāyakasyeva nisarga-dveṣiṇor api |**

**aṅgayor aṅginaḥ puṣṭyai bhaved ekatra saṅgatiḥ ||**

yathā—

**kumāras te mallī-kusuma-sukumāraḥ priyatame **

**gariṣṭho’yaṁ keśī girivad iti me vellati manaḥ |**

**śivaṁ bhūyāt paśyonnamita-bhuja-medhir muhur amuṁ **

khalaṁ kṣundan kuryāṁ vrajam atitarāṁ śālinam aham ||

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	atra vidviṣau vīra-bhayānakau vatsalaṁ puṣṇītaḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : kumāra** ity ādau viṣaya-bhedo’py apekṣyate | **śālinaṁ** ślāghinam, śāl ślāghāyāṁ dhātuḥ | **medhir** dhānya-palāla-pārthakyāya bhrāmyamāṇa-balīvarda-bandhana-stambhaḥ ||79||

**mukundadāsaḥ : vellati** aticañcalaṁ bhavati | **kṣundan** sañcūrṇayan | **śālinaṁ** ślāghinam | śāḍṛ ślāghāyām | **medhir** dhānya-palāla-pārthakyāya bhrāmyamāṇa-balīvarda-baddha-stambhaḥ ||79||

**viśvanāthaḥ : kiṁ ca** iti | svabhāvata eva dveṣiṇor api bhṛtyayo rāja-sevakayor nāyakasya sva-prabhoḥ sevārthaṁ yathā ekatra saṅgatiḥ, tathā paraspara-vairiṇor api aṅgayoḥ aṅginaḥ puṣṭau nimitte ekatra saṅgatir na doṣāya kalpate ||78||

śrī-nandaḥ prāha—**kumāra** ity ādau viṣaya-bhede’py apekṣyaḥ | he **priyatame** yaśode ! **mama manaḥ vellati** kampate | atra bhayānakaḥ | **unnamitaḥ bhuja **eva **medhir** yasya tathā-bhūto’ham **amuṁ** keśinaṁ **kṣundan** san **vrajam atiśālinaṁ** ślāghinaṁ kuryām | śāl ślāghāyām | **medhir** dhānya-palālayoḥ pārthakyāya bhrāmyamāṇa-balīvarda-stambhaḥ | tatra vīra-rasaḥ ||79||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.80 ||**

yathā (bha.ra.si. 4.8.31)—

**kamprā svedini cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe ity-ādi ||**

<p style="text-align: right">
<strong>	tatra hāsya-karuṇau vatsalam eva puṣṇītaḥ |</strong></p>


**śrī-jīvaḥ : kamprā** ity-ādau kiñcit kāla-bhedo’pi dṛśyate ||80||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : kamprā** ity-ādi ślokas tu pūrvam evoktaḥ ||80||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.81 ||**

**api ca—**

**mitho vairāv api dvau yau bhāvau dharma-sutādiṣu |**

**kālādi-bhedāt prākaṭyaṁ tau vindantau na duṣyataḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **mitha iti | tat-tad-bhāva-yogyeṣu teṣu bhāva-bhedasya yathā-kālam udayāt | dharma-sute hi prīta-vātsalyaṁ sakhyaṁ ca dṛśyate | yogyatā ca—tad-īśvaratā-jñānitvāt, jyeṣṭha-bhrātṛtvāt nātijyeṣṭha-bhrātṛtvāc ca, yathā śrī-baladevasya | doṣatvaṁ khalu ayogya eva vidhīyate, tasmān na teṣu doṣaḥ, kiṁ tv anyatraivety arthaḥ, ye vā kecit prayogāḥ śrī-bhāgavate viruddhā iva dṛśyante, tat-samādhānaṁ tu śrī-bhāgavata-sandarbhasya prīti-sandarbhe kṛtam asti ||81||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **mita iti kālādi-bhedād iti | yaṁ samastety atra prīti-vatsalayor ekadodayā vairasyam iti bhāvaḥ ||81||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mitho vairāv apīti | tat-tad-bhāva-yogyeṣu bhāva-bhedasya yathā-kālam udayāt dharma-sutādiṣu yudhiṣṭhirādiṣu | yudhiṣṭhire hi dāsyaṁ vātsalyaṁ sakhyaṁ ca dṛśyate | yogyatā ca—tad-īśvaratā-jñānitvāt, jyeṣṭha-bhrātṛtvāt, nātijyeṣṭha-bhrātṛtvāc ca ||81||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.82 ||**

**adhirūḍhe mahā-bhāve viruddhair virasāḥ yutiḥ |**

**na syād ity ujjvale rādhā-kṛṣṇayor darśitaṁ purā ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : darśitaṁ purā** iti ghorā khaṇḍita-śaṅkhacūḍam [bha.ra.si. 3.2.23] ity ādau ||82||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **mahā-bhāve viruddhaiḥ saha yutir milanaṁ viraso na bhavet ||82||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.83 ||**

**kvāpy acintya-mahā-śaktau mahā-puruṣa-śekhare |**

**rasāvali-samāveśaḥ svādāyaivopajāyate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **kvāpīti | viṣayatvena prāyaḥ svādo na vihanyate, āśrayatve’pi svādāyaiva syād ity arthaḥ ||83||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **kvāpīti | deśa-kāla-pātra-viśeṣa eva na sarvatra | ato brahmajñāyā ity-ādiṣu bhakta-viṣayakāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayāḥ parokṣāparokṣa-rasābhiprāyeṇa | vibhāvāder vairūpyād rasābhāsa-paryavasāyina eveti ||83||

**viśvanāthaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.84 ||**

tatra **rasānāṁ viṣayatve**, yathā lalita-mādhave (3.4)—

**daityācāryās tad-āsye vikṛtim aruṇatāṁ malla-varyāḥ sakhāyo**

**gaṇḍaunnatyaṁ khaleśāḥ pralayam ṛṣi-gaṇā dhyānam uṣṇāsram ambāḥ |**

**romāñcaṁ sāṁyugīnāḥ kam api nava-camatkāram antaḥ sureśā**

**lāsyaṁ dāsāḥ kaṭākṣaṁ yayur asita-dṛśaḥ prekṣya raṅge mukundam ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **daityācāryāḥ kaṁsa-purohitāḥ | tadā tadānīm, āsye mukhe vikṛtiṁ kūṇanādikaṁ yayuḥ gaja-rakta-madādi-liptatvaṁ dṛṣṭveti bhāvaḥ | anena bībhatsaḥ | sakhāya ity anena hāsyaḥ preyāṁś ceti rasa-dvayam | pralayaṁ bhayena naṣṭa-ceṣṭatām | dhyānaṁ dhyānāvasthām eva sākṣāt yayuḥ, anena śāntaḥ | ambā devaky-ādayaḥ, etena vatsalaḥ karuṇaś ca ||84||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **daityācāryāḥ kaṁsa-purohitāḥ | tadā tadānīm, āsye mukhe vikṛtiṁ kūṇanādikaṁ yayuḥ | gaja-rakta-madādi-liptatvaṁ dṛṣṭveti bhāvaḥ | aruṇatām iti raudraḥ | sakhāyo gaṇḍaunnatyam iti hāsyaḥ preyāṁś ceti rasa-dvayam | pralayaṁ bhayena naṣṭa-ceṣṭatām | dhyānaṁ yayuḥ para-brahmatvena tam āsvāditavanta ity arthaḥ | ambā devaky-ādyāḥ, uṣṇāsram iti vatsala-karuṇau | saṁyugīnā raṇe sādhavo romāñcam iti yuddha-vīrāḥ ||84||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **daityācāryāḥ kaṁsa-purohitāḥ | tadānīm āsye mukhe vikṛtiṁ yayuḥ | gaja-rakta-madādi-liptatvaṁ dṛṣṭveti bhāvaḥ | anena bībhatsaḥ | malla-śreṣṭhā aruṇatāṁ yayur iti raudraḥ | sakhāyo hāsyena gaṇḍonnatiṁ yayur, atra hāsāḥ preyāṁś ceti rasa-dvayam | khaleśāḥ kaṁsādayaḥ pralayaṁ bhayena naṣṭa-ceṣṭatām | ṛṣi-gaṇā dhyānaṁ dhyānāvasthām eva sākṣāt yayuḥ, anena śāntaḥ | ambā devaky-ādayaḥ asraṁ rodanam ity anena vatsalaḥ karuṇaś ca | romāñcam atra vīra-rasaḥ | sureśā indrādyā antaś-camatkāram iti adbhuta-rasaḥ | asita-dṛśaḥ yuvatayaḥ ||84||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.8.85 ||**

**āśrayatve, yathā—**

**svasmin dhūrye’py amānī śiśuṣu giri-dhṛtāv udyateṣu smitāsyas**

**thūtkārī dadhni visre praṇayiṣu vivṛta-prauḍhir indre’ruṇākṣaḥ |**

**goṣṭhe sāśrur vidūne guruṣu hari-makhaṁ prāsya kampaḥ sa pāyād**

**āsāre sphāra-dṛṣṭir yuvatiṣu pulakī bibhrad adriṁ vibhur vaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **amānīti nirahaṅkāratayā śāntaḥ uktaḥ | kampa ity anena bhayānakaḥ | evam anye’pi jñeyāḥ | prāsya khaṇḍayitvā ||85||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **amānīti nirahaṅkāratayā śāntaḥ uktaḥ | śiśuṣu smitāsya iti vatsala-hāsau | vivṛta-prauḍhir iti preyān | aruṇākṣa iti raudraḥ | guruṣu hari-makhaṁ prāsya khaṇḍayitveti prīta-bhayānakau | bibhrad adrim iti yuddha-vīraḥ ||85||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ekasya kṛṣṇasya sarva-rasānāṁ viṣayatve udāharaṇam uktvā tasya sarva-rasāśrayatve’pi udāharaṇam āha—svasminn iti | na vibhuḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ govardhanaṁ bibhrat san vaḥ yuṣmān pāyāt | dhūrye govardhana-bhāra-vāhake’pi svasmin amānīti nirahaṅkāratayā śānta-bhaktaḥ | visre āma-gandhe dadhni thūtkārīti bībhatsaḥ | praṇayiṣu sakhiṣu vivṛta-prauḍhiḥ, govardhana-dhāraṇa-janya-baliṣṭhatāviṣkāro yena sa iti vīra-rasaḥ | aruṇākṣa iti raudraḥ | varṣāpavanābhyāṁ goṣṭhe vidūne duḥkhite sati sāśrur iti karuṇaḥ | indra-makhaṁ prāsya khaṇḍayitvā guru-vargeṣu kampa ity anena bhayānakaḥ | āsāre dhārā-sampāte sphārā dṛṣṭir yasya saḥ ||85||

—o)0(o—

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge

rasānāṁ maitrī-vaira-sthiti-nāmnī 

laharī aṣṭamī 

|| 4.8 ||

**(4.9)**


### rasābhāsākhyā 


#### navama-laharī

**|| 4.9.1-2 ||**

**pūrvam evānuśiṣṭena vikalā rasa-lakṣaṇā |**

**rasā eva rasābhāsā rasa-jñair anukīrtitāḥ ||**

**syus tridhoparasāś cānurasāś cāparasāś ca te |**

**uttamā madhyamāḥ proktāḥ kaniṣṭhāś cety amī kramāt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : rasā** iti rasatvena āpātataḥ pratīyamānā apīty arthaḥ | **rasasya lakṣaṇā** lakṣaṇena, **vikalā** vibhāvādiṣu lakṣaṇa-hīnatayā hīnāḥ ||1||

**mukundadāsaḥ : rasā** **eva pūrvam** **eva** **anuśiṣṭena** kathitena **rasa-lakṣaṇa-vikalāḥ** sthāyy-ādīnāṁ lakṣaṇena hīnāḥ śāntādayo rasābhāsāḥ ||1||

**viśvanāthaḥ : rasā** iti rasatvenāpātataḥ pratīyamānā apīty arthaḥ | **rasasya lakṣaṇā** lakṣaṇena **vikalā** vibhāvādiṣu lakṣaṇa-hīnatayā hīnāḥ | sthāyi-prabhṛtīnāṁ vairūpyeṇa | uparasasyodāharaṇaṁ tv agre śṛṅgāra-rase eva vakṣyati ||1||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.3-4 ||**

atra **uparasāḥ**—

**prāptaiḥ sthāyi-vibhāvānubhāvādyais tu virūpatām |**

**śāntādayo rasā eva dvādaśoparasā matāḥ ||**

tatra **śāntoparasāḥ—**

**brahma-bhāvāt para-brahmaṇy advaitādhikya-yogataḥ |**

**tathā bībhatsa-bhūmādeḥ śānto hy uparaso bhavet ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **para-brahmaṇi brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham [gītā 14.27] ity-ādi pratipādite śrī-bhagavati brahma-bhāvān nirviśeṣatā-dṛṣṭeḥ | tathā advaitādhikya-yogataḥ sarva-kāraṇena tena saha sarvasyātyantābheda iti mananāt | tathā bībhatsa-bhūmādeḥ nirantaraṁ dehādau jugupsā-bhāvanā bhāvanā | ādi-grahaṇāc cid-acid-vivekāc ca iti jñeyam | itaḥ param udāharaṇāny eka-deśa-darśanād eva jñāpanīyāni ||4||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **para-brahmaṇi bhagavati brahma-bhāvād brahma-mātra-dṛṣṭeḥ | tathā advaitādhikya-yogataḥ sarva-kāraṇa-kāraṇena tena saha sarvasyātyantābheda-mananāt | anubhāve vairūpyam idam | agrimam api tathā bībhatsa-bhūmāder nirantaraṁ dehādau jugupsā-bhāvanāt ||4||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **para-brahmaṇi brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham [gītā 14.27] ity-ādi pratipādite śrī-bhagavati brahma-bhāvān nirviśeṣatā-dṛṣṭeḥ | tathā advaitādhikya-yogataḥ sarva-kāraṇena tena saha sarvasyātyantābheda iti mananāt | tathā bībhatsa-bhūmādeḥ nirantaraṁ dehādau jugupsā-bhāvāt | ādi-grahaṇāc cid-acid-vivekātirekāc ceti jñeyam | ataḥ param udāharaṇāny eka-deśa-darśanād vijñāpanīyāni ||4||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.5-6 ||**

tatra **ādyaṁ**, yathā—

**vijñāna-suṣamā-dhaute samādhau yad udañcati |**

**sukhaṁ dṛṣṭe tad evādya purāṇa-puruṣe tvayi ||**

**dvitīyaṁ**, yathā—

**yatra yatra viṣaye mama dṛṣṭis **

**taṁ tam eva kalayāmi bhavantam |**

**yan nirañjana parāvara-bījaṁ**

**tvāṁ vinā kim api nāparam asti ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : **taṁ tam eva viṣayam | yad yasmāt | tṛtīyam ūhyam | evam uttarāpi ||6||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dvitīyaṁ bhagavatā saha sarva-vastunaḥ atyanta-ābheda-darśanaṁ darśanaṁ yatheti | tṛtīyasya bībhatsa-bhūmāder udāharaṇam atra noktam, kintu tat svayam evohyam ||6||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.7-8 ||**

atha **prītoparasaḥ—**

**kṛṣṇasyāgre’tidhārṣṭyena tad-bhakteṣv avahelayā |**

**svābhīṣṭa-devatānyatra paramotkarṣa-vīkṣayā |**

**maryādātikramādyaiś ca prītoparasatā matā ||**

tatra **ādyaṁ**, yathā—

**praṇayanprathayan**[^11]** vapur vapur-vivaśatāṁ satāṁ kulair**

**avadhīryamāṇa-naṭano’py anargalaḥ |**

**vikira prabho dṛśam ihety akuṇṭha-vāk **

**caṭulo baṭu-r vyavṛṇutātmano ratim ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **vivaśatāṁ prathayan pṛthuṁ kurvann iti | svalpām api tāṁ pṛthutayā darśayann ity arthaḥ | prabho iti śrī-kṛṣṇa-pratimāṁ prati sambodhanam ||8||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **vapur vapur**-**vivaśatāṁ hantādy-anusandhāna-rāhityaṁ prathayan svalpām api pṛthutayā darśayann ity arthaḥ | prabho iti śrī-kṛṣṇa-pratimāṁ prati sambodhanam ||8||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vivaśatāṁ prathayann iti | pṛthuṁ kurvan svalpām api vivaśatāṁ pṛthutayā darśayann ity arthaḥ | satāṁ kulaiḥ samūhaiḥ tiraskṛtaṁ naṭanaṁ yasya tathā-bhūto’pi anargalaḥ nirlajjaḥ | he prabho iti śrī-kṛṣṇa-pratimāṁ prati sambodhanam | caṭulaś cañcalo baṭur brāhmaṇaaḥ ||8||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.9-10 ||**

atha **preya-uparasaḥ—**

**ekasminn eva sakhyena hari-mitrādy-avajñayā |**

**yuddha-bhūmādinā cāpi preyān uparaso bhavet ||**

tatra **ādyaṁ**, yathā—

**suhṛd ity udito bhiyā cakampe**

**chalito narma-girā stutiṁ cakāra |**

**sa nṛpaḥ pariripsatā**[^12]** bhujābhyāṁ**

**hariṇā daṇḍavad agrataḥ papāta ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **ekasminn eva, na tu mithaḥ ||9|| sa nṛpa iti śrī-hareḥ putryāḥ putrasya vā śvaśuraḥ kaścid ity arthaḥ ||10||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **chalito vañcita upahasita ity arthaḥ | sa nṛpa iti śrī-hareḥ putryāḥ putrasya vā śvaśuraḥ kaścid ity arthaḥ ||10||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **ekasminn eva sakhyaṁ, na tu dvayoḥ parasparaṁ sakhyam ||9|| sa nṛpa iti śrī-kṛṣṇasya kanyāyāḥ putrasya vā śvaśuraḥ kaścid ity arthaḥ | śrī-kṛṣṇena suhṛd ity uditaḥ san "nāhaṁ tava suhṛd-yogyaḥ" iti bhayāc cakampe | nṛpasya sakhi-bhāvābhāvād uparaso jñeyaḥ ||10||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.11-12 ||**

atha **vatsaloparasaḥ—**

**sāmarthyādhikyābhijñānāl lālanādy-aprayatnataḥ |**

**karuṇasyātirekādes turyaś coparaso bhavet ||**

tatra **ādyaṁ**, yathā—

**mallānāṁ yad-avadhi parvatodbhaṭānām**

**unmāthaṁ sapadi tavātmajād apaśyam |**

**nodvegaṁ tad-avadhi yāmi jāmi tasmin**

**drāghiṣṭhām api samitiṁ prapadyamāne ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **jāmi ! he bhagini ! ||12||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **jāmi ! he bhagini ! samitiṁ saṅgrāmam ||12||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **tūryo vātsalya-rasaḥ ||11|| devakīṁ prati tasyā bhaginī kācid vasudevasyāparā strī āha—tava putrāt mallānām unmāthaṁ parābhavam aham apaśyam, he jāmi bhagini ! drāghiṣṭhāṁ dīrghatarām api samitiṁ yuddhaṁ prapadyamāne’pi tasmin śrī-kṛṣṇe udvegaṁ na yāmi ||12||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.13 ||**

atha **śṛṅgāroparasaḥ** | tatra **sthāyi-vairūpyam—**

**dvayor ekatarasyaiva ratir yā khalu dṛśyate |**

**yān ekatra tathaikasya sthāyinaḥ sā virūpatā |**

**vibhāvasyaiva vairūpyaṁ sthāyiny atropacaryate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **vibhāvasya ālambana-rūpasyaiveti, kvacit tad-dehasya, kvacit tad-antaḥkaraṇasyety arthaḥ | svarūpataḥ sthāyino vairūpyāyogāt | tatraikatara-raty-udāharaṇe yajña-patnīṣu dehasyaiva vairūpyaṁ jñeyam, brāhmaṇa-dehatvāt | tac ca tādṛśīṁ ratiṁ virūpayati, anuciteyam iti śrī-kṛṣṇa-ratim api nodgamayati | tato’nya-doṣasyānyatra saṅkramaṇād upacaryate ity uktam | ekasyānekatra ratis tv antaḥkaraṇasyaiva vairūpyam, ekatrāniṣṭhitatvāt | tad etac ca nāyikā-gatam eva jñeyam | uttamānuttamayos tāratamyābhāve nāyaka-gataṁ ca ||13||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **vibhāvasya raty-āśrayaṇālambanasya vairūpyaṁ mano’naucityaṁ mano-dharmaḥ ratāv upacaryate, tasyās tad-āśrayatvāt ||13|| 

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dvayor nāyikā-nāyakayor madhye ekasyaiva ratiḥ, na tu parasparam | tathaikasyānekatra ratiḥ vibhāvasyālambana-rūpasyaiveti kvacit tad-dehasya kvacit tad-antaḥkaraṇasyety arthaḥ | svarūpataḥ sthāyino vairūpyāyogāt tatraikatara-raty-udāharaṇe yajña-patnīṣu dehasyaiva vairūpyaṁ jñeyam, brāhmaṇa-dehatvāt | tac ca tādṛśīṁ ratiṁ virūpayati, tathānucitatvāt śrī-kṛṣṇasyāpi ratiṁ nodgamayati | ato brāhmaṇī-niṣṭhitatvāt—tad etac ca nāyikā-gatam eva jñeyam | uttamānuttamayor nāyikayos tāratamyābhāve tac ca vairūpyaṁ nāyaka-gatam api jñeyam ||13||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.14 ||**

** **

tatra **ekatra ratir, **yathā lalita-mādhave (9.37)—

**manda-smitaṁ prakṛti-siddham api vyudantaṁ**

**saṅgopitaś ca sahajo’pi dṛśos taraṅgaḥ |**

**dhūmāyite dvija-vadhū-madanārti-vahnāv**

**ahnāya kāpi gatir aṅkuritā ayāsīt ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**mukundadāsaḥ : **ahnāya śīghraṁ kāpi śucy-udāsīnā brāhmaṇīnāṁ mayā riraṁsāṁ loka-vigītāṁ kurvatīnāṁ śucitva-bhāvanāyogyatvāt ||14||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **dvija-vadhūnāṁ yājñika-brāhmaṇīnāṁ kandarpārti-rūpa-vahnau prajvalanārthaṁ dhūmāyite svabhāva-siddham api smitaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇena vyudastaṁ dūrīkṛtaṁ, ato’hnāya śrī-kṛṣṇasya manasaḥ kāpi anirvacanīyā śānty-avalambinī gatir aṅkuritā āsīt ||14||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.15 ||**

**atyantābhāva evātra rateḥ khalu vivakṣitaḥ |**

**etasyāḥ prāg-abhāve tu śucir noparaso bhavet ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **atyantābhāvas traikāliky asattā | atreti atra iti tāsāṁ brāhmaṇī-deham adhikṛtya ity arthaḥ ||15||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **atyantābhāvas traikāliky asattā | atra vairūpye ||15||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **atyantābhāvas traikāliky asattā | atra brāhmaṇī-dehe yatra ratiman-nāyikā-viṣayakaṁ jñānaṁ nāyakasya nāsti, kintu dūtī-dvārā jñāne jāte nāyakasyāpi ratiḥ prādurbhaviṣyaty prādurbhaviṣyati, ato na rateḥ kāla-trayāvidyamānatva-rūpātyantābhāvaḥ, tasmāt tatra noparasa ity āha—etasyā iti rater ity arthaḥ ||15||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.16 ||**

**anekatra ratir**, yathā—

**gāndharvi kurvāṇam avekṣya līlām**

**agre dharaṇyāṁ sakhi kāma-pālam |**

**ākarṇayantī ca mukunda-veṇuṁ**

**bhinnādya sādhvi smarato dvidhāsi ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he gāndharvi ! dharaṇyāṁ līlāṁ kurvāṇaṁ kāma-pālaṁ baladevam avekṣya he sādhvi smaraṇe bhinnā satī dvidhāsi ||16||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.17 ||**

**kecit tu nāyakasyāpi sarvathā tulya-rāgataḥ |**

**nāyikāsv apy anekāsu vadanty uparasaṁ śucim ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **kecid rasa-tattva-vidaḥ | anekāsu prema-tāratamyena bahu-vidhāsu ||17||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **kecid iti | dakṣiṇa-nāyake tad-darśanāntaṁ sva-matam ity abhiprāyaḥ | yad vā, tatra sarvathā tv asyā bhāvāt teṣāṁ matam api svābhipretam ||17||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **anekāsu prema-tāratamyena uttama-madhyama-kaniṣṭhāsu bahu-vidhāsu nāyakasya vivekābhāvena tulya-rāgāt kecit rasa-tattva-vidaḥ uparasaṁ vadanti ||17||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.18 ||**

**vibhāva-vairūpyam—**

**vaidagdhyaujjvalya-viraho vibhāvasya virūpatā |**

**latā-paśu-pulindīṣu vṛddhāsv api sa vartate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **vaidagdhyādi-viraha ity upalakṣaṇaṁ gurutvādīnām | yathā yajña-patnīṣu vairūpyaṁ matam | latā-paśuṣv atra tat-sānnidhyādi-svabhāvenānanda-mātram eva madhura-ratitayotprekṣyate | vṛddhāsu hāsa-mātrārthaṁ tādṛśatvaṁ ca varṇyate | tasmād vāstava-tad-raty-abhāvād rasābhāsatvam | pulindīṣu tu vāstava-ratitve’pi jāti-vairūpyād yajñapatnīvat tad-ābhāsatvaṁ jñeyam | tatra latā-paśuṣu vaidagdhyaṁ nāsty eva | vṛddhāsu vaidagdhya-prātikūlyaṁ dṛśyate | pulindīṣu ca vaidagdhyaṁ nātisambhāvyate | tasmāt tad-viraha uddiṣṭaḥ | tathā aujjvalyaṁ nāma ākṛtyā jāty-ādinā ca yogyatvaṁ, tat-tad-yogyatā-virahaś ca yathā-yogyaṁ draṣṭavyam | sa vartata iti sa vaidagdhyādi-viraho vartate ||18||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **vaidagdhyety vaidagdhya- ity atra śucitva-suveśatve api vakṣyamāṇe jñeya jñeye ||18||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **vaidagdhyādi-viraha ity upalakṣaṇaṁ, gurutvādayo’pi grāhyāḥ | tena yajña-patny-ādiṣu vairūpyaṁ siddham | latā-paśuṣv atra tat-sānnidhyādi-svabhāvenānanda-mātram eva madhura-ratitayotprekṣyate | vṛddhāsu vāstava-ratimattve’pi jāti-vairūpyāt hāsa-mātrārthaṁ tādṛśatvaṁ ca varṇyate | tasmād vāstava-tad-raty-abhāvād rasābhāsatvam | pulindīṣu tu vāstava-ratimattve’pi jāti-vairūpyād yajñapatnīvat tad-ābhāsatvaṁ jñeyam | tatra latā-paśuṣu vaidagdhyaṁ nāsty eva | vṛddhāsu vaidagdhya-prātikūlyaṁ dṛśyate | pulindīṣu ca vaidagdhyaṁ nātisambhāvyate | tasmāt tad-viraha uddiṣṭaḥ | sa vaidagdhyādi-viraho vartate ||18||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.19 ||**

**tatra latā**, yathā—

**sakhi madhu kiratī niśamya vaṁśīṁ**

**madhu-mathanena kaṭākṣitātha mṛdvī |**

**mukula-pulakitā latāvalīyaṁ **

**ratim iha pallavitāṁ hṛdi vyanakti ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **sakhi madhv ity atra—


    “sa-mukula-pulakā niśamya vaṁśīṁ


    nakha-likhitā ca hariṁ prasajya jātā |


    tad iha nava-vayāḥ pratāninīyaṁ


    lasati yathā bhavatī tathā vārāṅgi ||” iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||19||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he sakhi ! śrī-kṛṣṇa-kaṭākṣītā latāvalī vaṁśīṁ niśamya madhu kiratī satī svasya hṛdi pallavitāṁ ratiṁ vyanakti | kathaṁ-bhūtā ? mukulena pulakitā ||19||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.20 ||**

**paśur**, yathā—

**paśyādbhutās tuṅga-madaḥ kuraṅgīḥ**

**pataṅga-kanyā-puline’dya dhanyāḥ |**

**yāḥ keśavāṅge tad-apāṅga-pūtāḥ **

**sānaṅga-raṅgāṁ dṛśam arpayanti ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **paśyādbhutā ity asyottarārdhe, “yāḥ keśavāṅgaṁ sakhi saṅgamayya, svairād apāṅgaṁ bhavatīr jayanti” iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||20||

**mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he sakhi ! yamunā-puline adbhutāḥ kuraṅgīr hariṇīḥ paśya | yāḥ kuraṅgyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇāpāṅgena pūtāḥ satyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇāṅge dṛśam arpayanti ||20||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.21 ||**

**pulindī**, yathā—

**kālindī-puline paśya pulindī pulakācitā |**

**harer dṛk-cāpalaṁ vīkṣya sahajaṁ yā vighūrṇate ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **śrī-kṛṣṇasya sāhajika-netra-cāpalyaṁ prekṣya vighūrṇate ||21||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.22 ||**

**vṛddhā**, yathā—

**kajjalena kṛta-keśa-kālimā**

**bilva-yugma-racitonnata-stanī |**

**paśya gauri kiratī dṛg-añcalaṁ**

**smerayaty aghaharaṁ jaraty asau ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**

**viśvanāthaḥ : **he gauri ! dṛg-añcalaṁ kiratī vṛddhā śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ smerayati hāsayati | ekatra vṛddhādiṣv eva rāgo na kṛṣṇa iti ||22||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.23-24 ||**

**sthāyino’tra virūpatvam eka-rāgatayāpi cet |**

**ghaṭetāsau vibhāvasya virūpatve’py udāhṛtiḥ ||**

**śucitvaujjvalya-vaidigdhyāt suveśatvāc ca kathyate |**

**śṛṅgārasya vibhāvatvam anyatrābhāsatā tataḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **vaidagdhety vaidagdhety-ādinā darśitam eva vivṛṇvann upasaṁharati—śucitveti śucitva- iti | śucitvādikam ālambanasya jñeyam | vibhāvatvaṁ viśiṣṭo bhāvaḥ sattvā sthāyī vā yatra tad-rūpatvam | “pāvitryaujjvalya-vaidagdhya-suveṣatvair vibhāvagaiḥ | śṛṅgāraḥ puṣṭim āgacched ābhāsatvam ato’nyathā” iti pāṭhāntaram ||24||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **uktaṁ vibhāva-vairūpyaṁ vivṛṇvann upasaṁharati—śucitveti śucitva- iti | vibhāvatvam āśrayatvaṁ, tato’nyatra śucitvādi-rahite vibhāve śṛṅgārasyābhāsataiva ||24||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **sthāyino vairūpyam udāhṛtam | asau udāhṛtiḥ vibhāvasya virūpatve’pi ghaṭeta sambhavatīty arthaḥ | ata eva vibhāva-gata-vairūpyam eva sthāyiny upacaritam iti prāk pratipāditam ||23|| śucitvaṁ śuddhatvam | etebhyaḥ śṛṅgāra-rasasya vibhāvatvaṁ kathyate, tataḥ śucitvādibhyo’nyatra śṛṅgāra-rasābhāsatā kathyate ||24||[^13]

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.25-26 ||**

atha **anubhāva-vairūpyam—**

**samayānāṁ vyatikrāntir grāmyatvaṁ dhṛṣṭatāpi ca |**

**vairūpyam anubhāvāder manīṣibhir udīritam ||**

tatra **samaya-vyatikrāntiḥ—**

**samayāḥ khaṇḍitādīnāṁ priye roṣoditādayaḥ |**

**puṁsaḥ smitādayaś cātra priyayā tāḍanādiṣu |**

**eteṣām anyathā-bhāvaḥ samayānāṁ vyatikramaḥ ||**

**śrī-jīvaḥ : **samayāḥ ācārāḥ ||25||

**mukundadāsaḥ : **samayānām ācārāṇām | anubhāvāder ity atra ādi-śabdād vyabhicāriṇām api vairūpyam ūhyam ||25-26||

**viśvanāthaḥ : **samayānām ācārāṇāṁ vyatikramaḥ—khaṇḍitādi-nāyikānāṁ kānte roṣa-vyañjaka-vacanādaya eva rasa-śāstroktācārāḥ, tathāpi priyayā kartryā puṣpādibhis tāḍanādiṣu satsu puṁsaḥ priyasya smitādaya eva ācārāḥ, na tu roṣoditādayaḥ | eteṣāṁ roṣoditānām anyathā-bhāvaḥ ||26||

—o)0(o—

**|| 4.9.27 ||**

tatra **ādyaṁ**, yathā —

**kāntā-nakhāṅkito’py adya parihṛtya hare hriyam |**

**kailāsa-vāsinīṁ dāsīṁ kṛpā-dṛṣṭyā bhajasva mām || \
**

**śrī-jīvaḥ, mukundadāsaḥ : _na vyākhyātam._**
